# 2026年4月2日 - 专业文献速递

## 1. 肺部高分化神经内分泌肿瘤：一项支持国际癌症研究机构/世界卫生组织（IARC/WHO）神经内分泌肿瘤通用命名与分级分类的病例系列研究。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41920417)
**期刊：** Endocrine pathology
**PMID：** 41920417
**DOI：** 10.1007/s12022-026-09914-2

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Well-Differentiated Neuroendocrine Tumors of Lung: A Case Series Supporting the IARC/WHO Common Classification of Neuroendocrine Tumor Nomenclature and Grading.

> **英文摘要：**
> No abstract available.

> **中文摘要：**
> 暂无摘要。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究通过肺部高分化神经内分泌肿瘤（WD-NETs）的病例系列分析，重点验证了国际癌症研究机构/世界卫生组织（IARC/WHO）提出的神经内分泌肿瘤通用命名法和分级标准的临床适用性。研究核心在于探讨统一跨器官分类标准在肺部肿瘤中的实践意义，旨在优化病理诊断的一致性。尽管目前缺乏详细摘要，但其主题对于完善神经内分泌肿瘤的全球化标准及指导精准医疗具有重要的学术参考价值。

## 2. 更正：利用日本及国际基因组数据库进行驱动变异的泛癌比较与综合分析。

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Correction: Pan-Cancer Comparative and Integrative Analyses of Driver Alterations Using Japanese and International Genomic Databases.

> **英文摘要：**
> No abstract available.

> **中文摘要：**
> 无摘要内容。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文献是对先前发表的关于日本与国际基因组数据库中癌症驱动变异比较研究的勘误说明。原研究旨在通过整合多国基因组数据，揭示不同人群间癌症驱动因素的异同，具有重要的跨人群基因组学参考价值。此类更正通告通常涉及数据标注、作者信息或图表细节的修正，体现了学术出版的严谨性。对于深入研究特定人群癌症驱动谱系的学者而言，关注此类更正有助于确保其引用的原始研究数据和结论的准确性。

## 3. 膳食纤维：一种具有多重积极效应的新型骨髓瘤预防方法

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41918359)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41918359
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-26-0152

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Fiber: A New Myeloma Prevention Approach with Abundant Positive Effects.

> **英文摘要：**
> In a recent study by Shah, Cogrossi, and colleagues, patients with overweight/obesity and pre-myeloma diseases (monoclonal gammopathy of undetermined significance or smoldering myeloma) were mailed 12 weeks of high-fiber meals, provided with nutritional counseling, and required to track their food intake and weight. The intervention was well tolerated and improved quality of life, metabolic health, gut microbiome composition, and immune system function while supporting stable or improved multiple myeloma disease trajectories. See related article by Shah et al., p. 697.

> **中文摘要：**
> 在 Shah、Cogrossi 及其同事最近开展的一项研究中，患有超重/肥胖及骨髓瘤前期疾病（意义未明的单克隆丙种球蛋白病或冒烟型骨髓瘤）的患者接受了为期 12 周的邮寄高纤维餐配送及营养咨询，并被要求记录其食物摄入量和体重。该干预措施耐受性良好，在改善患者生活质量、代谢健康、肠道微生物群组成及免疫系统功能的同时，支持了多发性骨髓瘤疾病轨迹的稳定或好转。详见第 697 页 Shah 等人的相关文章。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究评估了为期12周的高纤维饮食干预对骨髓瘤前期高风险人群（超重/肥胖及MGUS/SMM患者）的临床影响。研究表明，这种非侵入性的生活方式干预不仅具有极佳的耐受性，还能通过改善代谢、肠道微生态和免疫功能，有效稳定或优化多发性骨髓瘤的疾病轨迹。该发现强调了膳食干预在血液肿瘤二级预防中的巨大潜力，为通过精准营养手段延缓疾病进展提供了高质量的循证依据。

---

## 5. 通过精准预测推进癌症预防

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41918357)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41918357
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-25-2235

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Advancing Cancer Prevention through Precision Prediction.

> **英文摘要：**
> Emerging knowledge, integrative frameworks, and multidisciplinary partnerships together create an unprecedented opportunity to advance cancer prevention through precision. By combining multimodal risk assessment with causal biological insight and dynamic models of early carcinogenesis, precision prevention can enable actionable, equitable, and acceptable preventive and interception strategies.

> **中文摘要：**
> 新兴的知识、综合框架以及多学科伙伴关系共同创造了前所未有的机遇，通过精准化来推进癌症预防。通过将多模态风险评估与因果生物学见解以及早期癌症发生的动态模型相结合，精准预防可以实现具有可操作性、公平性且可接受的预防和拦截策略。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文强调了精准预测在当代癌症预防体系中的核心驱动作用。文章指出，通过整合多学科资源与多模态风险评估模型，可以将因果生物学机制转化为可实施的预防策略。其核心创新在于提出了动态监测与早期拦截相结合的框架，旨在提升癌症预防策略的科学性、公平性与社会接受度，为未来肿瘤精准防控指明了方向。

---

## 6. 移动的靶点：顺式突变驱动的对p53-Y220C再激活剂的耐药性

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41918356)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41918356
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-26-0153

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** The Moving Target: Cis-Mutation-Driven Resistance to p53-Y220C Reactivator.

> **英文摘要：**
> The study by Fece de la Cruz, Varkaris, and colleagues uncovered a critical mechanism underlying resistance to the p53-Y220C reactivator rezatapopt in the PYNNACLE clinical trial. Specifically, rezatapopt treatment was shown to select for secondary mutations in the TP53 gene on the Y220C-mutant background, thereby abrogating its therapeutic efficacy. See related article by Fece de la Cruz et al., p. 677.

> **中文摘要：**
> Fece de la Cruz、Varkaris及其同事的研究揭示了在PYNNACLE临床试验中，对p53-Y220C再激活剂rezatapopt产生耐药性的关键机制。具体而言，研究显示rezatapopt治疗在Y220C突变背景下筛选出TP53基因的二次突变，从而消除了其治疗功效。参见Fece de la Cruz等人的相关文章，第677页。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该研究深入探讨了新型p53-Y220C再激活剂rezatapopt在临床实践中遭遇的耐药瓶颈。通过分析PYNNACLE临床试验数据，研究人员证实了在Y220C突变基因组背景下，顺式（cis）发生的二次TP53突变是导致药物失效的主因。这一发现不仅阐明了肿瘤在靶向压力下的精准进化路径，也为未来开发能够克服获得性耐药的下一代p53再激活疗法提供了核心理论依据。

---

## 7. 生命早期诱变与早发性结直肠癌的兴起

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41918355)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41918355
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-26-0166

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Early-Life Mutagenesis and the Rise of Early-Onset Colorectal Cancer.

> **英文摘要：**
> Colorectal cancer incidence is rising globally among individuals younger than 50 years and remains poorly explained by established risk factors. In this study, we advance the hypothesis that early-childhood exposure to mutagen-producing bacteria contributes to lifetime colorectal cancer risk by imprinting oncogenic mutations in the developing colorectal epithelium, thereby initiating tumorigenesis decades before clinical diagnosis and redefining early-onset colorectal cancer as a disease rooted in early-life mutagenic exposure.

> **中文摘要：**
> 全球 50 岁以下人群的结直肠癌发病率正在上升，而既定的风险因素仍难以对其作出合理解释。在本研究中，我们提出了如下假设：儿童早期接触产生诱变剂的细菌，通过在发育中的结直肠上皮细胞中留下致癌突变印记，从而增加了终生患结直肠癌的风险。这种作用在临床诊断前几十年便启动了肿瘤发生过程，并将早发性结直肠癌重新定义为一种植根于生命早期诱变暴露的疾病。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该研究针对全球范围内早发性结直肠癌发病率上升这一医学难题，提出了极具启发性的“生命早期诱变”假说。文章核心观点认为，儿童时期肠道微生物群中产生诱变剂的细菌暴露是关键始动因素，通过在发育中的上皮组织中刻下致癌突变，导致数十年后的发病。这一理论打破了传统的成年期风险暴露模型，将防治视点大幅前移，为理解早发性癌症的病源学提供了全新的维度，具有重要的公共卫生预警价值。

---

## 8. 癌症拦截的七大原则

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41918354)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41918354
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-25-2061

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** The Seven Ps of Cancer Interception.

> **英文摘要：**
> Advances in technology, clinical innovation, cross-sector collaboration, and active societal engagement are converging to shift cancer from an unexpected and lethal disease to a condition that can be detected early, intercepted effectively, and ultimately prevented. Framed around seven core principles: purpose, prevalence, potential, precision, practicality, partnership, and persistence, this commentary highlights how strategic alignment across these dimensions can catalyze progress toward global cancer interception.

> **中文摘要：**
> 技术进步、临床创新、跨部门协作以及积极的社会参与正在产生交汇，共同推动癌症从一种突发且致命的疾病转变为一种可以被早期发现、有效拦截并最终被预防的疾病。本篇述评围绕七个核心原则展开：目的（purpose）、流行率（prevalence）、潜力（potential）、精准度（precision）、实用性（practicality）、伙伴关系（partnership）和坚持（persistence），重点阐述了这些维度的战略对齐如何能够催化全球癌症拦截领域的进展。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该述评系统性地提出了癌症拦截（Cancer Interception）的七大核心原则，旨在将癌症防控关口前移。文章通过整合技术创新、多方协作和精准医疗等要素，构建了一个从早期发现到最终预防的完整框架。其核心价值在于将复杂的公共卫生挑战拆解为“七个P”战略维度，为实现全球癌症预防的战略转型提供了具有启发性的跨学科行动指南。

---

## 9. 追踪休眠期癌症的“骨纹”

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41918353)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41918353
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-26-0163

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Tracking the Dormant Cancer Boneprint.

> **英文摘要：**
> Cancer cells can repurpose a fundamental bone development program to escape therapy in a dormant state. This finding offers a way to detect cancer dormancy and assess recurrence risk using routine bone scans. See related article by Sreekumar et al., p. 781.

> **中文摘要：**
> 癌细胞可以重新利用一套基础的骨发育程序，从而以休眠状态逃避治疗。这一发现为利用常规骨扫描检测癌症休眠状态并评估复发风险提供了一种新途径。参见 Sreekumar 等人的相关文章，第 781 页。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该研究揭示了癌细胞通过劫持宿主骨发育程序进入休眠状态以逃避治疗的关键生物学机制。提出的“骨纹（Boneprint）”概念具有显著的临床意义，因为它为利用现有的常规骨扫描技术监测休眠癌细胞及评估复发风险提供了新思路。该发现成功地将发育生物学与肿瘤影像诊断相结合，具有极高的转化医学价值，但其在不同癌种中的普适性及临床敏感度仍需进一步验证。

---

## 10. 精准、协作、目标：推进癌症科学以挽救全球生命

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41918352)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41918352
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-26-0411

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Precision, Partnership, Purpose: Advancing Cancer Science to Save Lives Globally.

> **英文摘要：**
> Increasing knowledge in molecular biology, enabled by multiomic technologies, data science, and global collaboration, extends cancer research beyond advanced disease settings toward earlier detection, interception, and more effective therapies. Through partnership, workforce development, and a commitment to equity and trust in science, discovery can be catalyzed into meaningful patient impact.

> **中文摘要：**
> 在多组学技术、数据科学和全球协作的推动下，分子生物学知识的不断增长，使癌症研究从晚期疾病阶段扩展到早期检测、拦截以及更有效的治疗。通过建立伙伴关系、加强人才队伍建设，以及对科学公平和信任的承诺，可以将科学发现转化为对患者具有重大意义的影响。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文阐述了在癌症科学研究中整合多组学和数据科学的重要性，旨在将研究重心从单纯的晚期治疗前移至早期筛查与干预。作者指出，通过全球协作、人才队伍建设以及对科研公平性的坚定承诺，能够有效加速基础科学发现向临床转化。这种多维度的合作模式为解决全球癌症防治挑战、提升医疗公平性提供了关键的战略指导和实践框架。

---

## 11. 将中国肿瘤创新整合至全球格局：精准、合作与使命的战略蓝图

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41918351)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41918351
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-25-2050

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Integrating China's Oncology Innovations into the Global Landscape: A Strategic Blueprint for Precision, Partnership, and Purpose.

> **英文摘要：**
> Global clinical oncology research is experiencing a profound structural shift, evolving from a historical underrepresentation of minority groups in Western-centric trials to a new representational imbalance marked by an increasing reliance on Chinese patient populations due to the nation's accelerating drug research and development. This article dissects this changing dynamic and proposes a systematic framework for a next-generation global oncology research and development paradigm that is inherently more inclusive, generalizable, and efficient for all patients worldwide.

> **中文摘要：**
> 全球临床肿瘤研究正经历着深刻的结构性转变，正从历史上西方中心化试验中少数族裔代表性不足，演变为由于中国药物研发加速而导致对中国患者群体依赖程度不断增加的新型代表性失衡。本文剖析了这一变化的动态，并为下一代全球肿瘤研发范式提出了一个系统性框架，该框架对全球所有患者而言，本质上更具包容性、普遍适用性且高效。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文敏锐捕捉到全球肿瘤临床试验格局从西方中心化向依赖中国患者群体的结构性转向。作者系统剖析了中国药物研发加速带来的代表性变化及其背后的动态机制。其核心价值在于提出了一个旨在提升包容性、普适性与研发效率的下一代全球肿瘤研发范式。该战略蓝图不仅为中国创新的全球化路径指明了方向，也为全球患者获得更公平、高效的精准治疗提供了重要参考。

---

## 12. 整合多维数据以推进全球肿瘤健康公平

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41918350)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41918350
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-25-2051

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Integrating Multi-Dimensional Data to Advance Global Health Equity in Oncology.

> **英文摘要：**
> Precision oncology has transformed cancer care, but its benefits remain unevenly distributed because of persistent gaps in resources and representation. Integrating multiomics data, clinical trial evidence, and real-world data enables the identification of both biological and extrinsic drivers of cancer inequities and can further advance treatment decisions across diverse populations worldwide.

> **中文摘要：**
> 精准肿瘤学已经改变了癌症护理，但由于资源和代表性方面持续存在的差距，其益处分配仍不均衡。整合多组学数据、临床试验证据和真实世界数据，能够识别导致癌症不平等的生物学和外在驱动因素，并能进一步推进全球不同人群的治疗决策。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文强调了在精准肿瘤学背景下，通过整合多组学、临床试验及真实世界等跨维度数据来应对全球癌症健康不平等问题的必要性。文章核心观点认为，数据驱动的策略不仅能揭示生物学差异，还能识别资源分配等外部因素对预后的影响。其价值在于提出了一种系统化的方法论，旨在通过增强全球异质性人群的数据覆盖度和代表性，为实现更具包容性的肿瘤治疗决策提供支撑。

---

## 13. 转移作为一种多器官疾病：迈向基于器官信息的精准肿瘤学

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41918349)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41918349
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-25-2052

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Metastasis as a Multiorgan Disease: Toward Organ-Informed Precision Oncology.

> **英文摘要：**
> Metastasis is a multiorgan disease in which disseminated cancer cells undergo profound, tissue-specific reprogramming that reshapes their identity, vulnerabilities, and therapeutic responses. We argue for an organ-informed precision oncology framework that integrates these site-imposed programs into treatment design.

> **中文摘要：**
> 转移是一种多器官疾病，其中播散的癌细胞经历深刻的组织特异性重编程，从而重塑其特性、弱点及治疗反应。我们倡导一种基于器官信息的精准肿瘤学框架，将这些由特定位点诱导的程序整合到治疗设计中。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文提出了一个极具前瞻性的医学观点，将癌症转移定义为一种受微环境驱动的多器官系统性疾病，而非单纯的肿瘤细胞扩散。其核心创新点在于强调了组织特异性重编程对癌细胞生物学特性的重塑作用，并据此构建了“基于器官信息的精准肿瘤学”理论框架。该论点挑战了传统的、忽视转移部位差异的通用治疗方案，为解决临床耐药性和优化转移性癌症的个性化治疗提供了关键的理论指引。

---

## 14. 一个控制癌细胞异质性和可塑性的物理框架

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41918348)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41918348
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-26-0083

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** A Physical Framework to Control Cancer Cell Heterogeneity and Plasticity.

> **英文摘要：**
> We propose a physics-based framework in which cancer cell state is defined by position and velocity in a continuous space of directly measurable physical variables-cell surface area (S) and volume (V)-and motion through S-V space as an interpretable proxy for plasticity. Therapy generates S-V vector fields that govern trajectories, enabling the design of drug combinations to steer heterogeneous cell populations toward nonviable states, offering a predictive and physically interpretable alternative to therapies directed against oncogenic mutations and/or predefined cell subpopulations.

> **中文摘要：**
> 我们提出了一个基于物理的框架，在该框架中，癌细胞状态由直接可测量的物理变量——细胞表面积 (S) 和体积 (V)——组成的连续空间中的位置和速度来定义，而通过 S-V 空间的运动则作为可塑性的可解释代理指标。治疗会产生引导轨迹的 S-V 向量场，从而能够设计药物组合，将异质细胞群体引向不可存活的状态，为针对致癌突变和/或预定义细胞亚群的疗法提供了一种具有预测性且物理可解释的替代方案。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该研究提出了一个创新的生物物理学框架，通过细胞表面积和体积这两个基础物理参数来量化癌细胞的状态及其动态可塑性。这种方法绕过了传统基因组学的复杂性，将治疗过程抽象为向量场中的轨迹控制。其核心价值在于能够预测并引导异质性细胞群体向不可存活状态演变，为设计新型药物组合方案提供了一个极具潜力的工程化物理模型，是癌症系统生物学领域的一次重要范式探索。

---

## 17. 修饰有CXCR4拮抗肽的脂质纳米颗粒协同递送AML1-ETO siRNA以增强难治性急性髓系白血病（AML）的化疗效果

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41917970)
**期刊：** Journal of hematology & oncology
**PMID：** 41917970
**DOI：** 10.1186/s13045-026-01785-8

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** CXCR4-antagonistic peptide-decorated lipid nanoparticles for co- delivery of AML1-ETO siRNA to enhance chemotherapy in refractory AML.

> **英文摘要：**
> Fusion protein AML1-ETO and chemokine receptor CXCR4 are crucial therapeutic targets for AML, the former plays a key role in differentiation blockade and leukemogenesis, and the latter is closely associated with drug resistance and relapse. This work developed a unified platform (referred as to E5-LNP@siAE) to integrate AML1-ETO-targeted RNA interference (RNAi) and CXCR4 antagonism by employing lipid nanoparticle (LNP) technology and antagonistic peptide E5 modification. The E5-LNP@siNC was slightly negative charged with 121.8 nm in diameter, showing homogenous spherical morphology and stability in PBS and 10% FBS. The E5-LNP@siAE could be specifically taken up by Kasumi-1 cells, down regulated levels of AML1-ETO, p-Erk and p-p38, and E5-LNP@siNC inhibited the CXCL12-mediated migration. In a refractory AML mouse model, E5-LNP@siAE monotherapy significantly reduced AML cells in peripheral blood, as well as infiltrations in the liver, lung and spleen. The expressions of CD11b, CD41a and Ter119 were upregulated while c-Kit decreased in the spleen of AML mice received E5-LNP@siAE treatment. The differentiation inductive effects were also observed in bone marrow mononuclear cells separated from AML patients with t(8;21) translocation. Moreover, E5-LNP@siAE significantly enhanced the therapeutic efficacy of doxorubicin (DOX) in the AML mice, evidenced by the reduced AML cells in peripheral blood, bone marrow and multiple organs, meanwhile, did not bring negative impacts on the counts of red blood cells and platelets. Consequently, the combination regimen achieved the much better result of survival prolongation than E5-LNP@siAE monotherapy, and the other control groups did not show therapeutic effects on the survival of the AML mice.

> **中文摘要：**
> 融合蛋白AML1-ETO和趋化因子受体CXCR4是AML的关键治疗靶点，前者在分化阻滞和白血病发生中起关键作用，而后者与耐药和复发密切相关。本研究通过采用脂质纳米颗粒（LNP）技术和拮抗肽E5修饰，开发了一个名为E5-LNP@siAE的统一平台，旨在整合靶向AML1-ETO的RNA干扰（RNAi）和CXCR4拮抗作用。E5-LNP@siNC带轻微负电荷，直径为121.8 nm，在磷酸盐缓冲液（PBS）和10%胎牛血清（FBS）中表现出均质的球形形态和稳定性。E5-LNP@siAE能被Kasumi-1细胞特异性摄取，下调AML1-ETO、p-Erk和p-p38的水平，而E5-LNP@siNC能抑制CXCL12介导的迁移。在难治性AML小鼠模型中，E5-LNP@siAE单药治疗显著减少了外周血中的AML细胞，并减轻了肝脏、肺部和脾脏的浸润。在接受E5-LNP@siAE治疗的AML小鼠脾脏中，CD11b、CD41a和Ter119的表达上调，而c-Kit减少。从具有t(8;21)易位的AML患者中分离出的骨髓单核细胞中也观察到了诱导分化作用。此外，E5-LNP@siAE显著增强了多柔比星（DOX）在AML小鼠中的疗效，表现为外周血、骨髓和多个器官中AML细胞的减少，同时未对红细胞和血小板计数产生负面影响。因此，联合治疗方案实现了比E5-LNP@siAE单药治疗更显著的生存期延长效果，而其他对照组未表现出对AML小鼠生存期的治疗作用。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该研究创新性地构建了双功能脂质纳米平台（E5-LNP@siAE），成功实现了CXCR4拮抗与AML1-ETO基因沉默的协同递送，直接针对难治性AML的分化阻滞与微环境相关耐药。实验不仅在细胞和动物水平验证了其诱导分化、抑制迁移及协同增敏化疗药物多柔比星的显著疗效，还在临床患者样本中观察到了明确的分化诱导作用。这种整合基因治疗与受体拮抗的策略，为攻克具有t(8;21)易位的难治性白血病提供了极具潜力的多靶点联合治疗方案。

---

## 21. GPRC5D 缺失增强了抗 GPRC5D 免疫治疗下骨髓瘤的增殖能力和竞争适应性

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41917280)
**期刊：** Leukemia
**PMID：** 41917280
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41375-026-02920-7

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Loss of GPRC5D enhances the proliferative capacity and competitive fitness of myeloma upon anti-GPRC5D immunotherapy.

> **英文摘要：**
> Immunotherapies targeting surface antigens have transformed the treatment landscape of multiple myeloma (MM), with GPRC5D emerging as a promising therapeutic target. Monoallelic loss of GPRC5D is frequently observed in newly diagnosed MM patients, and the incidence of acquired GPRC5D alterations increases following exposure to GPRC5D-directed therapies. However, the functional consequences of both baseline monoallelic and therapy-induced biallelic GPRC5D alterations remain poorly understood. In this study, we modeled monoallelic versus biallelic loss of GPRC5D to investigate their impact on MM cell biology and responsiveness to GPRC5D-targeted immunotherapies. Our results demonstrate that monoallelic GPRC5D loss in OPM-2 cells reduces surface expression of the antigen and confers resistance to GPRC5D-directed therapies. Complete loss of GPRC5D alters the transcriptional state of MM cells and promotes reprogramming of the phosphoproteomic circuitry ultimately resulting in a pro-proliferative chemokine environment. As a result, GPRC5D deficiency increases the basal proliferation rate of MM cells thereby providing a competitive advantage which may further be amplified by selecting these aggressive phenotypes during ongoing treatment with anti-GPRC5D immunotherapies.

> **中文摘要：**
> 以表面抗原为靶点的免疫疗法改变了多发性骨髓瘤（MM）的治疗格局，其中 GPRC5D 正成为一个极具前景的治疗靶点。在初诊 MM 患者中经常观察到 GPRC5D 的单等位基因缺失，而在接受 GPRC5D 定向治疗后，获得性 GPRC5D 改变的发生率会有所增加。然而，基线单等位基因缺失和治疗诱导的双等位基因 GPRC5D 改变的功能后果仍知之甚少。在本研究中，我们模拟了 GPRC5D 的单等位基因与双等位基因缺失，以研究它们对 MM 细胞生物学和对 GPRC5D 靶向免疫疗法反应性的影响。我们的研究结果表明，OPM-2 细胞中 GPRC5D 的单等位基因缺失会降低抗原的表面表达，并赋予细胞对 GPRC5D 定向疗法的抗性。GPRC5D 的完全缺失改变了 MM 细胞的转录状态，并促进了磷酸化蛋白组回路的重编程，最终导致了促增殖的趋化因子环境。因此，GPRC5D 缺陷增加了 MM 细胞的基础增殖速率，从而提供了竞争优势，而在持续的抗 GPRC5D 免疫治疗过程中，通过对这些侵略性表型的筛选，这种优势可能会进一步放大。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该研究通过构建单等位和双等位 GPRC5D 缺失模型，深入探讨了该靶点变异对多发性骨髓瘤细胞耐药性及生物学行为的影响。研究发现 GPRC5D 的完全缺失不仅通过降低抗原表达导致免疫逃逸，还通过重构转录组和磷酸化蛋白组信号通路创造了促增殖环境，显著增强了肿瘤细胞的适应性。这一发现揭示了抗 GPRC5D 治疗中耐药克隆演化的内在机制，为理解免疫治疗压力下的肿瘤进化及开发克服耐药的新策略提供了重要的科学依据。

---

## 22. 伊妥昔单抗通过细胞毒性作用在母细胞性浆细胞样树突状细胞肿瘤中诱导抗肿瘤活性

## 23. 本瑞利珠单抗对比安慰剂治疗高嗜酸性粒细胞综合征：一项随机、安慰剂对照的3期临床试验

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41917160)
**期刊：** Nature medicine
**PMID：** 41917160
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41591-026-04315-8

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Benralizumab versus placebo for hypereosinophilic syndrome: a randomized, placebo-controlled phase 3 trial.

> **英文摘要：**
> Benralizumab, an eosinophil-depleting anti-IL-5 receptor α antibody, has demonstrated efficacy in severe eosinophilic asthma and eosinophilic granulomatosis with polyangiitis and shown promising results in hypereosinophilic syndrome (HES). NATRON was a randomized, double-blind placebo-controlled phase 3 study evaluating the efficacy and safety of benralizumab in FIP1L1::PDGFRA-negative HES. The primary endpoint was time to first HES flare. In total, 133 patients (median (range) age 51 (14-87) years, 62% female) were randomized (1:1) to receive benralizumab 30 mg every 4 weeks or placebo for 24 weeks, in addition to background therapy. Benralizumab significantly reduced the risk of first flare versus placebo (hazard ratio 0.35, 95% CI 0.18 to 0.69, P = 0.0024). Adverse events occurred in 64.2% and 66.7% of benralizumab- and placebo-treated patients, respectively. Benralizumab's safety was consistent with its known profile. These results demonstrate the efficacy and safety of add-on benralizumab in the treatment of HES. ClinicalTrials.gov identifier: NCT04191304 .

> **中文摘要：**
> 本瑞利珠单抗（Benralizumab）是一种通过清除嗜酸性粒细胞起作用的抗白细胞介素-5（IL-5）受体α抗体，已在重症嗜酸性粒细胞性哮喘和嗜酸性肉芽肿性多血管炎中证明了疗效，并在高嗜酸性粒细胞综合征（HES）中显示出良好的前景。NATRON是一项随机、双盲、安慰剂对照的3期研究，评估了本瑞利珠单抗在FIP1L1::PDGFRA阴性HES患者中的有效性和安全性。主要终点是首次HES发作的时间。共有133名患者（中位年龄51岁 [范围14-87岁]，62%为女性）被随机（1:1）分配到在背景治疗的基础上，每4周接受一次30 mg本瑞利珠单抗或安慰剂治疗，持续24周。与安慰剂相比，本瑞利珠单抗显著降低了首次发作的风险（风险比 0.35，95% CI 0.18至0.69，P = 0.0024）。本瑞利珠单抗治疗组和安慰剂组发生不良事件的比例分别为64.2%和66.7%。本瑞利珠单抗的安全性与其已知的安全性特征一致。这些结果证明了本瑞利珠单抗作为辅助疗法治疗HES的有效性和安全性。ClinicalTrials.gov 标识符：NCT04191304。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

这项名为NATRON的3期临床试验系统性地验证了本瑞利珠单抗在FIP1L1::PDGFRA阴性HES患者中的临床价值。研究结果表明，该药物能显著降低65%的疾病发作风险，且安全性特征与既往研究一致，未发现新的安全风险。作为一种能够直接耗竭嗜酸性粒细胞的靶向疗法，本瑞利珠单抗为这种罕见且具有潜在生命威胁的血液系统疾病提供了强有力的证据支持，有望改变HES的临床治疗标准。

## 24. 微型且通用的基因组调节TnpB-ωRNA工具箱助力肿瘤免疫治疗

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41917051)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41917051
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-71327-w

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Miniature and versatile genome regulation TnpB-ωRNA toolkits facilitate cancer immunotherapy.

> **英文摘要：**
> CRISPR‒Cas systems represent powerful tools for genome regulation. However, the large size of Cas proteins limits their efficient delivery via an adeno-associated virus (AAV), thereby restricting their clinical translation. Here, we engineer the IS200/IS605 transposon-encoded nuclease TnpB, along with its ωRNA scaffold, to create an enhanced TnpB system, which serves as a compact toolkit for gene activation, genome editing, and base editing. The gene activator enTnpBa increases expression by 2889-fold with a minimized 93 nt ωRNA and robustly activates endogenous genes in mammalian cells. We develop a single-AAV-based regimen for immune activation (AAV-ImmunAct) that delivers enTnpBa to activate CXCL9, IL-15, and IFN-γ. AAV-ImmunAct effectively enhances T cell migration and activation, increases killing of cancer cell lines and patient-derived organoids, and synergizes with anti-PD-1 therapy in humanized mice. Here, we establish enTnpB as a compact and versatile platform for genome regulation and a promising tool for cancer immunotherapy.

> **中文摘要：**
> CRISPR-Cas系统是基因组调节的强大工具。然而，Cas蛋白的巨大体积限制了其通过腺相关病毒（AAV）的有效递送，从而制约了其临床转化。在这里，我们对IS200/IS605转座子编码的核酸酶TnpB及其ωRNA支架进行了工程化改造，创建了一个增强型TnpB系统，该系统可作为基因激活、基因组编辑和碱基编辑的紧凑型工具箱。基因激活因子enTnpBa配合最短化的93 nt ωRNA可将表达量提高2889倍，并能稳健地激活哺乳动物细胞中的内源性基因。我们开发了一种基于单一AAV的免疫激活方案（AAV-ImmunAct），递送enTnpBa以激活CXCL9、IL-15和IFN-γ。AAV-ImmunAct有效增强了T细胞的迁移和激活，增加了对癌细胞系和患者来源类器官的杀伤力，并在人源化小鼠中与抗PD-1疗法产生协同作用。在此，我们将enTnpB确立为一个紧凑且通用的基因组调节平台，以及一种极具前景的肿瘤免疫治疗工具。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该研究针对传统CRISPR系统由于蛋白分子量过大导致AAV递送困难的痛点，创新性地开发了基于微型转座子蛋白TnpB的基因调节工具箱。作者通过对TnpB及其ωRNA的工程化改造，显著提升了其在哺乳动物细胞中的基因激活效率，并实现了单一AAV载体介导的多靶点免疫激活。实验证明该系统在增强T细胞杀伤效力以及与免疫检查点阻断疗法协同方面具有显著优势，为肿瘤免疫基因治疗提供了一个极具临床转化潜力的紧凑型技术平台。

## 25. 管腔系谱丢失驱动预处理后的 ER+ HER2- 局部晚期或转移性乳腺癌对新一代 ERα 拮抗剂产生耐药

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41917040)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41917040
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-71233-1

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Loss of luminal lineage drives resistance to next-generation ERα antagonists in pretreated ER HER2 locally-advanced or metastatic breast cancer.

> **英文摘要：**
> Next-generation selective estrogen receptor-α (ERα) antagonist/degraders (SERDs) are being developed for ER-positive breast cancer (ER BC), with intentions of improving outcomes for patients. In recent clinical trials of metastatic ER BC, next-generation SERDs demonstrated clinical activity, and elacestrant received an approval for advanced ESR1-mutant disease. However, responses to these drugs were highly heterogeneous: across trials and independent of ESR1 status, 30-50% of patients progressed by their first follow-up scan while other patients sustained benefit for 2 years or more. Here, we interrogate the basis for heterogeneous responses by comparing biopsies from non-responding patients (NR; progression-free survival <2 months) and responding patients (Resp; PFS ≥ 2 months) who received the next-generation SERD giredestrant. While Resp tumors maintain high dependency on ERα signaling, NR tumors exhibit loss of luminal lineage identity and by extension, ERα dependence. NR tumors instead up-regulate multiple ERα-independent proliferative pathways, such as EGFR/MAPK and Hippo/TEAD, which may represent targetable dependencies in NR disease. Modeling resistance and lineage plasticity in vitro, we find that giredestrant-resistant ER BC cell lines exhibit profound shifts in chromatin accessibility, with the transcription factors, FOXA1 and FOXM1, implicated in gene expression of NR-upregulated proliferative pathways.

> **中文摘要：**
> 新一代选择性雌激素受体-α（ERα）拮抗剂/降解剂（SERDs）正在研发中，旨在改善 ER 阳性乳腺癌（ER+ BC）患者的预后。在最近的转移性 ER+ BC 临床试验中，新一代 SERDs 显示出临床活性，且 elacestrant 已获批用于晚期 ESR1 突变型疾病。然而，患者对这些药物的反应具有高度异质性：在各项试验中，无论 ESR1 状态如何，30-50% 的患者在首次随访扫描时已出现疾病进展，而其他患者的获益可持续 2 年或更久。在此，我们通过比较接受新一代 SERD giredestrant 治疗的非缓解患者（NR；无进展生存期 <2 个月）和缓解患者（Resp；PFS ≥2 个月）的活检样本，探讨了这种异质性反应的基础。研究发现，虽然缓解期肿瘤维持对 ERα 信号传导的高度依赖，但非缓解期肿瘤表现出管腔系谱身份的丢失，进而导致对 ERα 依赖性的丧失。非缓解期肿瘤转而上调多种不依赖 ERα 的增殖通路，如 EGFR/MAPK 和 Hippo/TEAD，这可能代表了非缓解期疾病中可作为靶点的依赖性。通过在体外模拟耐药性和系谱可塑性，我们发现 giredestrant 耐药的 ER+ BC 细胞系表现出染色质可及性的深刻改变，转录因子 FOXA1 和 FOXM1 参与了非缓解期上调的增殖通路的基因表达。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该研究深入探讨了 ER+ 转移性乳腺癌对新一代 SERD（如 giredestrant）产生耐药的分子机制，揭示了管腔系谱身份的丢失是导致早期耐药的关键驱动因素。通过对比临床缓解与非缓解患者的活检样本，研究明确了非缓解肿瘤从 ER 依赖转向 EGFR/MAPK 及 Hippo/TEAD 等非依赖性通路的谱系重塑过程。研究不仅阐明了 FOXA1 和 FOXM1 在介导染色质重塑和耐药基因表达中的核心作用，还为克服 SERD 耐药提供了潜在的联合治疗靶点。这一发现对于筛选获益人群和开发针对性二线治疗方案具有重要的临床指导价值。

---

## 26. 胸部放射治疗中危及器官深度学习自动分割的前瞻性多中心试验

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41917034)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41917034
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70863-9

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** A prospective multicenter trial of deep learning auto-segmentation for organs at risk in thoracic radiotherapy.

> **英文摘要：**
> Widespread clinical implementation of rapidly evolving auto-segmentation tools remains constrained by a scarcity of high-quality prospective evidence. Here we show the results of a prospective, multicenter, observational trial (NCT05787522) evaluating the clinical performance of a deep learning model (iCurveE) for artificial intelligence (AI)-assisted delineation of organs at risk (OARs) in thoracic and breast cancer radiotherapy. Computed tomography images from 500 patients across five centers are annotated by 37 physicians using manual, AI-generated, and AI-assisted methods. Eleven thoracic OARs are evaluated based on the primary endpoints of volumetric Dice similarity coefficient (vDSC) and contouring time, alongside secondary metrics including 95% Hausdorff Distance (HD95). We prospectively annotate 2,483 OAR sets (27,043 OARs): 993 manual, 497 AI-generated, and 993 AI-assisted. AI-assisted delineation achieves significantly better vDSC (mean, 0.902) and HD95 (mean, 5.20 mm) than manual delineation (mean vDSC, 0.857; mean HD95, 8.01 mm; p < 0.0001) while improving time efficiency by 81.63% (median: 10.0 vs. 55.0 min; p < 0.0001). AI-assisted delineation reduces performance variability across centers and physicians with varying expertise. This study validates the clinical applicability of AI-assisted delineation in improving delineation performance and promoting healthcare equity.

> **中文摘要：**
> 快速发展的自动分割工具在临床上的广泛应用仍受限于高质量前瞻性证据的缺乏。在此，我们展示了一项前瞻性、多中心、观察性试验（NCT05787522）的结果，该试验评估了深度学习模型（iCurveE）在胸部和乳腺癌放射治疗中人工智能（AI）辅助危及器官（OARs）勾画的临床表现。来自5个中心的500名患者的计算机断层扫描图像由37名医生使用手动、AI生成和AI辅助方法进行了标注。根据体积Dice相似系数（vDSC）和勾画时间的主要终点，以及包括95%豪斯多夫距离（HD95）在内的次要指标，对11个胸部OARs进行了评估。我们前瞻性地标注了2,483组OAR（27,043个OAR）：其中993组为手动标注，497组为AI生成，993组为AI辅助标注。AI辅助勾画在实现显著优于手动勾画的vDSC（平均0.902对0.857）和HD95（平均5.20 mm对8.01 mm；p < 0.0001）的同时，将时间效率提高了81.63%（中位数：10.0分钟对55.0分钟；p < 0.0001）。AI辅助勾画减少了不同中心及不同专业水平医生之间的表现差异。本研究验证了AI辅助勾画在提高勾画性能和促进医疗公平方面的临床适用性。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究通过一项大规模、前瞻性、多中心临床试验，有力地论证了深度学习模型iCurveE在胸部放疗危及器官勾画中的价值。研究结果显示，AI辅助模式不仅在几何精度上全面超越传统手动勾画，且效率提升显著，勾画时间缩短了80%以上。尤为重要的是，AI技术的介入显著降低了不同医疗机构和不同经验水平医生间的勾画变异性，这对于实现放疗流程标准化和提升基层医疗质量具有深远的临床意义。

---

## 27. 在 CARDIA 研究中开发一种评估心血管疾病邻里社会决定因素的新型指数

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41917033)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41917033
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70741-4

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Developing a novel index for neighborhood social determinants of cardiovascular diseases in the CARDIA study.

> **英文摘要：**
> Neighborhood social determinants of health have been shown to influence cardiovascular risk and the development of cardiovascular disease, but few studies have been done about early-life exposure as well as the combined effect of multiple neighborhood social determinants of health measures. Each 1-standard-deviation increase in the neighborhood social determinants of health index is associated with increased risk of coronary artery calcification at the year 7, year 15, and year 20 visits (Odds Ratios range from 1.15 to 1.17). The area under the Receiver Operating Characteristics curve ranges between 0.718 (year 7) and 0.719 (year 20). Compared to White participants, Black participants have a significant association between neighborhood social determinants of health indices and coronary artery calcification at Y15 and at Y20. In conclusion, higher early adulthood neighborhood social determinants of health indices are associated with higher middle-aged coronary artery calcification risk; this association is significant in Black adults at older age compared with White adults.

> **中文摘要：**
> 邻里健康社会决定因素已被证明会影响心血管风险和心血管疾病的发展，但关于生命早期暴露以及多种邻里健康社会决定因素测量指标综合影响的研究较少。邻里健康社会决定因素指数每增加 1 个标准差，与第 7 年、第 15 年和第 20 年随访时的冠状动脉钙化风险增加相关（优势比范围为 1.15 至 1.17）。受试者工作特征曲线下面积介于 0.718（第 7 年）和 0.719（第 20 年）之间。与白人参与者相比，黑人参与者的邻里健康社会决定因素指数与第 15 年和第 20 年的冠状动脉钙化之间存在显著关联。总之，成年早期较高的邻里健康社会决定因素指数与中年时期较高的冠状动脉钙化风险相关；与白人成年人相比，这种关联在年龄较大的黑人成年人中具有显著性。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究通过 CARDIA 长期队列数据，创新性地开发了一种评估邻里健康社会决定因素（SDoH）的综合指数，填补了生命早期多维度社会环境暴露对心血管风险影响的研究空白。研究结果明确了 SDoH 与中年冠状动脉钙化风险之间的正相关关系，并揭示了这种关联在黑人族群中更为突出的种族差异。该指数不仅具有良好的预测效能，也为心血管疾病的早期社会干预提供了重要的量化工具和公共卫生依据。

## 28. 硫酸酯酶修饰因子控制斑马鱼聚合延伸形态发生的时机

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41917030)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41917030
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70804-6

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Sulfatase modifying factors control the timing of zebrafish convergence and extension morphogenesis.

> **英文摘要：**
> Convergence and extension (C&E) cell movements that elongate the primary embryonic axis are precisely timed during vertebrate gastrulation, but mechanisms controlling their onset remain unknown. Using zebrafish embryonic explants that recapitulate C&E and its timing, we identified sulfatase modifying factor 2 (sumf2) as a candidate trigger gene for C&E onset. sumf2 and its paralog sumf1 encode negative and positive sulfatase regulators, respectively, whose expression levels invert and increase heparan sulfate sulfation during gastrulation. Overexpressing sumf1 or sumf2 causes delayed or precocious C&E, respectively, whereas their loss shifts C&E timing in the opposite direction. We identified Sulf1, a modifier of heparan sulfate proteoglycans (HSPGs), as their key downstream effector and found that altering heparan sulfate sulfation levels shifts C&E onset and suppresses sumf1 and sumf2 mutant phenotypes. This work supports a model in which sumf2 expression reduces sulfatase activity, rewriting HSPG sulfation patterns to promote the onset of C&E morphogenesis.

> **中文摘要：**
> 延长原肠期胚胎主轴的聚合延伸 (C&E) 细胞运动在脊椎动物原肠胚形成过程中受到精确的时间调控，但控制其启动的机制仍不清楚。利用能够重现 C&E 及其时机的斑马鱼胚胎外植体，我们鉴定出硫酸酯酶修饰因子 2 (sumf2) 是 C&E 启动的候选触发基因。sumf2 及其旁系同源基因 sumf1 分别编码硫酸酯酶的负向和正向调节因子，它们的表达水平在原肠胚形成过程中发生反转并增加硫酸乙酰肝素的硫酸化。过表达 sumf1 或 sumf2 分别导致 C&E 延迟或早熟，而它们的缺失则使 C&E 时机向相反方向移动。我们鉴定出硫酸乙酰肝素蛋白多糖 (HSPGs) 的修饰因子 Sulf1 是它们的关键下游效应因子，并发现改变硫酸乙酰肝素的硫酸化水平会改变 C&E 的启动并抑制 sumf1 和 sumf2 突变体的表型。这项工作支持了一个模型，即 sumf2 的表达降低了硫酸酯酶活性，通过重写 HSPG 硫酸化模式来促进 C&E 形态发生的启动。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究聚焦于脊椎动物发育过程中聚合延伸（C&E）运动的时间调控机制，通过斑马鱼模型揭示了硫酸酯酶修饰因子 sumf1 和 sumf2 的关键作用。研究发现 sumf2 通过抑制硫酸酯酶活性，重塑了硫酸乙酰肝素蛋白多糖（HSPG）的硫酸化模式，从而充当 C&E 启动的生化触发开关。该工作不仅填补了形态发生时机控制基因机制的空白，还深入阐述了糖胺聚糖修饰在胚胎发育时空精确性中的核心地位，具有极高的学术创新性。

---

## 29. 一种通过非经典STING途径选择性激活I型干扰素的仿生纳米圆盘系统用于癌症免疫治疗

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41917023)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41917023
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-71363-6

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** A biomimetic nanodisc system selectively activates type I interferons by nonclassical STING pathway for cancer immunotherapy.

> **英文摘要：**
> The epigenetic silencing or remarkably diminished expression of STING in cancer cells, along with the structural and functional impairment of the endoplasmic reticulum (ER) and Golgi apparatus, represents a unique mechanism of tumor immune escape and poses an important challenge for STING-targeted therapies. Here, we develop a cell membrane-derived nanodisc system (ND-cGAMP-HP; HP, heparin), which is capable of presenting activated STING proteins in their native form by means of cell membrane-directed display and biological self-assembly techniques. It can directly introduce activated STING protein to tumor cells and circumvent the translocation process between the ER and Golgi apparatus, selectively activating the IFN-I signaling pathway without initiating the inflammation-related pathway NF-κB. ND-cGAMP-HP triggers potent cellular immune responses and remodels the tumor immune microenvironment. Moreover, it augments immune memory by promoting the differentiation of TCF1 stem cell-like T cells. We thus manifest a strategy based on STING therapy that does not depend on the ER and Golgi apparatus pathways to activate the IFN-I pathway, for cancer immunotherapy.

> **中文摘要：**
> 癌细胞中STING的表观遗传沉默或表达显著减少，以及内质网（ER）和高尔基体的结构和功能受损，代表了一种独特的肿瘤免疫逃逸机制，并对靶向STING的疗法提出了重要挑战。在此，我们开发了一种细胞膜衍生的纳米圆盘系统（ND-cGAMP-HP；HP，肝素），该系统能够通过细胞膜定向展示和生物自组装技术，以天然形式呈递激活的STING蛋白。它能直接将激活的STING蛋白引入肿瘤细胞，并绕过内质网与高尔基体之间的易位过程，从而选择性地激活I型干扰素（IFN-I）信号通路，而不启动炎症相关的NF-κB通路。ND-cGAMP-HP可触发强效的细胞免疫反应并重塑肿瘤免疫微环境。此外，它通过促进TCF1干细胞样T细胞的分化来增强免疫记忆。因此，我们证明了一种基于STING疗法的策略，该策略不依赖于内质网和高尔基体通路来激活IFN-I通路，从而用于癌症免疫治疗。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究开发了一种创新的仿生纳米圆盘系统ND-cGAMP-HP，旨在克服肿瘤细胞中STING表达缺陷或经典内质网/高尔基体易位途径障碍导致的免疫逃逸。其核心创新在于通过外源性呈递天然形式的活化STING蛋白，实现了不依赖于宿主细胞转运机制的IFN-I通路精准激活，且有效规避了促炎的NF-κB途径。该系统在重塑免疫微环境和诱导持久免疫记忆方面表现出色，为STING激动剂类药物的临床转化提供了全新的策略。

## 30. 哺乳动物胚胎植入前发育过程中染色体外环状DNA（eccDNAs）的图谱及调控潜力

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41917015)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41917015
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-71227-z

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** The landscape and regulatory potential of eccDNAs in mammalian preimplantation embryos.

> **英文摘要：**
> Extrachromosomal circular DNA is an emerging regulatory element implicated in genomic stability and gene regulation, yet its role in preimplantation development remains elusive. Here, we report the widespread presence of extrachromosomal circular DNA in preimplantation embryos, characterized by homologous junction sequences and originating from genomic regions enriched for active histone marks and RNA Polymerase II occupancy. Functional perturbations demonstrate that RNA Polymerase II inhibition suppresses extrachromosomal circular DNA production, whereas disruption of the Fanconi anemia pathway elevates it, suggesting that transcription-replication conflicts affect its biogenesis. Notably, extrachromosomal circular DNA levels surge during major zygotic genome activation. Synthetic extrachromosomal circular DNAs carrying putative enhancers for the zygotic genome activation genes Mycn and Egfl7, and the developmental gene Emx1, significantly upregulate the expression of their respective genes upon transfection into fibroblasts and zygotes. Collectively, this study unveils the extrachromosomal circular DNA landscape in preimplantation embryos, elucidates a transcription-replication conflict mechanism underlying its generation, and establishes its regulatory potential during mammalian preimplantation development.

> **中文摘要：**
> 染色体外环状DNA（eccDNA）是一种新兴的调控元件，涉及基因组稳定性和基因调控，但其在胚胎植入前发育中的作用仍不清楚。在此，我们报告了eccDNA在植入前胚胎中的广泛存在，其特征是具有同源连接序列，并起源于富含活性组蛋白标记和RNA聚合酶II占据的基因组区域。功能干预表明，抑制RNA聚合酶II会抑制eccDNA的产生，而破坏范可尼贫血（Fanconi anemia）通路则会增加其产生，这表明转录-复制冲突影响了其生物合成。值得注意的是，eccDNA水平在合子基因组激活（ZGA）的主要阶段激增。携带合子基因组激活基因Mycn和Egfl7以及发育基因Emx1推定增强子的合成eccDNA，在转染至成纤维细胞和合子后，显著上调了其各自基因的表达。总之，本研究揭示了植入前胚胎中eccDNA的图谱，阐明了其产生的转录-复制冲突机制，并确立了其在哺乳动物植入前发育过程中的调控潜力。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究首次系统地描绘了哺乳动物胚胎植入前发育阶段的染色体外环状DNA（eccDNA）景观图谱，填补了该领域的空白。研究不仅揭示了eccDNA起源于活跃转录区且受转录-复制冲突驱动的生成机制，还通过合成eccDNA转染实验证实了其作为调控元件在合子基因组激活（ZGA）中的关键作用。该发现为理解早期胚胎发育的非染色体遗传调控提供了重要的新视角，具有极高的学术价值和创新性。

## 31. CASD1催化过程中高尔基体唾液酸O-乙酰化的SLC33A1依赖性与非依赖性相互作用

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41917001)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41917001
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-71333-y

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Interplay of SLC33A1-dependent and -independent Golgi sialic acid O-acetylation in CASD1 catalysis.

> **英文摘要：**
> Sialic acid O-acetylation is implicated in the modulation of sialoglycan recognition and ganglioside biology. The sugar modification is catalyzed by CASD1, a Golgi membrane protein that encompasses a luminal catalytic domain and a multipass transmembrane domain. The mechanism of how acetyl-CoA is provided to the Golgi remains poorly understood. Here, we show that the acetyl-CoA transporter SLC33A1 provides acetyl-CoA to the luminal domain of CASD1 and that patient-derived SLC33A1 variants linked to inherited neurodevelopmental and neurodegenerative disorders impair ganglioside 9-O-acetylation. Under conditions that enable the formation of 7,9-di-O-acetylated sialoglycans, genetic inactivation of SLC33A1 impaired di-O-acetylation, but unexpectedly, still enabled mono-O-acetylation. Structure prediction and site-directed mutagenesis revealed a second active site in CASD1 that shares striking similarities with the catalytic acetyl-CoA binding transmembrane tunnel of the lysosomal acetyltransferase HGSNAT. Together, our data provide strong evidence that CASD1 has dual functionalities and catalyzes 7,9-di-O-acetylation through SLC33A1-dependent luminal acetylation and SLC33A1-independent transmembrane acetylation.

> **中文摘要：**
> 唾液酸O-乙酰化参与调节唾液酸聚糖识别和神经节苷脂生物学。这种糖基修饰由CASD1催化，CASD1是一种包含管腔催化结构域和多跨膜结构域的高尔基体膜蛋白。乙酰辅酶A（acetyl-CoA）如何提供给高尔基体的机制仍不清楚。在此，我们展示了乙酰辅酶A转运体SLC33A1为CASD1的管腔结构域提供乙酰辅酶A，并且与遗传性神经发育和神经退行性疾病相关的患者来源SLC33A1变体损害了神经节苷脂的9-O-乙酰化。在能够形成7,9-二-O-乙酰化唾液酸聚糖的条件下，SLC33A1的基因灭活损害了二-O-乙酰化，但出乎意料的是，仍然能够进行单-O-乙酰化。结构预测和定点诱变揭示了CASD1中的第二个活性位点，该位点与溶酶体乙酰转移酶HGSNAT的催化乙酰辅酶A结合跨膜通道具有显著相似性。总之，我们的数据提供了强有力的证据，表明CASD1具有双重功能，并通过SLC33A1依赖的管腔乙酰化和SLC33A1非依赖的跨膜乙酰化催化7,9-二-O-乙酰化。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究深入探讨了高尔基体中唾液酸O-乙酰化的催化机制，重点揭示了关键酶CASD1的功能多样性。研究发现乙酰辅酶A转运体SLC33A1不仅为CASD1管腔催化提供底物，其变体还与多种神经系统疾病相关。最具创新性的是，作者通过结构预测与实验验证，发现CASD1拥有一个类似于HGSNAT的跨膜催化位点，从而实现了独立于SLC33A1的乙酰化途径。该双重功能模型的建立，为理解复杂糖基修饰及其在神经发育中的病理生理作用提供了全新的分子基础。

## 32. 单次屏息3D腹部代谢MRI实现肝癌的无标记诊断

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41917000)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41917000
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-71124-5

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Single-breath-hold 3D abdominal metabolic MRI enables label-free diagnosis of liver cancer.

> **英文摘要：**
> Chemical exchange saturation transfer (CEST) MRI could detect proteins/peptides, creatine, glucose, and glycogen by labeling their exchangeable amide, amine, and hydroxyl groups respectively, via frequency-selective RF pulses. Without the need for contrast agents or specialized hardware, CEST can be conveniently integrated into existing clinical MR protocols. However, its abdominal application is limited by long scan time (> 5 min) and susceptibility to respiratory motion (60-70% successful scan rate). We develop an ultra-fast 3D CEST MRI approach using spatial-spectral encoding (SSE), enabling a full spectral scan of whole-liver 3D images within a single breath-hold. SSE-CEST employs an efficient z-ω encoding pattern by applying a saturation gradient, followed by a data-driven spatial spectral reconstruction based on the low-rankness of CEST spectra. SSE-CEST is comprehensively evaluated in glycogen phantoms, ex vivo porcine liver, healthy volunteers and patients. Single breath-hold SSE-CEST largely improves successful rate, with a correlation of 0.95 between two repeated scans. SSE-CEST enables the detection of multi-metabolite changes in the liver and pancreas after an overnight fasting, and the dynamic mapping of hepatic glucose metabolism during an oral glucose test. For liver cancer patients, SSE could differentiate active lesions from post-treatment necrosis, featuring superior in-slice spatial resolution and motion-stabilized images. SSE-CEST MRI potentially could facilitate the diagnosis and patient management for liver and other abdominal diseases.

> **中文摘要：**
> 化学交换饱和转移 (CEST) MRI 可通过频率选择性射频脉冲分别标记蛋白质/多肽、肌酸、葡萄糖和糖原中可交换的酰胺基、胺基和羟基，从而实现对这些物质的检测。在无需对比剂或专用硬件的情况下，CEST 可以方便地集成到现有的临床磁共振协议中。然而，其在腹部的应用受限于较长的扫描时间（超过5分钟）以及对呼吸运动的敏感性（成功率仅为60-70%）。我们开发了一种基于空谱编码 (SSE) 的超快速 3D CEST MRI 方法，能够在单次屏息内完成全肝 3D 图像的全谱扫描。SSE-CEST 通过施加饱和梯度采用高效的 z-ω 编码模式，随后基于 CEST 光谱的低秩性进行数据驱动的空谱重建。研究在糖原模型、离体猪肝、健康志愿者及患者中对 SSE-CEST 进行了全面评估。单次屏息 SSE-CEST 大幅提高了扫描成功率，两次重复扫描之间的相关性达0.95。SSE-CEST 能够检测禁食一夜后肝脏和胰腺的多代谢物变化，并能对口服葡萄糖试验期间的肝脏葡萄糖代谢进行动态成像。对于肝癌患者，SSE 凭借卓越的层内空间分辨率和运动稳定的图像，能够区分活性病变与治疗后的坏死组织。SSE-CEST MRI 有望促进肝脏及其他腹部疾病的诊断和患者管理。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该研究提出了一种基于空谱编码（SSE）的超快速3D CEST MRI技术，旨在解决传统腹部代谢成像扫描时间长且易受呼吸伪影干扰的临床痛点。通过在单次屏息内实现全肝3D代谢成像，该技术显著提升了扫描成功率，并在区分肝癌活性病灶与治疗后坏死方面展现出优越性能。其核心创新在于结合了高效的z-ω编码与低秩约束的数据驱动重建算法，为肝脏及腹部器官的无标记、定量代谢评估提供了极具临床转化潜力的影像学手段。

## 33. 同步放化疗联合尼妥珠单抗对比单纯同步放化疗治疗诱导化疗反应不佳的局部晚期鼻咽癌：一项随机2期临床试验

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41916997)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41916997
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-71019-5

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Concurrent chemoradiotherapy plus nimotuzumab versus chemoradiotherapy alone for locoregionally advanced nasopharyngeal carcinoma with a suboptimal response to induction chemotherapy: a randomized phase 2 trial.

> **英文摘要：**
> Induction chemotherapy (IC) followed by concurrent chemoradiotherapy (CCRT) is the standard treatment for locoregionally advanced nasopharyngeal carcinoma (LA-NPC); however, patients with a suboptimal response to IC, defined as detectable Epstein-Barr virus DNA and/or stable or progressive disease after IC, remain at high risk of treatment failure. Here we report an open-label, randomised, phase 2 trial evaluating whether adding nimotuzumab, a humanised anti-epidermal growth factor receptor antibody, to CCRT improves outcomes in this high-risk population. A total of 246 patients with untreated, non-keratinising, stage II-IVA LA-NPC were randomly assigned (1:1) to receive CCRT with or without nimotuzumab. The primary endpoint was 2-year progression-free survival (PFS); secondary endpoints included overall survival, distant metastasis-free survival, locoregional relapse-free survival, short-term response rate, and safety. At a median follow-up of 47 months, the 2-year PFS was 81.0% (90% confidence interval [CI], 74.3-86.1) in the nimotuzumab plus CCRT group and 80.8% (90% CI, 74.2-85.7) in the CCRT-alone group (hazard ratio, 0.93 [90% CI, 0.63-1.37]; p = 0.70). Survival outcomes were similar between groups, while low-grade rash occurred more frequently with nimotuzumab. These findings indicate that adding nimotuzumab to CCRT does not improve survival in patients with LA-NPC with a suboptimal response to IC, underscoring the need for predictive biomarkers and alternative therapeutic strategies. Trial registration: NCT04223024.

> **中文摘要：**
> 诱导化疗（IC）序贯同步放化疗（CCRT）是局部晚期鼻咽癌（LA-NPC）的标准治疗方案；然而，对于IC反应不佳（定义为IC后可检测到爱泼斯坦-巴尔病毒[EBV] DNA和/或疾病稳定或进展）的患者，仍面临较高的治疗失败风险。在此，我们报告了一项开放标签、随机、2期临床试验，旨在评估在CCRT的基础上加用尼妥珠单抗（一种人源化抗表皮生长因子受体抗体）是否能改善这一高危人群的预后。共有246名初治、非角化型II-IVA期LA-NPC患者被随机分配（1:1）接受联合或不联合尼妥珠单抗的CCRT治疗。主要终点是2年无进展生存率（PFS）；次要终点包括总生存率、远处无转移生存率、局部无复发生存率、近期有效率和安全性。在中位随访47个月时，尼妥珠单抗联合CCRT组的2年PFS为81.0%（90%置信区间 [CI], 74.3-86.1），而单纯CCRT组为80.8%（90% CI, 74.2-85.7）（风险比为0.93 [90% CI, 0.63-1.37]；p = 0.70）。两组间的生存结果相似，而尼妥珠单抗组发生低级别皮疹的频率更高。这些发现表明，在CCRT中加入尼妥珠单抗并不能改善对IC反应不佳的LA-NPC患者的生存率，这凸显了对预测性生物标志物和替代治疗策略的需求。临床试验注册号：NCT04223024。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究聚焦于诱导化疗反应不佳这一局部晚期鼻咽癌预后差的亚群，通过随机2期试验评估了加用抗EGFR单抗尼妥珠单抗的临床获益。结果显示，虽然联合用药安全性良好，但在2年无进展生存率及总生存率上均未观察到显著提升。该研究以严谨的试验设计给出了阴性结论，有力地证明了单纯通过增加抗EGFR靶向药难以克服化疗反应不佳带来的治疗耐药，为未来探索新型生物标志物及免疫联合方案提供了重要的反面证据和研究方向。

---

## 34. PD-1阻断联合酪氨酸激酶抑制剂重塑晚期肾细胞癌的肿瘤微环境

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41916996)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41916996
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70978-z

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** PD-1 blockade plus tyrosine kinase inhibitor remodels the tumor microenvironment in advanced renal cell carcinoma.

> **英文摘要：**
> The combination of tyrosine kinase inhibitors (TKIs) and immune checkpoint inhibitors (ICIs) has improved clinical outcomes in advanced renal cell carcinoma (aRCC), though therapeutic resistance remains a major challenge. We conducted single-cell transcriptomic analysis on 61 tumor samples from 34 aRCC patients treated with TKIs alone or in combination with ICIs. Non-responders exhibited increased neutrophil infiltration and enrichment of SAA+ tumor cells following treatment. We identified a VEGF+CEACAM1+ neutrophil subset exhibiting immunosuppressive properties that is associated with poor clinical response. In vivo, pharmacologic inhibition of SAA enhanced sensitivity to ICI plus TKI combination therapy, while blockade of the CEACAM1-TIM-3 axis in humanized PD-1 mouse models significantly potentiated anti-PD-1 efficacy. Our study establishes a single-cell atlas of the aRCC tumor microenvironment under treatment pressure and identifies a previously unrecognized SAA-CEACAM1-TIM-3 axis driving drug resistance, highlighting potential targets to improve therapy efficacy.

> **中文摘要：**
> 酪氨酸激酶抑制剂（TKIs）与免疫检查点抑制剂（ICIs）的联合应用改善了晚期肾细胞癌（aRCC）的临床预后，但治疗耐药性仍是一个主要挑战。我们对接受单独TKI或TKI联合ICI治疗的34名aRCC患者的61份肿瘤样本进行了单细胞转录组分析。非响应者在治疗后表现出中性粒细胞浸润增加和SAA+肿瘤细胞富集。我们鉴定出一类具有免疫抑制特性的VEGF+CEACAM1+中性粒细胞亚群，该亚群与不良的临床反应相关。在体内实验中，药理学抑制SAA增强了对ICI加TKI联合疗法的敏感性，而在人源化PD-1小鼠模型中阻断CEACAM1-TIM-3轴显著增强了抗PD-1的疗效。我们的研究建立了治疗压力下aRCC肿瘤微环境的单细胞图谱，并发现了一个先前未被识别的驱动耐药性的SAA-CEACAM1-TIM-3轴，强调了提高疗效的潜在靶点。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究通过对接受联合治疗的晚期肾癌患者进行大规模单细胞测序，成功构建了治疗压力下的肿瘤微环境动态图谱。研究的核心创新点在于发现了由SAA+肿瘤细胞和VEGF+CEACAM1+中性粒细胞共同构成的免疫抑制微环境，并首次阐明了SAA-CEACAM1-TIM-3这一全新的耐药轴。通过体内实验验证了阻断该轴可显著逆转免疫耐药，为临床解决TKI+ICI联合治疗耐药问题提供了极具前景的新靶点。尽管机制详实，但该发现仍需在更广泛的临床队列中进行验证以评估其作为生物标志物的普适性。

---

## 35. 古菌和真核生物的 MCM 环序贯解链 DNA 以启动复制

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41916983)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41916983
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70961-8

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Archaeal and eukaryotic MCM rings sequentially melt DNA for replication initiation.

> **英文摘要：**
> DNA replication initiation requires local melting of fully base-paired DNA for a helicase to gain a foothold and initiate processive DNA unwinding. In eukaryotes and archaea, the helicase engine is the hexameric ring minichromosome maintenance (MCM) complex. In eukaryotes, a defined biochemical sequence assembles two Cdc45-MCM-GINS (CMG) complexes that provide limited DNA unwinding as the species that immediately precedes extensive unwinding. A prior structure revealed how MCM subunits interact with this form of DNA, but the atomic progression from undistorted DNA to this melted DNA species is unknown. Here, we present a sequential DNA melting mechanism determined by snapshots of an archaeal MCM ring with DNA in varying degrees of melting. In this mechanism, successive ATP-binding at MCM ATPase sites drives sequential discrete DNA melting steps mediated a specific MCM aromatic residue. Analysis of eukaryotic structures shows loaded MCM rings principally adopt only two molecular arrangements at the ATPase: one that does not melt DNA and one tuned to melt DNA with equivalent aromatic residues, indicating a universal sequential mechanism melts DNA in archaea and eukaryotes for replication initiation.

> **中文摘要：**
> DNA 复制启动需要完全碱基配对的 DNA 发生局部解链，以便解旋酶获得立足点并启动进行性 DNA 解旋。在真核生物和古菌中，解旋酶的核心引擎是六聚体环状微小染色体维持 (MCM) 复合物。在真核生物中，一个明确的生化序列组装了两个 Cdc45-MCM-GINS (CMG) 复合物，作为广泛解旋之前的中间体提供有限的 DNA 解旋。先前的结构揭示了 MCM 亚基如何与这种形式的 DNA 相互作用，但从无扭曲 DNA 到这种解链 DNA 状态的原子级进展过程尚不清楚。在此，我们通过处于不同解链程度的古菌 MCM 环与 DNA 结合的快照，展示了一种序贯 DNA 解链机制。在该机制中，MCM ATP 酶位点的连续 ATP 结合驱动了由特定 MCM 芳香族残基介导的序贯离散 DNA 解链步骤。对真核生物结构的分析表明，加载的 MCM 环在 ATP 酶处主要仅采用两种分子排列：一种不解链 DNA，另一种则通过等效的芳香族残基调节以解链 DNA，这表明在古菌和真核生物中存在一种通用的序贯机制来解链 DNA 以启动复制。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究通过冷冻电镜技术捕捉了古菌 MCM 环在不同解链阶段的动态快照，揭示了 DNA 复制启动过程中关键的序贯解链机制。研究发现，MCM 复合物通过 ATP 酶位点的连续 ATP 结合，利用特定的芳香族残基驱动离散的解链步骤，实现了从稳定双链到解链状态的原子级转变。通过与真核生物结构对比，该研究证明了这种序贯解链机制在进化上的高度保守性，为理解生命体 DNA 复制起始的分子基础提供了重要的结构生物学证据。

---

## 36. 知母皂苷 AIII 通过削弱 CAR-Tregs 来增强 CAR-T 细胞效力并防止复发

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41916982)
**期刊：** Nature communications
**PMID：** 41916982
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41467-026-70867-5

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Timosaponin AIII enhances CAR-T cell potency and prevents relapse through impairing CAR-Tregs.

> **英文摘要：**
> Chimeric antigen receptor (CAR)-T cell therapy has transformed treatment of relapsed/refractory DLBCL, yet resistance driven by regulatory T cells (Tregs) limits its efficacy. Here we identify Timosaponin AIII (TAIII), a clinical-stage natural product, as an effective modulator of CAR-T function that depletes CAR-Tregs while enhancing effector activity. Mechanistically, TAIII acts as an allosteric A2AR inhibitor by competing with cholesterol, suppressing CREB-dependent FoxP3 transcription and disrupting the A2AR-Treg axis. Ablation of A2AR or Tregs in vitro and in vivo abolishes TAIII activity, confirming specificity. Furthermore, TAIII reduces intratumoral Tregs, increases CD8⁺ T cells infiltration, and potentiates PD-1 blockade in solid tumor models. Importantly, TAIII promotes central memory T-cell formation and enhances CAR-T cytotoxic cytokine secretion. Combining or pretreating CAR-T cells with TAIII markedly improves antitumor efficacy and prevents late relapse across preclinical models. These findings establish TAIII as a combinatorial strategy to deplete CAR-Tregs, enhance CAR-T activity, and extend therapeutic durability.

> **中文摘要：**
> 嵌合抗原受体 (CAR)-T 细胞疗法改变了复发/难治性弥漫性大 B 细胞淋巴瘤 (DLBCL) 的治疗现状，但由调节性 T 细胞 (Tregs) 驱动的耐药性限制了其疗效。在此，我们鉴定出一种处于临床阶段的天然产物——知母皂苷 AIII (TAIII)，它是一种有效的 CAR-T 功能调节剂，能够清除 CAR-Tregs 并同时增强效应活性。从机制上讲，TAIII 通过与胆固醇竞争发挥别构 A2AR 抑制剂的作用，从而抑制 CREB 依赖性 FoxP3 转录并破坏 A2AR-Treg 轴。在体外和体内消融 A2AR 或 Tregs 会消除 TAIII 的活性，从而证实了其特异性。此外，在实体瘤模型中，TAIII 减少了瘤内 Tregs，增加了 CD8⁺ T 细胞浸润，并增强了 PD-1 阻断剂的效力。重要的是，TAIII 促进了中心记忆 T 细胞的形成并增强了 CAR-T 细胞毒性细胞因子的分泌。将 CAR-T 细胞与 TAIII 联合使用或进行预处理，可显著提高抗肿瘤效力，并在多种临床前模型中防止后期复发。这些发现确立了 TAIII 作为一种联合策略，可清除 CAR-Tregs、增强 CAR-T 活性并延长治疗持久性。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究创新性地发现天然产物知母皂苷 AIII (TAIII) 可作为别构 A2AR 抑制剂，通过竞争胆固醇结合位点精准清除 CAR-Tregs 并诱导 CAR-T 细胞向中心记忆表型转化。研究不仅阐明了 TAIII 调节 FoxP3 转录的分子机制，还通过多种临床前模型证明了其在增强实体瘤浸润及预防后期复发方面的显著效力。这一发现为克服 CAR-T 细胞疗法的免疫抑制微环境耐药提供了极具临床转化前景的联合治疗策略。

## 37. TGF-βR1 抑制剂 galunisertib 通过限制蜕膜样自然杀伤细胞极化来重塑 PDAC 肿瘤微环境

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41916960)
**期刊：** Cell death & disease
**PMID：** 41916960
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41419-026-08581-9

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** The TGF-βR1 inhibitor galunisertib re-shapes the PDAC-TME by limiting decidual-like natural killer cells polarization.

> **英文摘要：**
> Pancreatic ductal adenocarcinoma (PDAC) is the third leading cause of cancer-related mortality worldwide. Natural Killer (NKs) cells are pivotal for tumor surveillance but are dysfunctional in PDAC. We evaluated whether pharmacological blockade of TGF-β1/TGF-βR1 axis in PDAC cells and cancer-associated fibroblasts (CAFs) could modulate NK polarization via soluble factors. The phenotype/functions of NKs from PDAC patients versus healthy controls (HC) were compared, and the polarization state of NKs exposed to the conditioned media of PDAC cells and fibroblasts was evaluated by flow cytometry. The ability of galunisertib (GAL) to reverse NK dysfunction in immunocompetent mice orthotopically implanted with FC1199 PDAC cells was evaluated. PDAC patients showed higher TGF-β1/ TGF-βR1 levels than HC, with worse outcomes in TGF-β1/TGF-βR1 patients. Circulating CD9 NKs were expanded in PDAC patients compared with HC and exhibited a pro-angiogenic secretome and higher pro-angiogenic activities in vitro and in vivo (leech Hirudo verbana), compared to the CD9 NK cells. PDAC cells and CAF induced a CD9-decidual-like phenotype, also impairing NK degranulation. GAL treatment restrains PDAC cell/CAF-induced NK anergy, restoring their cytotoxicity. Also, TGFβ-R1 knockdown in PDAC cells exhibited the capability to limit the generation of decidual-like NKs, while restoring their antitumor ability, via soluble factors. Secretome profiling of BxPC3 and MIAPaCA2 PDAC cell lines and CAFs showed that GAL downregulated the release of several growth, angiogenic, and immunoregulatory factors, including FGF2, HGF, IL11, PLGF, EGFR, and VEGF. In vivo in orthotopic tumors formed by FC1199 cells GAL decreased CD9-NK frequency, promoted M1-macrophage polarization, and activated NK and CD8T-cells, together with a significant reduction of tumor weight, fibrosis and inhibition of angiogenesis. Our study identifies CD9NKs as a novel cell subset expanded in PDAC and underscores the role of TGF-β1/TGF-βR1 signalling in promoting a pro-tumoral NKs GAL-treatment emerges as immunomodulator able in re-educating pro-tumor NKs cells in PDAC.

> **中文摘要：**
> 胰腺导管腺癌 (PDAC) 是全球癌症相关死亡的第三大原因。自然杀伤 (NK) 细胞对肿瘤监测至关重要，但在 PDAC 中功能失调。我们评估了在 PDAC 细胞和癌症相关成纤维细胞 (CAFs) 中通过药理学阻断 TGF-β1/TGF-βR1 轴是否可以通过可溶性因子调节 NK 极化。我们比较了 PDAC 患者与健康对照 (HC) 的 NK 细胞表型/功能，并通过流式细胞术评估了暴露于 PDAC 细胞和成纤维细胞条件培养基中的 NK 细胞极化状态。评估了 galunisertib (GAL) 在原位植入 FC1199 PDAC 细胞的免疫健全小鼠中逆转 NK 功能障碍的能力。研究发现，PDAC 患者表现出比 HC 更高的 TGF-β1/TGF-βR1 水平，且 TGF-β1/TGF-βR1 水平较高的患者预后较差。与 CD9- NK 细胞相比，循环 CD9+ NK 细胞在 PDAC 患者中较 HC 显著扩增，并表现出促血管生成的效应组分以及在体内和体外（医蛭 Hirudo verbana）更高的促血管生成活性。PDAC 细胞和 CAF 诱导了 CD9+ 蜕膜样表型，同时也损害了 NK 细胞的脱颗粒作用。GAL 处理抑制了 PDAC 细胞/CAF 诱导的 NK 细胞无反应性，恢复了其细胞毒性。此外，PDAC 细胞中的 TGFβ-R1 敲低显示出通过可溶性因子限制蜕膜样 NK 细胞产生的能力，同时恢复了其抗肿瘤能力。对 BxPC3 和 MIAPaCA2 PDAC 细胞系及 CAFs 的分泌组分析显示，GAL 下调了多种生长、血管生成和免疫调节因子的释放，包括 FGF2、HGF、IL11、PLGF、EGFR 和 VEGF。在由 FC1199 细胞形成的原位肿瘤体内实验中，GAL 降低了 CD9+ NK 的频率，促进了 M1 型巨噬细胞极化，并激活了 NK 和 CD8+ T 细胞，同时显著减轻了肿瘤重量、纤维化并抑制了血管生成。我们的研究将 CD9+ NK 细胞确定为在 PDAC 中扩增的新型细胞亚群，并强调了 TGF-β1/TGF-βR1 信号传导在促进促肿瘤型 NK 细胞中的作用。GAL 处理作为一种免疫调节剂，能够重新教育 PDAC 中的促肿瘤 NK 细胞。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究深入揭示了 TGF-β1/TGF-βR1 信号通路在重塑胰腺导管腺癌 (PDAC) 免疫微环境中的核心作用，重点鉴定了 CD9+ 蜕膜样 NK 细胞这一新型促肿瘤细胞亚群。通过使用 galunisertib (GAL) 阻断该信号轴，研究成功展示了在体外及原位肿瘤模型中逆转 NK 细胞功能衰竭、恢复其细胞毒性并抑制肿瘤进展的潜力。该研究的创新之处在于阐明了肿瘤分泌因子对 NK 细胞极化的调控机制，为 PDAC 提供了针对肿瘤微环境重塑的潜在免疫治疗新策略。

## 38. 通过流式细胞术双重评估 cyTRBC1 和 cyTRBC2 在识别表面 CD3 阴性至弱表达 T 细胞克隆性中的应用价值

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41916956)

**PMID：** 41916956
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41408-026-01483-1

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Utility of dual assessment of cyTRBC1 and cyTRBC2 by flow cytometry for identifying clonality in sCD3-negative to dimly expressing T cells.

> **英文摘要：**

> **中文摘要：**

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究针对表面CD3（sCD3）阴性或弱表达的特殊T细胞群体，探讨了胞内TRBC1与TRBC2双重评估在克隆性鉴定中的临床价值。该方法利用流式细胞术克服了传统免疫表型分析在诊断不典型T细胞肿瘤时的局限性，为精准识别异常T细胞克隆提供了创新的技术路径。这种双指标策略显著提升了淋巴增殖性疾病的诊断效能，尤其在缺乏典型表面标记表达的情况下，展现出极高的实用性和病理诊断参考价值。

## 39. Teclistamab治疗的多发性骨髓瘤患者中巨细胞病毒再激活的临床结局及风险因素研究

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41916955)
**期刊：** Blood cancer journal
**PMID：** 41916955
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41408-026-01484-0

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Clinical outcomes and risk factors of cytomegalovirus reactivation in teclistamab-treated multiple myeloma patients.

> **英文摘要：**
> Teclistamab, a bispecific T-cell engager targeting BCMA and CD3, has demonstrated efficacy in relapsed/refractory multiple myeloma but may increase infection risk due to immunosuppression. Cytomegalovirus (CMV) reactivation is a concern in immunocompromised patients, yet its incidence and clinical significance in teclistamab-treated patients remain poorly characterized. We conducted a retrospective analysis of 177 multiple myeloma patients who received teclistamab between December 2022 and December 2024. We assessed CMV reactivation incidence, risk factors, and clinical outcomes. Binary logistic regression identified predictors of CMV reactivation. CMV testing was done in 173 (98%) patients. CMV reactivation occurred in 38 patients (22%) during teclistamab treatment, with a median initial viral load of 87.2 IU/mL (range: 37.1-4807.0). The median highest CMV level was 288 IU/mL (range: 45.3-20,000). Most reactivations were asymptomatic (89.5%), with only four symptomatic cases, three requiring treatment, and no end-organ damage. Eight patients (21.1%) experienced second viremia episodes. Multivariable analysis identified prior CMV reactivation as a significant predictor (OR = 3.34, p = 0.005). CMV reactivation did not impact overall survival (p = 0.673). Prophylactic IVIG use was associated with improved survival (HR = 0.49, p = 0.011). CMV reactivation occurs in approximately one-fifth of teclistamab-treated multiple myeloma patients but is typically asymptomatic and does not affect survival. Prior CMV reactivation predicts subsequent reactivation. These findings support risk-stratified CMV monitoring approaches in this population.

> **中文摘要：**
> Teclistamab是一种靶向BCMA和CD3的双特异性T细胞衔接器，已在复发/难治性多发性骨髓瘤中显示出疗效，但由于免疫抑制作用，可能会增加感染风险。巨细胞病毒（CMV）再激活是免疫功能受损患者关注的问题，但在接受teclistamab治疗的患者中，其发生率和临床意义尚不明确。我们对2022年12月至2024年12月期间接受teclistamab治疗的177名多发性骨髓瘤患者进行了回顾性分析。我们评估了CMV再激活的发生率、风险因素和临床结局。通过二元逻辑回归确定了CMV再激活的预测因子。173名（98%）患者进行了CMV检测。在teclistamab治疗期间，38名患者（22%）发生了CMV再激活，中位初始病毒载量为87.2 IU/mL（范围：37.1-4807.0）。中位最高CMV水平为288 IU/mL（范围：45.3-20,000）。大多数再激活为无症状（89.5%），仅有4例有症状病例，其中3例需要治疗，且无终末器官损伤。8名患者（21.1%）经历了第二次病毒血症发作。多变量分析确定既往CMV再激活是显著的预测因子（OR = 3.34, p = 0.005）。CMV再激活不影响总生存期（p = 0.673）。预防性使用静脉注射免疫球蛋白（IVIG）与生存获益相关（HR = 0.49, p = 0.011）。CMV再激活发生在大约五分之一接受teclistamab治疗的多发性骨髓瘤患者中，但通常为无症状且不影响生存。既往CMV再激活可预测后续再激活。这些发现支持在该人群中采取基于风险分层的CMV监测方法。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究通过对177例真实世界患者的回顾性分析，填补了BCMA/CD3双特异性抗体治疗中CMV再激活临床数据的空白。研究揭示了teclistamab治疗中CMV再激活虽具一定发生率（22%），但多为自限性且不影响短期生存，具有重要的临床定心丸作用。同时，研究明确了既往再激活史的预测价值，并意外发现预防性IVIG对生存的改善，为该类患者的免疫支持治疗提供了新的实证依据。

---

## 40. 利用真实世界队列开发并跨国验证多发性骨髓瘤特异性共病指数：CAREMM-2108

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41916953)
**期刊：** Blood cancer journal
**PMID：** 41916953
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41408-026-01475-1

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Development and multinational validation of a multiple myeloma-specific comorbidity index using real-world cohorts: CAREMM-2108.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND: Frailty and comorbidity substantially influence clinical outcomes in patients with multiple myeloma (MM), yet existing tools such as the IMWG frailty score and Charlson Comorbidity Index (CCI) have limitations in real-world applicability and disease specificity. OBJECTIVE: To develop and externally validate a multiple myeloma-specific comorbidity index (MM-CI) using real-world data from Korean and Japanese cohorts. MATERIALS AND METHODS: This retrospective study was conducted in two parts: (I) development of MM-CI using a nationwide Korean claims cohort of 17,273 MM patients diagnosed between 2007 and 2022; and (II) external validation using two independent multicenter registry cohorts: 1473 Korean patients (2010-2021) and 314 Japanese patients (2008-2023). Multivariable Cox regression was performed incorporating key clinical factors, including ECOG performance status, R2-ISS stage, and frontline treatment intensity. RESULTS: The MM-CI was derived from eight variables: male sex; age 60-69, 70-79, and ≥80 years; congestive heart failure, cerebrovascular disease, hepatic disease, and cancer: 1 × (Sex: Male) + 2 × (Age: 60-69 years) + 4 × (Age: 70-79 years) + 6 × (Age ≥80 years) + 2 × (Congestive heart failure: Yes) + 1 × (Cerebrovascular disease: Yes) + 1 × (Hepatic disease: Yes) + 1 × (Cancer: Yes). Risk scores stratified patients into four groups: low (0-2), intermediate-I (3-4), intermediate-II (5), and high (≥6), with corresponding median overall survival (OS) of 72.5, 43.8, 30.9, and 20.3 months, respectively. Validation analyses demonstrated superior predictive performance of the MM-CI (AUC: 0.637) compared to the conventional age-adjusted CCI (AUC: 0.613) and the concise CCI used in the IMWG frailty score (AUC: 0.569). The MM-CI remained independently prognostic after adjustment for ECOG, R2-ISS, and treatment intensity. CONCLUSION: The MM-CI provides a simple, objective, and clinically applicable tool for comorbidity-based risk stratification in MM. It outperforms existing models and may support treatment decisions in real-world practice.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景：衰弱和共病显著影响多发性骨髓瘤（MM）患者的临床结局，然而现有工具如IMWG衰弱评分和查尔森共病指数（CCI）在真实世界的适用性和疾病特异性方面存在局限性。目的：利用来自韩国和日本队列的真实世界数据，开发并外部验证一种多发性骨髓瘤特异性共病指数（MM-CI）。材料与方法：这项回顾性研究分为两个部分：（I）利用2007年至2022年间确诊的17,273名MM患者的韩国全国医保报销队列开发MM-CI；（II）利用两个独立的、多中心登记队列进行外部验证，包括1,473名韩国患者（2010-2021年）和314名日本患者（2008-2023年）。研究采用了多变量Cox回归分析，并纳入了关键临床因素，包括ECOG体能状态评分、R2-ISS分期和一线治疗强度。结果：MM-CI由8个变量推导得出：男性；年龄60-69岁、70-79岁和≥80岁；充血性心力衰竭、脑血管疾病、肝病和癌症：1 × (性别：男) + 2 × (年龄：60-69岁) + 4 × (年龄：70-79岁) + 6 × (年龄≥80岁) + 2 × (充血性心力衰竭：有) + 1 × (脑血管疾病：有) + 1 × (肝病：有) + 1 × (癌症：有)。根据风险评分将患者分为四组：低危（0-2）、中危-I（3-4）、中危-II（5）和高危（≥6），对应的中位总生存期（OS）分别为72.5、43.8、30.9和20.3个月。验证分析表明，与传统的年龄调整CCI（AUC: 0.613）和IMWG衰弱评分中使用的简明CCI（AUC: 0.569）相比，MM-CI具有更优的预测性能（AUC: 0.637）。在对ECOG、R2-ISS和治疗强度进行调整后，MM-CI仍具有独立的预后价值。结论：MM-CI为多发性骨髓瘤基于共病的风险分层提供了一种简单、客观且具有临床适用性的工具。其性能优于现有模型，并可为真实世界临床实践中的治疗决策提供支持。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究通过对超过1.7万名多发性骨髓瘤患者的大规模真实世界数据进行分析，成功构建并验证了首个疾病特异性的共病指数（MM-CI）。该工具通过整合性别、年龄及四类关键共病，实现了比传统CCI更精准的生存预测（AUC 0.637），并表现出良好的跨国适用性。尽管其预测效能仍有提升空间，但其简洁的评分体系为临床医生在复杂真实世界环境下优化MM患者的个体化治疗方案提供了客观的循证支持。

---

## 41. 双趋化因子武装的溶瘤塞内卡病毒A协同招募cDC1和CXCR3+ T细胞，转化“冷”黑色素瘤并驱动持久的肿瘤退缩

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41916730)
**期刊：** Journal for immunotherapy of cancer
**PMID：** 41916730
**DOI：** 10.1136/jitc-2025-014258

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Dual-chemokine-armed oncolytic Senecavirus A co-recruits cDC1 and CXCR3 T cells to convert 'cold' melanoma and drive durable regression.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND: Oncolytic virotherapy represents a promising anticancer strategy by combining direct tumor lysis with in situ immune activation. However, its efficacy remains limited in immune-cold tumors, which are characterized by poor T-cell infiltration and an immunosuppressive microenvironment. Although engineering oncolytic viruses to deliver chemokines has been explored to modulate immune recruitment, most existing approaches activate only a single immune axis. Senecavirus A (SVA), a tumor-selective RNA virus with high genetic stability and flexible transgene capacity, offers an attractive platform for coordinated intratumoral delivery of immune payloads. METHODS: We engineered recombinant SVA vectors to achieve co-expression of CXCL11 and vXCL1 within tumor, aiming to synergistically recruit both T cells and cross-presenting dendritic cells and remodel the tumor immune landscape. In vitro and in vivo assays were conducted to assess viral properties (stability, replication kinetics, gene expression) and cytotoxicity against B16-F10 melanoma cells in different stages, with tumor burden, immune cell infiltration, and mouse survival in C57BL/6 mice analyzed to evaluate the overall therapeutic efficacy. RESULTS: Signal-peptide deletion significantly improved the genetic stability of transgenes and enhanced intratumoral payload retention, without compromising viral fitness. In murine models, CXCL11-expressing virus monotherapy achieved enhanced tumor control, prolonged survival, and provided preliminary evidence suggestive of protection on tumor rechallenge. Furthermore, the combination of CXCL11 and vXCL1 further augmented dendritic cell activation, promoted CD8 T cell infiltration, and shifted macrophages toward an M1-polarized phenotype, while sustaining higher intratumoral viral loads. These coordinated immune changes led to deeper and more durable tumor regression. CONCLUSIONS: Our findings validate the combination of CXCL11- and vXCL1-armed SVA as a potent immunovirotherapy strategy and propose a design principle for multistage, multigene intervention: concurrently targeting leukocyte recruitment, antigen presentation, and effector activation provides complementary mechanisms that synergistically amplify therapeutic efficacy.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景：溶瘤病毒疗法通过将直接肿瘤裂解与原位免疫激活相结合，代表了一种极具前景的抗癌策略。然而，其在以T细胞浸润匮乏和免疫抑制微环境为特征的免疫“冷”肿瘤中疗效受限。虽然已探索通过改造溶瘤病毒递送趋化因子来调节免疫招募，但现有方法大多仅激活单一免疫轴。塞内卡病毒A（SVA）作为一种具有高遗传稳定性和灵活转基因容量的肿瘤选择性RNA病毒，为肿瘤内协调递送免疫载荷提供了一个极具吸引力的平台。方法：我们构建了重组SVA载体以实现在肿瘤内共同表达CXCL11和vXCL1，旨在协同招募T细胞和交叉呈递树突状细胞，并重塑肿瘤免疫景观。通过开展体外和体内实验评估了病毒特性（稳定性、复制动力学、基因表达）以及对不同阶段B16-F10黑色素瘤细胞的细胞毒性，并分析了C57BL/6小鼠的肿瘤负担、免疫细胞浸润和存活率，以评价整体治疗效果。结果：信号肽缺失显著提高了转基因的遗传稳定性，并增强了肿瘤内载荷的保留，且不损害病毒的适应性。在小鼠模型中，表达CXCL11的病毒单药治疗实现了增强的肿瘤控制和延长的生存期，并提供了提示肿瘤再次挑战保护作用的初步证据。此外，CXCL11和vXCL1的组合进一步增强了树突状细胞的活化，促进了CD8+ T细胞的浸润，并将巨噬细胞向M1极化表型转变，同时维持了更高的肿瘤内病毒载量。这些协调的免疫变化导致了更深层且更持久的肿瘤退缩。结论：我们的研究结果证实了CXCL11和vXCL1武装的SVA组合是一种强效的免疫溶瘤病毒疗法策略，并提出了一种多阶段、多基因干预的设计原则：同时针对白细胞招募、抗原呈递和效应器激活，可提供互补机制以协同增强治疗效果。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究通过利用塞内卡病毒A（SVA）作为递送平台，成功开发出一种共表达CXCL11和vXCL1的双趋化因子溶瘤病毒。该设计精妙地解决了免疫“冷”肿瘤对单一干预反应不佳的痛点，通过信号肽优化增强了病毒稳定性与载荷驻留。实验数据充分证明了该疗法在招募cDC1和激活CXCR3+ T细胞方面的协同作用，为多靶点协同增强免疫溶瘤疗效提供了重要的理论支撑和设计准则。

---

## 42. 肿瘤突变负荷在早期非小细胞肺癌新辅助和辅助免疫检查点抑制剂治疗中的临床价值

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41916729)
**期刊：** Journal for immunotherapy of cancer
**PMID：** 41916729
**DOI：** 10.1136/jitc-2025-014168

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Clinical value of tumor mutational burden for neoadjuvant and adjuvant immune checkpoint inhibitor in early-stage non-small cell lung cancer.

> **英文摘要：**
> Tumor mutational burden (TMB) and PD-L1 are established biomarkers for guiding immune checkpoint inhibitor (ICI) therapy in advanced non-small cell lung cancer (NSCLC). As ICI use expands into early-stage disease, we explored the feasibility of using TMB, which can be determined via a comprehensive genomic profiling assay along with  and  genomic alterations, as a biomarker for outcomes in both neoadjuvant and adjuvant settings. TMB-high status (≥10 mut/Mb) showed a numerically higher, but not statistically significant, rate of pathological complete response among patients receiving neoadjuvant ICI and significantly associated with more favorable time to recurrence in patients receiving adjuvant ICI, particularly among patients with PD-L1 expression <50%. TMB should be considered in future early-stage NSCLC ICI clinical trials to further validate these results.

> **中文摘要：**
> 肿瘤突变负荷（TMB）和 PD-L1 是指导晚期非小细胞肺癌（NSCLC）免疫检查点抑制剂（ICI）治疗的既定生物标志物。随着 ICI 治疗的应用扩展到早期疾病阶段，我们探索了将 TMB 作为新辅助和辅助治疗预后生物标志物的可行性；TMB 可通过综合基因组谱分析与基因组变异检测共同确定。研究结果显示，在接受新辅助 ICI 治疗的患者中，高 TMB 状态（≥10 mut/Mb）表现出数值上较高但无统计学显著差异的病理完全缓解率；而在接受辅助 ICI 治疗的患者中，高 TMB 与更有利的复发时间显著相关，尤其是在 PD-L1 表达 <50% 的患者群体中。为了进一步验证这些结果，未来的早期 NSCLC ICI 临床试验应考虑纳入 TMB 评估。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究评估了 TMB 在早期 NSCLC 围手术期免疫治疗中的预测价值，旨在将晚期肺癌的成熟标志物向早期阶段延伸。研究发现高 TMB 与辅助治疗后的复发风险降低显著相关，尤其在 PD-L1 低表达亚组中展现出更强的临床分层潜力。虽然新辅助阶段的病理获益尚未达到统计学意义，但其数据趋势和在辅助阶段的显著相关性，为未来早期肺癌精准免疫治疗方案的优化和多维度标志物整合提供了重要的循证支持。

---

## 43. 常用处方药作为艰难梭菌感染的风险因素：一项瑞典基于人群的病例对照研究

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41916675)
**期刊：** Gut
**PMID：** 41916675
**DOI：** 10.1136/gutjnl-2025-337629

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Commonly prescribed drugs as risk factors for Clostridioides difficile infections: a Swedish population-based case-control study.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND: infections (CDIs) are associated with antibiotic use, although the link with other drugs remains underexplored.
> 
> OBJECTIVES: To investigate the association between antibiotic and non-antibiotic drugs with microbiome-modulating activity on new occurrences of CDI.
> 
> DESIGN: We conducted a Swedish population-based case-control study from 2006 to 2019 including 42 921 cases matched with 355 159 population controls on age and sex, obtained from multiple linked Swedish registries. The effect of antibiotic and non-antibiotic use within 30 days from the index date on CDI occurrence was estimated using multivariable conditional logistic regression additionally with a lasso penalty. Models were adjusted for age and sex by design and for Charlson Comorbidity Index and concomitant drug use, providing adjusted ORs (aORs) with 95% CIs.
> 
> RESULTS: Antibiotics with the greatest CDI risk were lincosamides (aOR=31.4, 95% CI 27.9 to 35.3), combinations of penicillins (aOR=19.8, 95% CI 15.9 to 24.5), sulfonamides and trimethoprim, and cephalosporins, though no association for tetracyclines. Among non-antibiotic drugs, we found decreased risks of CDI for lipid-modifiers (aOR=0.8, 95% CI 0.8 to 0.8) and aspirin (aOR=0.8, 95% CI 0.7 to 0.8) and increased risks for antidiarrhoeals (aOR=7.3, 95% CI 6.8 to 7.8), corticosteroids (aOR=2.4, 95% CI 2.3 to 2.5), proton-pump inhibitors (PPIs) (aOR=1.8, 95% CI 1.7 to 1.8), nervous system drugs, constipation drugs, histamine H2-receptor antagonists, antidepressants, and beta blockers, but no significant risk for non-steroidal anti-inflammatory drugs.
> 
> CONCLUSIONS: We found varying effects of antibiotics on CDI, providing evidence for ongoing efforts in prudent prescribing decisions and antimicrobial stewardship. We confirmed PPI as a main risk factor for CDI and provided new evidence for other non-antibiotic drugs as potentially important risk factors considering their high prescription prevalence.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景：艰难梭菌感染（CDIs）与抗生素使用密切相关，但与其他药物之间的联系仍未得到充分探索。目的：调查具有微生物组调节活性的抗生素和非抗生素药物与 CDI 新发病例之间的关联。设计：我们开展了一项 2006 年至 2019 年的瑞典基于人群的病例对照研究，包括 42,921 例病例，并根据年龄和性别从多个关联的瑞典登记库中匹配了 355,159 例人群对照。研究使用多变量条件逻辑回归并辅以 Lasso 惩罚，估算了索引日期前 30 天内使用抗生素和非抗生素药物对 CDI 发生的影响。模型针对年龄和性别进行了设计调整，并校正了查尔森合并症指数（Charlson Comorbidity Index）和合并用药情况，提供了调整后的比值比（aORs）及其 95% 置信区间（CIs）。结果：CDI 风险最高的抗生素是林可酰胺类（aOR=31.4, 95% CI 27.9 - 35.3）、青霉素类组合（aOR=19.8, 95% CI 15.9 - 24.5）、磺胺类和甲氧苄啶以及头孢菌素类，而四环素类未见显著关联。在非抗生素药物中，我们发现调脂药（aOR=0.8, 95% CI 0.8 - 0.8）和阿司匹林（aOR=0.8, 95% CI 0.7 - 0.8）可降低 CDI 风险；而止泻药（aOR=7.3, 95% CI 6.8 - 7.8）、皮质类固醇（aOR=2.4, 95% CI 2.3 - 2.5）、质子泵抑制剂（PPIs）（aOR=1.8, 95% CI 1.7 - 1.8）、神经系统药物、便秘药物、组胺 H2 受体拮抗剂、抗抑郁药和 β 受体阻滞剂的风险增加，但非甾体抗炎药无显著风险。结论：我们发现不同抗生素对 CDI 的影响程度各异，这为持续推动谨慎的处方决策和抗菌药物管理提供了证据。本研究确认了 PPI 是 CDI 的主要风险因素，并为其他考虑到处方普及率极高的非抗生素药物作为潜在的重要风险因素提供了新证据。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

这项大规模瑞典全国性病例对照研究通过关联多项注册数据，详尽描绘了抗生素及非抗生素药物对艰难梭菌感染（CDI）风险的影响图谱。研究不仅细化了不同类别抗生素的极高风险（尤其是林可酰胺类和联合青霉素类），更重要的突破在于揭示了除 PPI 之外的多类非抗生素药物（如止泻药、皮质类固醇及抗抑郁药等）与 CDI 风险的显著相关性。此外，调脂药和阿司匹林的潜在保护作用为未来研究提供了新方向，该研究对临床多重用药管理和感染预防具有重要的实证价值。

## 45. BPI26-015：利用临床医生引导的AI推理平台补充NCCN指南：BlueScrubs系统的评估

## 47. BPI26-016：通过人工智能 (AI) 技术解决方案加强公益网络医院（Safety Net Hospital）的指南符合性护理交付

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41916423)
**期刊：** Journal of the National Comprehensive Cancer Network : JNCCN
**PMID：** 41916423
**DOI：** 10.6004/jnccn.2025.7373

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** BPI26-016: Strengthening Guideline Compliant Care Delivery in a Safety Net Hospital Through Artificial Intelligence (AI) Enabled Technology Solutions.

> **英文摘要：**
> No abstract available.

> **中文摘要：**
> 暂无摘要。

**DOI：** 10.1002/advs.202517631

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** ECM-Stiffness Mediated Persistent Fibroblast Activation Requires Integrin and Formin Dependent Chromatin Remodeling.

> **英文摘要：**
> Transient activation of fibroblasts into contractile myofibroblasts is essential for extracellular matrix (ECM) production and remodeling during wound healing and tissue regeneration. While ECM-dependent mechanisms mediating transient activation is well studied, how fibroblasts switch from transient to a persistently activated state and drive fibrosis and aberrant tissue repair in diseases such as cancer is less understood. Here, we show that human cancer-associated fibroblasts (CAFs) switch from transient to persistently activated states upon prolonged exposure to stiff ECMs and stiffness-dependent secreted factors. This switch is accompanied by activation of ECM-stiffness-dependent mechanotransduction pathways and changes in the nuclear architecture and its association with chromatin. Mechanistically, we identify two pathways required for this switch- ECM ligand binding and activation of β1 integrins smoothens the nuclear lamina during prolonged exposure and reduces lamin-chromatin contacts while in parallel, exposure to the stiff ECM activates the formin mammalian Diaphanous-related formin 2 (mDia2) and independent of alterations in the nuclear architecture alters lamin-chromatin coupling, likely through its role in assembling nuclear actin. Importantly, we find that blocking either pathway prevents persistent myofibroblast activation, which is rescued by inhibition of histone deacetylases, indicating that dynamic chromatin modifications act downstream of these ECM-dependent pathways to maintain the persistently activated state. These findings link integrin-based ECM sensing to chromatin remodeling and fibroblast memory, with implications for stromal plasticity in the tumor microenvironment.

> **中文摘要：**
> 成纤维细胞向收缩性肌成纤维细胞的一过性激活，对于伤口愈合和组织再生过程中的细胞外基质（ECM）产生及重塑至关重要。虽然介导一过性激活的ECM依赖性机制已得到深入研究，但成纤维细胞如何从一过性状态转变为持续激活状态，并在癌症等疾病中驱动纤维化和异常组织修复，目前尚不清楚。在本文中，我们证明了人类癌症相关成纤维细胞（CAFs）在长期暴露于硬ECM和硬度依赖性分泌因子后，会从一过性激活状态转变为持续激活状态。这种转变伴随着ECM硬度依赖性机械转导通路的激活，以及细胞核结构及其与染色质结合方式的变化。从机制上讲，我们确定了这种转变所需的两条途径：长期暴露期间，ECM配体结合及β1整合素的激活使核纤层平滑并减少了核纤层与染色质的接触；与此同时，暴露于硬ECM会激活哺乳动物Diaphanous相关formin 2 (mDia2)，并以不依赖于核结构改变的方式改变核纤层-染色质偶联，这可能是通过其在组装核肌动蛋白中的作用实现的。重要的是，我们发现阻断任一途径都能防止肌成纤维细胞的持续激活，而通过抑制组蛋白去乙酰化酶可以挽救这一过程，这表明动态染色质修饰作用于这些ECM依赖性途径的下游，以维持持续激活状态。这些发现将基于整合素的ECM感知与染色质重塑和成纤维细胞记忆联系起来，对肿瘤微环境中的间质可塑性具有重要意义。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究深入探讨了癌症相关成纤维细胞（CAFs）从一过性激活向持续激活状态转变的机械生物学机制。研究创新性地揭示了硬细胞外基质（ECM）通过β1整合素介导的核纤层平滑以及mDia2驱动的染色质偶联改变，共同触发了下游的染色质重塑。该发现不仅阐明了“成纤维细胞记忆”形成的结构与表观遗传基础，还强调了动态染色质修饰在维持基质持续活化中的核心作用，为靶向肿瘤微环境中的间质可塑性提供了新的理论支撑。
