## 384. 冒烟型多发性骨髓瘤的诊断、风险分层与管理

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41571958)
**期刊：** Nature reviews. Clinical oncology
**PMID：** 41571958
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41571-026-01119-0

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Diagnosis, risk stratification and management of smouldering multiple myeloma.

> **英文摘要：**
> New therapies have markedly improved survival outcomes for patients with multiple myeloma (MM). However, the onset of active disease, as defined by the 2014 International Myeloma Working Group SLiM-CRAB criteria, is often linked to substantial and irreversible morbidity. MM always develops from an asymptomatic precursor state called smouldering multiple myeloma (SMM). The clinical trajectory of SMM varies considerably; low-risk SMM often has an indolent course, similar to monoclonal gammopathy of undetermined significance, whereas nearly half of the subset of patients with high-risk SMM have progression to symptomatic MM within 2 years. Highly active treatments for MM, which remains an incurable disease, are being investigated for the management of SMM, with the aim of delaying or even preventing such progression. Both early therapeutic intervention and active surveillance are reasonable management options for patients with high-risk SMM, with decisions individualized through a detailed risk-benefit discussion with the patient. In this Review, we discuss current approaches for diagnostic evaluation, risk stratification and management of SMM, as well as future challenges and emerging opportunities in the field.

> **中文摘要：**
> 新型疗法显著改善了多发性骨髓瘤（MM）患者的生存结局。然而，根据2014年国际骨髓瘤工作组SLiM-CRAB标准定义的活动性疾病发作，通常与严重且不可逆的发病率相关。MM总是由一种被称为冒烟型多发性骨髓瘤（SMM）的无症状前驱状态发展而来。SMM的临床轨迹差异巨大；低危SMM通常病程进展缓慢，类似于意义未明的单克隆丙种球蛋白病（MGUS），而近半数高危SMM患者子集会在2年内进展为症状性MM。针对MM（目前仍无法治愈）的高活性治疗方法正被研究用于SMM的管理，旨在延迟甚至预防此类进展。早期治疗干预和主动监测对于高危SMM患者而言均是合理的管理选择，其决策需通过与患者进行详细的风险-获益讨论后实现个体化制定。在本综述中，我们讨论了目前SMM诊断评估、风险分层和管理的方法，以及该领域未来的挑战和新兴机遇。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本综述深入探讨了冒烟型多发性骨髓瘤（SMM）作为活动性骨髓瘤前驱阶段的临床重要性，系统总结了从无症状状态到恶性进展的风险评估体系。文章核心在于区分低危与高危SMM患者，并权衡了早期高强度治疗干预与主动监测的利弊，反映了当前血液肿瘤学向“精准预防”转化的趋势。其创新性地整合了最新的SLiM-CRAB标准，为优化SMM的个体化管理路径提供了权威的理论支撑与前瞻性见解。

## 385. 异质性中性粒细胞：调节肿瘤免疫的关键参与者

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41571211)
**期刊：** Biochimica et biophysica acta. Reviews on cancer
**PMID：** 41571211
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.bbcan.2026.189538

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Heterogeneous neutrophils: Key players in regulating tumor immunity.

> **英文摘要：**
> As the most abundant innate immune cells in bone marrow and peripheral blood, neutrophils were once considered functionally homogeneous and exerted inflammatory and anti-infection functions. However, emerging evidence reshapes the perception of neutrophils from passive effectors to dynamic regulators with high plasticity and heterogeneity, especially within the tumor microenvironment (TME). This review summarizes recent advances, particularly driven by single-cell technologies, demonstrating that tumor-associated neutrophils (TANs) represent a continuum of distinct functional states originating from heterogeneous developmental pathways in bone marrow, circulation and spleen. We classified TANs into diverse subsets based on unique molecular signatures and functions, including pro-tumor, inflammatory, interferon-stimulated genes (ISGs), and antigen-presenting subsets, and highlighted that TANs profoundly impacting tumor progression through distinct molecular mechanisms. Importantly, we delineate how TANs functionally interact with T cells, NK cells, macrophages and other immune cells, revealing the pivotal role of TANs in reconfiguring immune response networks to modulate tumor progression. Lastly, we discuss emerging therapeutic strategies targeting TAN recruitment, reprogramming, or specific pro-tumor subsets to overcome therapy resistance, aiming to provide insights for future research directions on neutrophils and the development of neutrophil-targeted cancer therapeutic strategies.

> **中文摘要：**
> 作为骨髓和外周血中最丰富的先天免疫细胞，中性粒细胞曾被认为在功能上是均一的，并发挥炎症和抗感染功能。然而，新兴证据重新塑造了对中性粒细胞的认知，使其从被动效应器转变为具有高度可塑性和异质性的动态调节因子，特别是在肿瘤微环境（TME）中。本综述总结了最近的进展，特别是由单细胞技术驱动的进展，证明了肿瘤相关中性粒细胞（TANs）代表了一系列独特的功能状态连续体，这些状态起源于骨髓、循环系统和脾脏中的异质发育途径。我们根据独特的分子特征和功能，将 TANs 分为多种亚群，包括促肿瘤、炎症、干扰素刺激基因（ISGs）和抗原呈递亚群，并强调了 TANs 通过不同的分子机制深刻影响肿瘤进展。重要的是，我们描绘了 TANs 如何在功能上与 T 细胞、NK 细胞、巨噬细胞和其他免疫细胞相互作用，揭示了 TANs 在重构免疫反应网络以调节肿瘤进展中的关键作用。最后，我们讨论了针对 TAN 招募、重编程或特定促肿瘤亚群的新兴治疗策略，以克服治疗耐药性，旨在为中性粒细胞的未来研究方向和针对中性粒细胞的癌症治疗策略的开发提供见解。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文全面综述了中性粒细胞从传统免疫效应器到复杂肿瘤调节因子的角色转变，重点探讨了单细胞技术背景下肿瘤相关中性粒细胞（TANs）的异质性与发育路径。作者通过对促肿瘤、炎症及抗原呈递等不同亚群的细致分类，深入解析了 TANs 在肿瘤微环境网络中与其他免疫细胞的互作机制。该综述不仅阐明了 TANs 调控肿瘤进展的分子逻辑，还前瞻性地提出了针对性清除或功能重塑 TANs 的临床治疗策略，对癌症免疫治疗的精准化设计具有重要的理论指导价值。

## 387. CX3CL1-CX3CR1轴的时空动态调节：肿瘤免疫微环境中的双刃剑与精准治疗新策略

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41564496)
**期刊：** Cytokine & growth factor reviews
**PMID：** 41564496
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.cytogfr.2026.01.006

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Spatiotemporal dynamic regulation of the CX3CL1-CX3CR1 axis: A double-edged sword in the tumor immune microenvironment and new strategies for precision therapy.

> **英文摘要：**
> The CX3CL1-CX3CR1 signaling axis is a key yet functionally contradictory regulatory hub within the tumor immune microenvironment (TME), with its output shaped by spatiotemporal dynamics. This review seeks to address the core scientific question of how this axis mediates both pro-tumor and anti-tumor effects simultaneously by analyzing a multi-layered regulatory framework. The duality of its function is rooted in two main mechanisms: (1) the regulation of CX3CL1 ligand cleavage by ADAM10/17 proteases, which determines the balance between membrane-bound (mCX3CL1, mediating adhesion) and soluble (sCX3CL1, mediating chemotaxis) isoforms; (2) the expression gradient of its sole receptor CX3CR1 on immune cells, which functions as a molecular code that precisely programs cell differentiation trajectories, such as the differentiation of CD8T cells from a stem-like state to a terminally exhausted state. Specific TME signals (such as TGF-β in pancreatic ductal adenocarcinoma (PDAC) and TLR4 signaling in colorectal cancer (CRC)) integrate these mechanisms and ultimately dictate distinct functional outputs. We propose that interventions targeting this axis must move beyond traditional agonist/antagonist approaches toward spatiotemporally specific precision control strategies, including intelligent delivery systems, CRISPR-based cell engineering, and AI-driven personalized treatments. Rationally reprogramming the functional orientation of this axis holds promise in overcoming immune checkpoint inhibitor resistance and provides a theoretical foundation for the development of a new generation of cancer immunotherapies.

> **中文摘要：**
> CX3CL1-CX3CR1 信号轴是肿瘤免疫微环境（TME）中一个关键但功能矛盾的调节枢纽，其输出受时空动态的调节。本综述旨在通过分析多层调节框架，探讨该轴如何同时介导促肿瘤和抗肿瘤作用的核心科学问题。其功能的双重性源于两个主要机制：（1）ADAM10/17 蛋白酶对 CX3CL1 配体切割的调节，决定了膜结合型（mCX3CL1，介导粘附）和可溶型（sCX3CL1，介导趋化）异构体之间的平衡；（2）其唯一受体 CX3CR1 在免疫细胞上的表达梯度，作为分子代码精确编程细胞分化轨迹，例如 CD8+ T 细胞从干细胞样状态向终末耗竭状态的分化。特定的 TME 信号（如胰腺导管腺癌 [PDAC] 中的 TGF-β 和结直肠癌 [CRC] 中的 TLR4 信号）整合了这些机制，并最终决定了不同的功能输出。我们建议，针对该轴的干预措施必须超越传统的激动剂/拮抗剂方法，转向具有时空特异性的精准控制策略，包括智能递送系统、基于 CRISPR 的细胞工程和 AI 驱动的个体化治疗。合理重编程该轴的功能取向有望克服免疫检查点抑制剂耐药性，并为开发新一代癌症免疫疗法提供理论基础。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本综述深入探讨了 CX3CL1-CX3CR1 信号轴在肿瘤免疫中的双重调节机制，重点剖析了配体切割及受体表达梯度如何决定其抗癌或促癌的功能取向。文章不仅从分子层面解释了该轴的功能矛盾性，还前瞻性地提出了整合 CRISPR 和 AI 技术的时空精准干预策略。这为克服免疫治疗耐药性提供了坚实的理论支撑，对开发下一代精准癌症免疫疗法具有重要的指导意义。

---

## 388. 区域淋巴结阳性膀胱癌：基于围手术期及晚期疾病临床试验结果的治疗决策

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41558886)
**期刊：** European urology
**PMID：** 41558886
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.eururo.2026.01.013

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Regional Node-positive Bladder Cancer: Therapeutic Decisions Based on Trial Results in Perioperative and Advanced Disease Settings.

> **英文摘要：**
> Optimal therapeutic management for cN1 M0 bladder cancer consists of perioperative systemic therapy and radical cystectomy. For patients with cN2-3 M0 disease, evidence supports upfront systemic therapy, preferably with enfortumab vedotin + pembrolizumab. Consolidative locoregional therapy may be an option in selected responders. Questions remain regarding the optimal duration of systemic therapy and the role of biomarkers. Multidisciplinary expert opinion can be critical for informed shared decision-making.

> **中文摘要：**
> cN1 M0期膀胱癌的最佳治疗管理包括围手术期全身治疗和根治性膀胱切除术。对于cN2-3 M0期患者，证据支持前期全身治疗，且首选维恩妥尤单抗（Enfortumab Vedotin）联合帕博利珠单抗（Pembrolizumab）。巩固性局部治疗可能是部分产生应答的患者的一种选择。关于全身治疗的最佳持续时间以及生物标志物的作用仍存在疑问。多学科专家意见对于知情的共同决策至关重要。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该文献系统总结了区域淋巴结阳性（cN+）非转移性膀胱癌的最新治疗范式，明确了针对cN1与cN2-3患者的差异化处理路径。文章强调了新型ADC药物联合免疫疗法（EV+PNA）在晚期分期中的关键地位，并探讨了巩固性局部治疗的潜在价值。尽管该综述基于最新试验结果为临床决策提供了有力支撑，但同时指出在治疗时程优化和精准生物标志物筛选方面仍面临挑战，体现了当前泌尿肿瘤领域向精准化与多学科协作发展的趋势。

---

## 389. 癌症生物学中的组蛋白乙酰转移酶 HBO1：核心机制及其对靶向治疗的意义

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41558589)
**期刊：** Biochimica et biophysica acta. Reviews on cancer
**PMID：** 41558589
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.bbcan.2026.189533

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Histone acetyltransferase HBO1 in cancer biology: Essential mechanisms and implications for targeted therapeutics.

> **英文摘要：**
> The histone acetyltransferase complex HBO1 (KAT7) is an oncogenic regulator across multiple cancers, promoting cell proliferation and migration. Though clinically important, no targeted therapies address HBO1 dysregulation. HBO1 forms complexes with MEAF6, JADE(1/2/3), ING(ING4/5), and BRPF1/2/3 to acetylate histones H3 and H4, especially at H3K14, promoting transcriptional activation and genomic stability. It colocalizes with active transcriptional sites and participates in gene regulation, DNA repair and replication. Most HBO1-associated cancer mutations are missense, though their effects remain unclear. Silencing HBO1 restores normal proliferation and gene expression, underscoring its oncogenic role. HBO1 activity supports cancer pathways, including apoptosis resistance, DNA damage response, and cell cycle regulation. The HBO1 inhibitor WM-3835 disrupts H3K14 acetylation, reducing tumor growth in several cancers. This review provides insights into the function of HBO1 in cancer, especially in histone acetylation, ubiquitination, stem cell maintenance, and pro- and anti-oncogenic signaling. Understanding the roles of HBO1 may guide new epigenetic therapies for HBO1-driven malignancies.

> **中文摘要：**
> 组蛋白乙酰转移酶复合物 HBO1 (KAT7) 是多种癌症中的致癌调节因子，促进细胞增殖和迁移。尽管其在临床上具有重要意义，但目前尚无针对 HBO1 失调的靶向疗法。HBO1 与 MEAF6、JADE(1/2/3)、ING(ING4/5) 以及 BRPF1/2/3 形成复合物，从而对组蛋白 H3 和 H4（尤其是 H3K14 位点）进行乙酰化，促进转录激活和基因组稳定性。它与活跃的转录位点共定位，并参与基因表达调控、DNA 修复和复制。大多数与 HBO1 相关的癌症突变为错义突变，但其具体影响尚不明确。沉默 HBO1 可恢复正常的细胞增殖和基因表达，进一步彰显了其致癌作用。HBO1 的活性支持包括凋亡抵抗、DNA 损伤反应和细胞周期调节在内的多种癌症相关通路。HBO1 抑制剂 WM-3835 可阻断 H3K14 乙酰化，从而抑制多种癌症中的肿瘤生长。本综述提供了关于 HBO1 在癌症中功能的见解，特别是在组蛋白乙酰化、泛素化、干细胞维持以及促癌和抑癌信号传导方面。深入理解 HBO1 的作用可能为 HBO1 驱动的恶性肿瘤指导开发新型表观遗传疗法。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文系统综述了组蛋白乙酰转移酶 HBO1 在癌症演进中的多重生物学功能，重点阐述了其通过 H3K14 乙酰化调控基因表达及维持基因组稳定性的分子机制。文章深入探讨了 HBO1 在多亚基复合物中的相互作用及其作为潜在治疗靶点的价值，特别是对小分子抑制剂 WM-3835 的药理作用进行了梳理。该综述不仅揭示了 HBO1 介导的表观遗传失调在促癌通路中的核心作用，也为针对 HBO1 驱动型恶性肿瘤的精准医疗提供了重要的理论支撑。

## 390. TGF-β-YY1 信号通路作为胰腺癌免疫逃逸的关键驱动因素：治疗意义

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41558149)
**期刊：** Cytokine & growth factor reviews
**PMID：** 41558149
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.cytogfr.2026.01.005

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** TGF-β-YY1 signaling as a key driver of immune evasion in pancreatic cancer: Therapeutic implications.

> **英文摘要：**
> Pancreatic ductal adenocarcinoma (PDAC) is a highly lethal malignancy characterized by a dense desmoplastic stroma, profound immune suppression, and resistance to conventional therapeutics. Poor patient outcomes are driven by resistance to chemotherapy and immunotherapy arising from both tumor-intrinsic and microenvironmental mechanisms. Elucidating the molecular pathways underlying therapeutic failure is therefore critical. Transforming growth factor-β (TGF-β) is a central regulator of PDAC progression, promoting epithelial-mesenchymal-transition (EMT), stromal remodeling, immune exclusion, and checkpoint activation at advanced disease stages. The transcription factor Yin Yang 1 (YY1) is a critical downstream integrator and amplifier of TGF-β-driven signaling programs. YY1 reinforces EMT, metabolic adaptation, and immune evasion through transcriptional, epigenetic, and post-transcriptional regulations. Several key immune modulators of immune evasion include PD-L1, indoleamine 2,3-dioxygenase, FOXP3, and pro-tumoral chemokines. The coordinated TGF-β-YY1 signaling suppresses CD8 cytotoxic T-cell (CTL) and natural killer (NK) cell functions, promotes regulatory T (Treg) cells and myeloid-derived suppressor cells (MDSCs), and establishes an immune-cold, therapy-resistant tumor microenvironment. This review explores the mechanistic basis of the TGF-β-YY1 cross-talk regulation in the immune evasion of PDAC. It also discusses emerging therapeutic opportunities in targeting the TGF-β-YY1 axis to overcome immune escape and improve treatment outcomes in PDAC.

> **中文摘要：**
> 胰腺导管腺癌 (PDAC) 是一种高度致命的恶性肿瘤，其特征是致密的促结缔组织增生间质、深刻的免疫抑制以及对常规疗法的耐药性。患者预后不良是由源于肿瘤内在和微环境机制的化疗和免疫疗法耐药性驱动的。因此，阐明导致治疗失败的分子通路至关重要。转化生长因子-β (TGF-β) 是 PDAC 进展的核心调节因子，在疾病晚期促进上皮-间质转化 (EMT)、间质重塑、免疫排除和检查点激活。转录因子阴阳 1 (YY1) 是 TGF-β 驱动信号通路的关键下游整合器和放大器。YY1 通过转录、表观遗传和转录后调节增强 EMT、代谢适应和免疫逃逸。免疫逃逸的几个关键免疫调节因子包括 PD-L1、吲哚胺 2,3-双加氧酶、FOXP3 和促肿瘤趋化因子。协调的 TGF-β-YY1 信号会抑制 CD8 细胞毒性 T 细胞 (CTL) 和自然杀伤 (NK) 细胞功能，促进调节性 T (Treg) 细胞和髓源性抑制细胞 (MDSCs)，并建立一种免疫冷色调、耐药的肿瘤微环境。本综述探讨了 TGF-β-YY1 交叉调节在 PDAC 免疫逃逸中的机制基础。它还讨论了靶向 TGF-β-YY1 轴以克服免疫逃逸并改善 PDAC 治疗效果的新兴治疗机会。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文系统性地阐述了 TGF-β-YY1 信号轴在胰腺导管腺癌（PDAC）免疫逃逸中的核心驱动作用，强调了 YY1 作为 TGF-β 下游关键整合者的分子机制。综述不仅涵盖了该通路对肿瘤间质重塑和代谢适应的影响，还详细解析了其如何通过调控多种免疫因子构建抑制性微环境。文章的创新性在于将复杂的分子交叉对话与临床治疗耐药紧密结合，为开发靶向该轴的免疫联合疗法提供了重要的理论支撑和潜在靶点。

---

## 391. 癌症中的 SCF-FBXO31 E3 泛素连接酶：分子机制见解与临床意义

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41554415)
**期刊：** Biochimica et biophysica acta. Reviews on cancer
**PMID：** 41554415
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.bbcan.2026.189534

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** SCF-FBXO31 E3 ubiquitin ligase in cancer: Molecular insights and clinical implications.

> **英文摘要：**
> F-box only protein 31 (FBXO31), a substrate adapter of SKP1-Cullin1-F-box (SCF) E3 ubiquitin ligase, was first identified as a candidate tumor suppressor in breast cancer due to its role in inducing senescence. Over the past two decades, FBXO31 has emerged as a crucial regulator in several human cancers, where it promotes the proteasomal degradation of various oncoproteins. FBXO31 plays a crucial role in regulating the cell cycle to maintain genomic integrity and inhibits processes such as epithelial-to-mesenchymal transition (EMT), invasion, and metastasis. This review examines the molecular mechanisms underlying the potent tumor-suppressive functions of FBXO31 in diverse human cancers. We also discuss the underlying causes of FBXO31 deregulation in cancer, providing insights into the intricate regulatory networks governing its expression. Additionally, we also examine the unexpected oncogenic functions of FBXO31 in certain cellular contexts. Finally, we highlight the clinical potential of FBXO31 in human malignancies, discussing its implications as both a biomarker and a therapeutic target. In conclusion, understanding the nuanced biology of FBXO31 is crucial for unravelling its role in tumorigenesis and advancing future therapeutic strategies.

> **中文摘要：**
> F-box 蛋白 31 (FBXO31) 是 SKP1-Cullin1-F-box (SCF) E3 泛素连接酶的一个底物适配体，最初由于其在诱导衰老中的作用，被确定为乳腺癌中的候选抑癌因子。在过去的二十年里，FBXO31 已成为几种人类癌症中的关键调节因子，它促进了多种致癌蛋白的蛋白酶体降解。FBXO31 在调节细胞周期以维持基因组完整性方面发挥着至关重要的作用，并能抑制上皮-间质转化 (EMT)、侵袭和转移等过程。本综述探讨了 FBXO31 在多种人类癌症中发挥强大抑癌功能的分子机制。我们还讨论了癌症中 FBXO31 失调的根本原因，为控制其表达的复杂调控网络提供了见解。此外，我们还研究了 FBXO31 在特定细胞背景下意想不到的致癌功能。最后，我们强调了 FBXO31 在人类恶性肿瘤中的临床潜力，讨论了其作为生物标志物和治疗靶点的意义。总之，深入了解 FBXO31 的细微生物学特性，对于揭示其在肿瘤发生中的作用并推进未来的治疗策略至关重要。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文全面系统地综述了 SCF-FBXO31 E3 泛素连接酶在癌症生物学中的双重角色，重点阐述了其作为抑癌因子在细胞周期调控和基因组稳定性维护中的核心机制。文章不仅深入剖析了 FBXO31 降解癌蛋白的分子路径，还前瞻性地讨论了其在特定环境下的致癌潜能及其表达失调的复杂调控网络。该综述整合了过去二十年的研究成果，明确了 FBXO31 作为临床生物标志物和潜在治疗靶点的巨大价值，为泛素化靶向药物的研发提供了重要的理论支撑。

## 392. 靶向前列腺癌中的糖酵解：分子机制与治疗进展

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41548699)
**期刊：** Biochimica et biophysica acta. Reviews on cancer
**PMID：** 41548699
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.bbcan.2026.189537

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Targeting glycolysis in prostate cancer: Molecular mechanisms and therapeutic advances.

> **英文摘要：**
> Prostate cancer (PCa) is the second most common cancer among men worldwide and poses a significant threat to male health. A key feature of tumor progression is metabolic reprogramming, which involves the abnormal activation of glycolysis. This metabolic process supports PCa proliferation, metastasis, and drug resistance through rapid energy production, the provision of biosynthetic precursors, and the remodeling of the tumor microenvironment (TME). Key enzymes such as hexokinase 2 (HK2), phosphofructokinase (PFK), pyruvate kinase M2 (PKM2), glucose transporters (GLUTs), and lactate dehydrogenase A (LDHA) play pivotal roles in regulating aerobic glycolysis in PCa cells. Glycolytic enzymes are modulated by a variety of mechanisms, including the PI3K/AKT and AMPK signaling pathways, hypoxia-inducible factor 1α (HIF-1α), c-Myc, and non-coding RNAs. Current therapeutic strategies targeting glycolysis include natural products and small-molecule inhibitors. Targeting glycolysis presents novel opportunities to address existing limitations in PCa management. This review discusses the advances, challenges, and future research directions in glycolysis-focused PCa studies, providing a theoretical foundation for the development of precise metabolic interventions.

> **中文摘要：**
> 前列腺癌（PCa）是全球男性中第二常见的癌症，对男性健康构成了重大威胁。肿瘤进展的一个关键特征是代谢重塑，其中包括糖酵解的异常激活。这一代谢过程通过快速产生能量、提供生物合成前体以及重塑肿瘤微环境（TME），支持前列腺癌的增殖、转移和耐药。己糖激酶 2（HK2）、磷酸果糖激酶（PFK）、丙酮酸激酶 M2（PKM2）、葡萄糖转运蛋白（GLUTs）和乳酸脱氢酶 A（LDHA）等关键酶在前列腺癌细胞有氧糖酵解的调节中发挥着枢纽作用。糖酵解酶受多种机制调节，包括 PI3K/AKT 和 AMPK 信号通路、缺氧诱导因子 1α（HIF-1α）、c-Myc 以及非编码 RNA。目前靶向糖酵解的治疗策略包括天然产物和小分子抑制剂。靶向糖酵解为解决前列腺癌管理中现有的局限性提供了新的机遇。本综述讨论了以糖酵解为中心的前列腺癌研究进展、挑战和未来研究方向，为开发精准代谢干预措施提供了理论基础。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该综述系统地阐述了糖酵解在前列腺癌代谢重塑中的核心驱动作用，深入分析了关键限速酶及其上游复杂的分子调节网络。文章不仅揭示了糖酵解如何介导肿瘤的恶性进展与耐药，还前瞻性地总结了天然产物及小分子抑制剂的治疗潜力。该综述逻辑严密，为克服前列腺癌常规疗法的瓶颈提供了精准代谢干预的新视角，具有极高的学术价值和临床转化参考意义。

---

## 393. 肿瘤微环境中的GDF15：癌症免疫代谢和治疗耐药性的核心调节因子

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41546893)
**期刊：** Cytokine & growth factor reviews
**PMID：** 41546893
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.cytogfr.2026.01.004

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** GDF15 in the tumor microenvironment: A central mediator of cancer immunometabolism and therapeutic resistance.

> **英文摘要：**
> Growth differentiation factor 15 (GDF15), a divergent member of the transforming growth factor-β (TGFβ) superfamily, has emerged as a pivotal cytokine linking cancer metabolism, immune suppression, and systemic energy balance. Initially characterized as a stress-induced cytokine with roles in appetite regulation and cachexia, GDF15 was first identified in activated macrophages and is also secreted by tumor cells, stromal cells and stressed epithelial cells across multiple tissues. Functionally, GDF15 exerts pleiotropic effects on both immune and nonimmune cell populations, modulating T cells, dendritic cells, and macrophages in the tumor microenvironment (TME), and metabolic tissues such as liver, adipose and muscle, thereby promoting tumor progression, therapeutic resistance, and cancer-associated metabolic dysregulation. In several human cancers of such as colorectal, pancreatic, breast and brain, elevated GDF15 levels correlate with poor prognosis, immune evasion, and chemoresistance. Mechanistically, GDF15 modulates fatty acid metabolism, promotes epithelial-mesenchymal transition, and suppresses anti-tumor immunity by impairing dendritic cell maturation and excluding CD8 T cell infiltration. Targeting GDF15 may reprogram immunometabolic suppression and enhance checkpoint blockade efficacy. This review synthesizes current knowledge on GDF15's multifaceted roles in tumor biology, emphasizing its function as a central node of cancer immunometabolism. We highlight advances in spatial multi-omics, integrating transcriptomics and immune imaging, that reveal GDF15 spatially restricted immunosuppression in the tumor microenvironment.

> **中文摘要：**
> 生长分化因子15（GDF15）是转化生长因子-β（TGFβ）超家族的一个差异化成员，已成为连接癌症代谢、免疫抑制和全身能量平衡的关键细胞因子。GDF15最初被描述为一种与食欲调节和恶病质有关的应激诱导细胞因子，最初在活化的巨噬细胞中被发现，也由肿瘤细胞、间质细胞和多种组织中受压的上皮细胞分泌。在功能上，GDF15对免疫和非免疫细胞群发挥多重作用，调节肿瘤微环境（TME）中的T细胞、树突状细胞和巨噬细胞，以及肝脏、脂肪和肌肉等代谢组织，从而促进肿瘤进展、治疗耐药和癌症相关的代谢失调。在结直肠癌、胰腺癌、乳腺癌和脑癌等多种人类癌症中，GDF15水平升高与预后不良、免疫逃逸和化疗耐药相关。从机制上讲，GDF15调节脂肪酸代谢，促进上皮-间质转化，并通过损害树突状细胞成熟和排除CD8 T细胞浸润来抑制抗肿瘤免疫。靶向GDF15可能会重新编程免疫代谢抑制并增强免疫检查点阻断的疗效。本综述综合了关于GDF15在肿瘤生物学中多面作用的现有知识，强调了其作为癌症免疫代谢核心节点的功能。我们重点介绍了空间多组学的进展，整合了转录组学和免疫成像，揭示了GDF15在肿瘤微环境中空间受限的免疫抑制。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文深入探讨了GDF15作为连接癌症代谢与免疫逃逸的核心分子机制，揭示了其在调节肿瘤微环境及全身能量平衡中的多重角色。文章系统总结了GDF15通过影响脂肪酸代谢和免疫细胞浸润介导治疗耐药的路径，具有极高的学术价值。通过整合空间多组学数据，该综述为靶向GDF15以克服免疫治疗耐药提供了前瞻性的理论依据和潜在的治疗策略。

---

## 394. 胰腺导管腺癌中的蛋白质棕榈酰化与免疫调节：整合跨癌症研究的见解

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41544825)
**期刊：** Biochimica et biophysica acta. Reviews on cancer
**PMID：** 41544825
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.bbcan.2026.189532

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Protein palmitoylation and immune regulation in pancreatic ductal adenocarcinoma: Integrating insights from cross-cancer studies.

> **英文摘要：**
> Pancreatic ductal adenocarcinoma (PDAC) is characterized by an immunologically "cold" tumor microenvironment (TME), marked by a dense stromal barrier, impaired antigen presentation, and extensive infiltration of immunosuppressive cells. In recent years, protein S-palmitoylation, a reversible lipid modification, has emerged as a critical mechanism regulating immune signaling, receptor trafficking, and membrane localization of immune-related proteins. This review highlights the multifaceted roles of S-palmitoylation in shaping the immunological landscape of PDAC. We systematically discuss its involvement in immune checkpoint regulation, T-cell activation, antigen presentation, and the function of myeloid-derived suppressor cells (MDSCs), integrating evidence from both PDAC and other cancer types. Special attention is given to key palmitoylated molecules, including programmed death-ligand 1 (PD-L1), cluster of differentiation 80 (CD80), lymphocyte-specific protein tyrosine kinase (LCK), linker for activation of T cells (LAT), interferon-induced transmembrane proteins (IFITMs), and major histocompatibility complex class I (MHC-I), and their potential roles in the immunosuppressive network of PDAC. Moreover, we explore therapeutic strategies targeting palmitoylation, such as the use of selective palmitoyltransferase inhibitors, the design of palmitoylation-deficient CAR-T cells, and the development of nanotechnology-based delivery platforms. By incorporating cross-cancer insights, we propose that palmitoylation is a promising regulatory axis for reprogramming the PDAC immune microenvironment and overcoming resistance to immunotherapy.

> **中文摘要：**
> 胰腺导管腺癌 (PDAC) 的特征是免疫“冷”肿瘤微环境 (TME)，其标志是致密的间质屏障、受损的抗原呈递以及广泛的免疫抑制细胞浸润。近年来，蛋白质 S-棕榈酰化（一种可逆的脂质修饰）已成为调节免疫信号传导、受体运输和免疫相关蛋白膜定位的关键机制。本综述强调了 S-棕榈酰化在塑造 PDAC 免疫景观中的多重作用。我们系统地讨论了其在免疫检查点调节、T 细胞激活、抗原呈递以及髓源性抑制细胞 (MDSCs) 功能中的参与，并整合了来自 PDAC 和其他癌症类型的证据。特别关注了关键的棕榈酰化分子，包括程序性死亡配体 1 (PD-L1)、分化簇 80 (CD80)、淋巴细胞特异性蛋白酪氨酸激酶 (LCK)、T 细胞激活接头蛋白 (LAT)、干扰素诱导跨膜蛋白 (IFITMs) 和主要组织相容性复合体 I 类 (MHC-I)，以及它们在 PDAC 免疫抑制网络中的潜在作用。此外，我们探讨了针对棕榈酰化的治疗策略，例如选择性棕榈酰转移酶抑制剂的使用、棕榈酰化缺陷型 CAR-T 细胞的设计以及基于纳米技术的递送平台的开发。通过整合跨癌症的见解，我们提出棕榈酰化是一个有前景的调节轴，可用于重编程 PDAC 免疫微环境并克服对免疫疗法的耐药性。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本综述深入探讨了蛋白质棕榈酰化这一关键转译后修饰在调节胰腺导管腺癌（PDAC）免疫微环境中的多重角色，系统分析了其对 PD-L1、MHC-I 等核心免疫分子的空间定位和功能调控。文章通过整合跨癌种的研究证据，揭示了棕榈酰化如何参与塑造 PDAC 特有的免疫抑制景观，并前瞻性地提出了靶向棕榈酰转移酶和工程化 CAR-T 细胞等创新疗法。该研究为转化 PDAC 免疫“冷”表型提供了全新的分子靶点和理论依据，具有极高的学术前瞻性和临床指导价值。

---

## 395. 回复：仑伐替尼联合依维莫司对比卡博替尼治疗 PD-1 免疫检查点抑制剂进展后的转移性透明细胞肾细胞癌的多中心随机 II 期临床试验（LenCabo）。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41539910)
**期刊：** European urology
**PMID：** 41539910
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.eururo.2025.11.020

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Re: A Multicenter Randomized Phase II Trial of Lenvatinib plus Everolimus Versus Cabozantinib in Patients with Metastatic Clear Cell RCC that Progressed on PD-1 Immune Checkpoint Inhibition (LenCabo).

> **英文摘要：**
> No abstract available.

> **中文摘要：**
> 暂无摘要。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该文献是对 LenCabo 研究的评述或讨论。LenCabo 试验聚焦于 PD-1 抑制剂耐药后的转移性透明细胞肾癌（mccRCC）患者，对比了仑伐替尼联合依维莫司与卡博替尼这两种临床常用方案的疗效。尽管本文为评论性质且无摘要，但其针对的研究课题是当前晚期肾癌二线治疗中的核心痛点，即免疫治疗进展后的最佳序贯方案选择。在《European Urology》这一顶级期刊上的持续讨论，进一步凸显了该临床试验结论在泌尿肿瘤学界的关注度与学术价值。

## 396. 验证预测肉瘤患者 PD-1 抑制剂免疫治疗疗效的七基因特征

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41537707)
**期刊：** Clinical cancer research : an official journal of the American Association for Cancer Research
**PMID：** 41537707
**DOI：** 10.1158/1078-0432.CCR-25-2580

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Validation of a Seven-Gene Predictive SIGNature for the Efficacy of Immuno-Oncology PD-1 Inhibitors in Patients with Sarcoma.

> **英文摘要：**
> PURPOSE: Immune checkpoint inhibitors (ICI) have transformed cancer therapy, but their efficacy in sarcomas remains limited. A seven-gene predictive signature (CD86, CHI3L1, CXCL10, CXCL9, LAG3, NR4A1, and VCAM1) was previously identified as a biomarker for response to combined antiangiogenic and PD-1 inhibitor therapy in soft-tissue sarcomas. This study aimed to externally validate the predictive utility of this signature [SIGNature for immuno-oncology PD-1 inhibitors in sarcoma (SIGNIOS)] in an independent cohort of patients with sarcoma treated with ICIs.
> 
> EXPERIMENTAL DESIGN: Using RNA sequencing data from pretreatment tumor samples from the SARC028 phase II trial (pembrolizumab for advanced sarcomas) and the GEIS-32 phase II trial (pazopanib in advanced solitary fibrous tumor), we calculated the SIGNIOS score. Patients were stratified into low (score 0-4) and high (score 5-7) risk groups.
> 
> RESULTS: The SARC028 validation cohort comprised 31 patients, with a median age of 33 years, and 45.2% were female. The most common histologic subtypes included osteosarcoma (25.8%) and Ewing sarcoma (19.4%). The seven-gene signature significantly stratified patients into groups with significantly different progression-free survival (PFS): Those with scores of 0 to 4 had a median PFS of 49 days, whereas those with scores of 5 to 7 had a median PFS of 170 days [HR = 0.71 (95% confidence interval, 0.55-0.91), P = 0.007].
> 
> CONCLUSIONS: This external validation confirms the seven-gene signature as a potential biomarker for predicting ICI efficacy in advanced sarcomas. Prospective studies are needed to determine the prognostic versus predictive value of SIGNIOS, refine its use across sarcoma subtypes, and explore its applicability in other tumor types.

> **中文摘要：**
> 目的：免疫检查点抑制剂（ICI）改变了癌症治疗，但在肉瘤中的疗效仍有限。此前，一项包含七个基因（CD86、CHI3L1、CXCL10、CXCL9、LAG3、NR4A1 和 VCAM1）的预测性特征被确定为软组织肉瘤对抗血管生成联合 PD-1 抑制剂治疗反应的生物标志物。本研究旨在独立验证队列中，针对接受 ICI 治疗的肉瘤患者，外部验证该特征 [肉瘤免疫肿瘤学 PD-1 抑制剂特征 (SIGNIOS)] 的预测效用。实验设计：利用来自 SARC028 II 期临床试验（帕博利珠单抗治疗晚期肉瘤）和 GEIS-32 II 期临床试验（帕唑帕尼治疗晚期孤立性纤维性肿瘤）的治疗前肿瘤样本 RNA 测序数据，我们计算了 SIGNIOS 评分。患者被分为低风险组（评分 0-4）和高风险组（评分 5-7）。结果：SARC028 验证队列包含 31 名患者，中位年龄为 33 岁，45.2% 为女性。最常见的组织学亚型包括骨肉瘤（25.8%）和尤文肉瘤（19.4%）。该七基因特征显著地将患者分为无进展生存期（PFS）差异显著的组别：评分 0 至 4 分者的中位 PFS 为 49 天，而评分 5 至 7 分者的中位 PFS 为 170 天 [HR = 0.71 (95% 置信区间, 0.55-0.91), P = 0.007]。结论：该外部验证确认了七基因特征作为预测晚期肉瘤 ICI 疗效的潜在生物标志物的地位。仍需前瞻性研究来确定 SIGNIOS 的预后与预测价值，完善其在肉瘤亚型中的应用，并探索其在其他肿瘤类型中的适用性。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究通过对 SARC028 等临床试验数据的外部验证，成功证实了 SIGNIOS（七基因特征）在预测晚期肉瘤患者 PD-1 抑制剂疗效中的重要价值。该特征能显著区分出不同无进展生存获益的患者群体，为肉瘤免疫治疗的精准患者筛选提供了有力支持。尽管验证队列样本量有限且肉瘤亚型具有异质性，但研究结果对于优化肉瘤个体化治疗方案具有重要的临床参考价值，未来需进一步通过大规模前瞻性研究以完善其在特定亚型中的应用。

---

## 397. 探索针对三阴性乳腺癌的细胞外基质靶向放射性药物的 89Zr/177Lu 诊疗配对

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41537706)
**期刊：** Clinical cancer research : an official journal of the American Association for Cancer Research
**PMID：** 41537706
**DOI：** 10.1158/1078-0432.CCR-25-3354

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Exploring the 89Zr/177Lu Theranostic Pairing with an Extracellular Matrix-Targeted Radiopharmaceutical against Triple-Negative Breast Cancer.

> **英文摘要：**
> PURPOSE: Triple-negative breast cancer (TNBC) is highly aggressive and heterogeneous, with high rates of disease recurrence and poor treatment outcomes. The extra domain A of fibronectin is an extracellular matrix protein with high abundance in TNBC stroma and limited expression in healthy human tissues. Theranostic approaches have demonstrated improved patient outcomes by using identical targeting vectors for patient stratification through targeted positron emission tomography imaging and radioligand therapy; however, no radiopharmaceuticals are currently approved for TNBC. EXPERIMENTAL DESIGN: [89Zr]Zr-DFO-F8 (89Zr-F8) and [177Lu]Lu-CHX-A''-DTPA-F8 (177Lu-F8) were synthesized and characterized in vitro and in vivo for comparability in binding and biodistribution. Dosimetry estimation identified optimal dosing parameters for therapeutic benefit with limited off-target toxicities. 177Lu-F8 was assessed as a therapeutic against two TNBC xenograft mouse models. Weekly health and hematologic assessments with terminal serum chemistry and histopathology analysis were performed to evaluate toxicities. RESULTS: 89Zr-F8 and 177Lu-F8 exhibited similar in vitro characteristics and similar tumor accumulation in two different xenografted mouse models of TNBC. 177Lu-F8 treatment significantly prolonged survival in both mouse models, with only transient myelosuppression and off-target myelotoxicity in Rag2-/- mice receiving the highest dose of the radiolabeled F8 antibody, as determined by blood measurements and terminal histopathology. CONCLUSIONS: The zirconium-89/lutetium-177 theranostic nuclide coupling with the F8 delivery vector successfully identified TNBC xenografts and significantly extended the survival of xenografted mice.

> **中文摘要：**
> 目的：三阴性乳腺癌 (TNBC) 具有高度侵袭性和异质性，复发率高且治疗结果较差。纤维连接蛋白的额外结构域 A (EDA) 是一种在 TNBC 基质中高丰度表达但在健康人体组织中表达有限的细胞外基质蛋白。诊疗一体化方法通过使用相同的靶向载体进行靶向正电子发射断层扫描 (PET) 成像以实现患者分层，并结合放射性配体治疗，已证明可改善患者预后；然而，目前尚无获批用于 TNBC 的放射性药物。实验设计：合成了 [89Zr]Zr-DFO-F8 (89Zr-F8) 和 [177Lu]Lu-CHX-A''-DTPA-F8 (177Lu-F8)，并在体内外对其结合力和生物分布的可比性进行了表征。剂量学评估确定了在限制脱靶毒性的同时获得治疗益处的最佳给药参数。在两种 TNBC 异种移植小鼠模型中评估了 177Lu-F8 的治疗效果。通过每周的健康和血液学评估，以及终末血清生化和组织病理学分析来评估毒性。结果：89Zr-F8 和 177Lu-F8 在两种不同的 TNBC 异种移植小鼠模型中表现出相似的体外特性和肿瘤蓄积。177Lu-F8 治疗显著延长了两种小鼠模型的生存期；根据血液测量和终末组织病理学结果，仅在接受最高剂量放射性标记 F8 抗体的 Rag2-/- 小鼠中观察到短暂的骨髓抑制和脱靶骨髓毒性。结论：锆-89/镥-177 诊疗核素对与 F8 递送载体的结合成功识别了 TNBC 异种移植物，并显著延长了异种移植小鼠的生存期。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该研究针对临床治疗极具挑战性的三阴性乳腺癌（TNBC），成功开发了基于 F8 抗体靶向细胞外基质 EDA-FN 的 89Zr/177Lu 诊疗一体化方案。通过 PET 成像实现精准病灶识别与放射性配体疗法的无缝衔接，实验证实该配对体系在多种模型中具有高度的生物分布一致性和显著的生存获益，且毒副作用可控。该成果填补了 TNBC 领域缺乏有效放射性药物的空白，验证了基质靶向诊疗策略在难治性实体瘤中的巨大潜力。

---

## 398. COLUMBUS研究中针对BRAF V600E/K突变晚期或转移性黑色素瘤的生物标志物与治疗预后的探索性分析。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41537702)
**期刊：** Clinical cancer research : an official journal of the American Association for Cancer Research
**PMID：** 41537702
**DOI：** 10.1158/1078-0432.CCR-25-3262

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Exploratory Analysis of Biomarkers and Treatment Outcomes from the COLUMBUS Study in BRAF V600E/K-Mutant Advanced or Metastatic Melanoma.

> **英文摘要：**
> PURPOSE: Treatment with encorafenib ± binimetinib is associated with improved survival versus vemurafenib in patients with BRAF V600E/K-mutant advanced melanoma. We retrospectively analyzed genomic and transcriptomic data from the phase III COLUMBUS trial to identify molecular correlates of benefit with encorafenib ± binimetinib. EXPERIMENTAL DESIGN: In COLUMBUS, patients with BRAF V600E/K-mutant locally advanced, unresectable, or metastatic melanoma (n = 921) were randomized to receive encorafenib plus binimetinib, encorafenib, or vemurafenib. We used whole-exome sequencing (n = 666), whole-transcriptome sequencing (RNA sequencing; n = 514), and assessment of circulating tumor DNA (ctDNA) at baseline (n = 336) and on treatment (cycle 2 day 1, n = 184) to evaluate biomarker associations with progression-free and overall survival. RESULTS: Survival benefits with encorafenib plus binimetinib versus vemurafenib were greatest in patients with higher tumor mutational burden (TMB) and those with evidence of tumor immune infiltration (i.e., higher cytolytic score, PD-L1 expression, or IFNγ gene signature scores). Clustering of gene expression profiles identified three tumor subgroups, including an "immune" subgroup associated with improved survival. Detection of BRAF V600 alterations in baseline ctDNA was associated with shorter survival; clearance of BRAF V600 alterations at cycle 2 day 1 was associated with improved survival across arms. CONCLUSIONS: The greatest benefits of encorafenib plus binimetinib were observed in patients with evidence of high TMB and/or tumor-immune infiltration, suggesting potential immune contributions to efficacy, which were not observed with vemurafenib. BRAF V600 detectability in ctDNA seems to have utility as a marker of prognosis and response in this population.

> **中文摘要：**
> 目的：在BRAF V600E/K突变的晚期黑色素瘤患者中，与威罗非尼相比，恩考非尼±比尼美替尼治疗与生存期改善相关。我们回顾性分析了III期COLUMBUS试验的基因组和转录组数据，旨在识别与恩考非尼±比尼美替尼获益相关的分子相关因子。
> 实验设计：在COLUMBUS研究中，BRAF V600E/K突变的局部晚期、不可切除或转移性黑色素瘤患者（n = 921）被随机分配接受恩考非尼联合比尼美替尼、恩考非尼单药或威罗非尼治疗。我们利用全外显子组测序（n = 666）、全转录组测序（RNA测序；n = 514）以及基线（n = 336）和治疗中（第2周期第1天，n = 184）的循环肿瘤DNA（ctDNA）评估，来评价生物标志物与无进展生存期及总生存期的相关性。
> 结果：在肿瘤突变负荷（TMB）较高以及具有肿瘤免疫浸润证据（即较高的细胞毒性评分、PD-L1表达或IFNγ基因特征评分）的患者中，恩考非尼联合比尼美替尼对比威罗非尼的生存获益最为显著。基因表达谱聚类识别出三个肿瘤亚群，包括一个与生存改善相关的“免疫”亚群。基线ctDNA中检测到BRAF V600改变与生存期较短相关；在第2周期第1天清除BRAF V600改变与各组的生存期改善均相关。
> 结论：在具有高TMB和/或肿瘤免疫浸润证据的患者中，观察到恩考非尼联合比尼美替尼的最大获益，这表明免疫因素可能对疗效有所贡献，而这在威罗非尼中未被观察到。ctDNA中BRAF V600的可检测性似乎在该人群中具有作为预后和疗效评价指标的效用。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究通过对III期COLUMBUS临床试验的多组学数据进行深度回顾性分析，系统性地揭示了双靶向治疗（BRAF/MEK抑制剂）在黑色素瘤中的关键疗效预测因子。研究亮点在于结合了全外显子组、转录组及动态ctDNA检测，明确了高TMB、活跃的肿瘤免疫微环境以及ctDNA早期清除与优异预后的显著相关性。这些发现为临床决策提供了分子层面的精准分层依据，强调了免疫浸润在非免疫疗法中的潜在贡献，同时也证实了ctDNA作为非侵入性监测工具的可靠性。

---

## 399. ctDNA用于接受奥拉帕利治疗的转移性子宫内膜癌患者的预后评估和监测：GINECO-UTOLA试验的验证

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41537701)
**期刊：** Clinical cancer research : an official journal of the American Association for Cancer Research
**PMID：** 41537701
**DOI：** 10.1158/1078-0432.CCR-25-2959

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** ctDNA for Prognostication and Monitoring in Patients with Metastatic Endometrial Carcinoma Treated with Olaparib: Validation in the GINECO-UTOLA Trial.

> **英文摘要：**
> PURPOSE: ctDNA may offer a noninvasive means to evaluate tumor response and anticipate disease dynamics before radiologic changes in advanced endometrial carcinoma.
> 
> EXPERIMENTAL DESIGN: This ancillary analysis included patients from the multicenter, randomized, phase II GINECO-UTerin OLAparib (UTOLA) trial (NCT03745950) evaluating olaparib/placebo as maintenance after first-line platinum-based chemotherapy. Plasma samples were collected at screening after chemotherapy (baseline), 3 months (M3), and progression. ctDNA detection was assessed by a validated methylation-based Droplet Digital PCR (MethddPCR) assay targeting DNA positions universally methylated in endometrial carcinoma.
> 
> RESULTS: Among 130 evaluable patients, ctDNA was detected in 25 of 129 (19%, 1 technical fail) at baseline, 15 of 80 (19%) at M3, and 33 of 52 (63%) at progression. Baseline ctDNA positivity was independently associated with poorer progression-free survival (PFS) [median 1.81 vs. 7.39 months; adjusted HR = 5.33 (3.17-8.97)] and overall survival (OS) [10.3 vs. 24.7 months; adjusted HR = 3.98 (2.28-6.91); adjusted for age, stage IV at diagnosis, p53abn subgroup, and residual measurable lesions after chemotherapy]. Patients with baseline ctDNA had median OS of 9.36 months under olaparib versus 19.6 months under placebo (log-rank P = 0.05). Patients with increasing ctDNA at M3 had median PFS of 1.67 months, versus 9.64 months without, and median OS of 18.8 versus 25.8 months. ctDNA rising was predictive of poor postprogression OS under olaparib but not under placebo (interaction test, P < 0.001).
> 
> CONCLUSIONS: MethddPCR-ctDNA is an independent prognostic biomarker for OS in advanced/metastatic endometrial carcinoma. MethddPCR-ctDNA may identify patients unlikely to benefit from PARP inhibition, guide therapeutic decisions, and should be further evaluated as a new stratification parameter in future endometrial carcinoma trials.

> **中文摘要：**
> 目的：循环肿瘤DNA（ctDNA）可能为晚期子宫内膜癌在放射学变化发生前评估肿瘤反应和预测疾病动态提供一种无创手段。
> 
> 实验设计：本项辅助分析纳入了来自多中心、随机、II期GINECO-UTerin OLAparib (UTOLA) 临床试验（NCT03745950）的患者，该试验旨在评估一线含铂化疗后使用奥拉帕利或安慰剂进行维持治疗的疗效。在化疗后的筛选期（基线）、3个月（M3）以及疾病进展时收集血浆样本。通过一种经过验证的甲基化微滴数字PCR（MethddPCR）方法检测ctDNA，该方法针对子宫内膜癌中普遍存在的DNA甲基化位点。
> 
> 结果：在130名可评估的患者中，基线时ctDNA检出率为19%（129人中检出25人，1例技术失败），M3时为19%（80人中检出15人），进展时为63%（52人中检出33人）。基线ctDNA阳性与较差的无进展生存期（PFS）[中位1.81个月 vs 7.39个月；校正后风险比（HR）= 5.33 (3.17-8.97)]和总生存期（OS）[10.3个月 vs 24.7个月；校正后HR = 3.98 (2.28-6.91)]独立相关（校正因素包括年龄、诊断时IV期、p53异常亚组以及化疗后残留的可测量病灶）。基线ctDNA阳性患者在奥拉帕利组的中位OS为9.36个月，而安慰剂组为19.6个月（对数秩检验 P = 0.05）。M3时ctDNA水平上升的患者中位PFS为1.67个月，而未上升者为9.64个月，中位OS分别为18.8个月和25.8个月。在奥拉帕利组中，ctDNA上升可预示较差的进展后OS，但在安慰剂组中则不然（交互作用检验，P < 0.001）。
> 
> 结论：MethddPCR-ctDNA是晚期/转移性子宫内膜癌总生存期的独立预后生物标志物。MethddPCR-ctDNA可能识别出不太可能从PARP抑制剂治疗中获益的患者，从而指导临床治疗决策，并应在未来的子宫内膜癌试验中作为一种新的分层参数进行进一步评估。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究利用GINECO-UTOLA随机对照试验的数据，验证了基于甲基化的ctDNA检测在转移性子宫内膜癌中的临床价值。研究关键性地发现，基线ctDNA状态及治疗早期的动态变化不仅是强有力的独立预后因子，且能识别对奥拉帕利维持治疗获益有限的亚群。该研究的创新点在于采用普适性的甲基化标志物而非个体化突变追踪，提升了临床应用的便捷性，为子宫内膜癌精准医疗提供了可靠的分子分层工具。

---

## 400. 机器学习揭示全球癌症结局的国别特定驱动因素

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41535168)
**期刊：** Annals of oncology : official journal of the European Society for Medical Oncology
**PMID：** 41535168
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.annonc.2025.11.014

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Machine learning reveals country-specific drivers of global cancer outcomes.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND: Global inequities in access to cancer diagnostics and treatment contribute to wide variation in cancer mortality-to-incidence ratios (MIRs), a proxy for survival. We aimed to develop an interpretable machine learning framework to quantify country-specific health system contributors to MIR and inform policy prioritization. MATERIALS AND METHODS: We assembled national MIRs from GLOBOCAN 2022 for 185 countries and health system indicators from multilateral sources, including gross domestic product (GDP) per capita, universal health coverage (UHC) index, radiotherapy centers per population, health spending (%GDP), out-of-pocket expenditure, work force densities (physicians; nurses/midwives; surgical work force), pathology availability, Human Development Index, and gender inequality index. A CatBoost gradient-boosting model was trained with repeated leave-one-country-out cross-validation (10 repeats; 1850 predictions). Nested hyperparameter optimization and strict leakage control were used. Model interpretability employed SHapley Additive exPlanations (SHAP; TreeExplainer) to generate global and country-level feature attributions. SHAP values, model-derived metrics quantifying each factor's contribution to cancer outcomes, were generated. Performance metrics included R, root mean squared error (RMSE), mean absolute error, and Pearson correlation; uncertainty was estimated by bootstrap resampling. RESULTS: The model showed strong out-of-sample performance [R = 0.852, 95% confidence interval (CI) 0.801-0.891; RMSE 0.057, 95% CI 0.050-0.064]; correlation between predicted and observed MIRs was r = 0.923 (P = 8.30 × 10). Global SHAP contributions ranked GDP per capita (22.5%), radiotherapy centers per population (15.4%), and UHC index (12.9%) as the leading determinants. Country-specific SHAP profiles revealed substantial heterogeneity in dominant drivers across settings, enabling tailored policy levers (e.g. infrastructure, coverage expansion, or financial protection). An accompanying web interface provides country-level SHAP summaries for decision support. CONCLUSIONS: An explainable machine learning approach accurately predicts national MIRs and decomposes predictions into country-specific health system attributions. While ecological and noncausal by design, the SHAP profiles translate population-level associations into actionable hypotheses for prioritizing investments-highlighting, across many contexts, radiotherapy capacity and UHC expansion as recurrent levers, and underscoring that higher total health spending alone may be insufficient without strategic allocation. Prospective, country-specific evaluations are warranted to test whether targeting model-identified drivers improve cancer outcomes.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景：全球在获取癌症诊断和治疗方面的不平等导致了癌症死亡率与发病率比（MIR）的巨大差异，而MIR是生存率的替代指标。我们旨在开发一种可解释的机器学习框架，以量化国别特定的医疗系统因素对MIR的贡献，并为政策优先级提供依据。
> 材料与方法：我们收集了来自GLOBOCAN 2022的185个国家的国家MIR，以及来自多边来源的医疗系统指标，包括人均国内生产总值（GDP）、全民健康覆盖（UHC）指数、每人口放射治疗中心数、卫生支出（占GDP的百分比）、个人自付支出、劳动力密度（医生、护士/助产士、外科劳动力）、病理可及性、人类发展指数和性别不平等指数。使用重复留一国家交叉验证（10次重复；1850次预测）训练了CatBoost梯度提升模型。采用了嵌套超参数优化和严格的泄露控制。模型可解释性采用SHapley Additive exPlanations（SHAP; TreeExplainer）来生成全球和国家层面的特征归因。生成了SHAP值，即量化各因素对癌症结局贡献的模型衍生指标。性能指标包括R、均方根误差（RMSE）、平均绝对误差和Pearson相关性；通过自助重采样法估算了不确定性。
> 结果：模型表现出强大的样本外性能[R = 0.852, 95% 置信区间 (CI) 0.801-0.891; RMSE 0.057, 95% CI 0.050-0.064]；预测MIR与观察到的MIR之间的相关性为r = 0.923 (P = 8.30 × 10)。全球SHAP贡献排名显示，人均GDP（22.5%）、每人口放射治疗中心数（15.4%）和UHC指数（12.9%）是主要的决定因素。国别特定的SHAP概况揭示了不同背景下主导驱动因素的显著异质性，从而支持定制化的政策杠杆（例如基础设施建设、覆盖范围扩大或财务保护）。配套的网络界面为决策支持提供了国家层面的SHAP总结。
> 结论：一种可解释的机器学习方法能够准确预测国家MIR，并将预测分解为国别特定的医疗系统归因。尽管该设计属于生态学且非因果性，但SHAP概况将人群层面的关联转化为优先投资的可行假设——在许多背景下，放射治疗能力和UHC扩张被强调为经常性的政策杠杆，并强调如果缺乏战略配置，仅靠提高总卫生支出可能不足。有必要进行前瞻性的、针对特定国家的评估，以测试针对模型识别的驱动因素是否能改善癌症结局。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究通过整合GLOBOCAN 2022全球癌症数据与多维医疗卫生指标，成功构建了基于CatBoost算法的高精度预测模型，深入解析了影响各国癌症死亡率与发病率比（MIR）的关键因素。研究的创新之处在于引入了SHAP可解释性框架，将复杂的全局关联转化为可行动的国别特定政策建议，强调了放射治疗能力和全民健康覆盖（UHC）在改善癌症预后中的核心地位。尽管作为生态学研究存在非因果性的局限，但其为全球卫生管理提供了一个强大的决策支持平台，明确了单纯增加财政投入若无战略性分配将难以优化健康结局，具有显著的公共卫生政策指导价值。

---

## 401. 肥胖相关银屑病中代谢-表皮界面的免疫重编程

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41534195)
**期刊：** Cytokine & growth factor reviews
**PMID：** 41534195
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.cytogfr.2026.01.003

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Reprogramming immunity at the metabolic-epidermal interface in obesity-associated psoriasis.

> **英文摘要：**
> Obesity and psoriasis are chronic inflammatory disorders, now recognized to be interconnected, in which metabolic overload drives immune dysregulation and therapeutic resistance. Excess adiposity converts adipose tissue into an inflammatory organ that releases adipokines and cytokine-like mediators, reprogramming keratinocytes and immune cells to sustain cytokine-driven inflammatory circuits in the skin. Excess nutrients and lipotoxic stress impair mitochondrial function, enhance glycolysis, and induce epigenetic remodeling in myeloid and epithelial lineages, generating metabolic memory that perpetuates inflammation. Increased body mass index and insulin resistance are clinically associated with reduced responses to biologics targeting tumor necrosis factor, interleukin (IL)-17, and IL-23, whereas metabolic interventions including caloric restriction and glucagon-like peptide-1 receptor agonists improve responsiveness. Recent multi-omics, single-cell, and spatial studies demonstrate that obesity reshapes dermal and adipose immune niches and rewires epidermal innate immunity, attenuating cytokine blockade. Obesity-associated psoriasis thus represents a metabolically imprinted inflammatory state driven by chronic metabolic stress. This review integrates mechanistic and clinical insights and discusses strategies to restore metabolic-immune plasticity to sustain disease remission.

> **中文摘要：**
> 肥胖和银屑病是慢性炎症性疾病，目前被认为相互关联，其中代谢负荷过重驱动了免疫失调和治疗抵抗。过量的脂肪堆积使脂肪组织转化为炎症器官，释放脂肪因子和类细胞因子介质，重编程角质形成细胞和免疫细胞，从而维持皮肤中细胞因子驱动的炎症环路。过剩的营养和脂毒性压力损害线粒体功能，增强糖酵解，并诱导髓系和上皮谱系的表观遗传重塑，产生使炎症持久化的代谢记忆。体重指数增加和胰岛素抵抗在临床上与针对肿瘤坏死因子、白细胞介素 (IL)-17 和 IL-23 的生物制剂疗效下降相关，而包括热量限制和胰高血糖素样肽-1 受体激动剂在内的代谢干预措施可改善治疗反应性。最近的多组学、单细胞和空间研究表明，肥胖重塑了真皮和脂肪的免疫微环境，并重新连接了表皮先天免疫，从而削弱了细胞因子阻断疗法的效果。因此，肥胖相关银屑病代表了一种由慢性代谢压力驱动的代谢印记炎症状态。本综述整合了机制和临床见解，并讨论了恢复代谢-免疫塑性以维持疾病缓解的策略。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文深入探讨了肥胖与银屑病之间复杂的代谢-免疫交互机制，指出代谢负荷通过诱导表观遗传重塑和代谢记忆，导致皮肤免疫系统的深度重编程。文章系统阐述了脂肪组织作为炎症器官在驱动系统性与局部炎症中的核心作用，并揭示了肥胖导致生物制剂疗效下降的分子基础。其创新性在于提出了“代谢印记炎症状态”这一概念，并前瞻性地讨论了通过热量限制或GLP-1受体激动剂等代谢干预手段恢复免疫塑性的临床价值，为解决银屑病治疗抵抗提供了跨学科的新视角。

---

## 402. GCN5-ERK乳酰化-磷酸化循环放大乳酸驱动的癌症进展

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41530530)
**期刊：** Nature chemical biology
**PMID：** 41530530
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41589-025-02107-8

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** GCN5-ERK lactylation-phosphorylation loop amplifies lactate-driven cancer progression.

> **英文摘要：**
> The Warburg effect leads to increased lactate production and promotes cancer progression but the underlying mechanisms remain unclear. Here, we found that lactate activates the MAPK pathway through ERK lactylation, which promotes cancer progression. We identified GCN5 as the lactyltransferase responsible for ERK lactylation. Activated ERK phosphorylates GCN5, increasing its lactyltransferase activity toward ERK and establishing a positive feedback loop that amplifies lactate-mediated cancer progression. We provide evidence that lactylation of ERK at residue K231 weakens its interaction with MEK, thereby promoting ERK dimerization and activation. We developed a cell-penetrating peptide that specifically inhibits ERK lactylation. This peptide impairs tumor growth in KRAS-mutant cancer models. Taken together, our findings reveal a molecular mechanism by which lactate accelerates cancer progression through the ERK-GCN5 lactylation-phosphorylation cascade and suggest a strategy to disrupt ERK lactylation in RAS-ERK-driven cancers.

> **中文摘要：**
> 瓦伯格效应导致乳酸产生增加并促进癌症进展，但其潜在机制仍不清楚。在这里，我们发现乳酸通过ERK乳酰化激活MAPK通路，从而促进癌症进展。我们鉴定出GCN5是负责ERK乳酰化的乳酰转移酶。激活的ERK磷酸化GCN5，增加其对ERK的乳酰转移酶活性，并建立了一个放大乳酸介导的癌症进展的正反馈循环。我们提供了证据表明，ERK在K231残基处的乳酰化削弱了其与MEK的相互作用，从而促进了ERK的二聚化和激活。我们开发了一种专门抑制ERK乳酰化的细胞穿透肽。该肽在KRAS突变癌症模型中损害了肿瘤生长。综上所述，我们的发现揭示了乳酸通过ERK-GCN5乳酰化-磷酸化级联反应加速癌症进展的分子机制，并提出了一种在RAS-ERK驱动的癌症中破坏ERK乳酰化的策略。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

这项研究深入探讨了代谢产物乳酸在癌症进展中的非代谢功能，揭示了GCN5介导的ERK乳酰化这一全新的翻译后修饰机制。作者通过生化与细胞模型证明，ERK乳酰化与磷酸化形成的反馈回路是乳酸驱动MAPK信号持续激活的关键，并精准锁定了K231这一关键修饰位点。该研究不仅丰富了瓦伯格效应的分子病理内涵，还开发了针对ERK乳酰化的抑制肽，为KRAS突变等RAS-ERK异常激活的肿瘤治疗提供了极具潜力的创新策略。

## 403. 明晰的静谧工作

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41529229)
**期刊：** Journal of clinical oncology : official journal of the American Society of Clinical Oncology
**PMID：** 41529229
**DOI：** 10.1200/JCO-25-02215

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Quiet Work of Clarity.

> **英文摘要：**
> An ophthalmology resident discovers how vision care can honor end-of-life goals, helping a cancer patient with failing sight write to his children while considering how and when such letters should be read.

> **中文摘要：**
> 一名眼科住院医师发现，视力护理如何能够尊重生命终点的目标，通过帮助一位视力衰退的癌症患者给他的孩子们写信，同时思考此类信件应当在何时以及如何被阅读。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

这是一篇发表在JCO上的具有深刻人文关怀的叙事医学文章，重点探讨了眼科护理在终末期癌症患者安宁疗护中的独特作用。作者通过协助视力衰退患者撰写遗嘱家书的真实案例，揭示了通过改善基本感官功能来维护患者尊严与生命终点愿景的重要性。这种视角拓展了肿瘤临床护理的边界，强调了跨学科合作在满足患者心理社会需求和实现情感传承中的潜在价值。

## 404. 循环转录组分析发现基因特征及免疫细胞激活和丰度可预测膀胱癌的免疫治疗反应

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41528984)
**期刊：** Clinical cancer research : an official journal of the American Association for Cancer Research
**PMID：** 41528984
**DOI：** 10.1158/1078-0432.CCR-25-2306

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Circulating Transcriptome Analysis Finds Gene Signatures and Immune Cell Activation and Abundance Predict Response to Immunotherapy in Bladder Cancer.

> **英文摘要：**
> PURPOSE: Immune checkpoint blockers (ICB) have revolutionized oncology by achieving durable tumor responses in advanced cancers. Nevertheless, currently approved biomarkers (PD-L1, microsatellite instability, and tumor mutational burden) have suboptimal positive and negative predictive values for tumor response and survival. EXPERIMENTAL DESIGN: We aimed to assess the value of RNA sequencing from whole blood to predict responses to ICB. We performed total paired-end RNA sequencing at 20 million reads and analyzed differential gene expression, signaling pathway activation, and immune cell abundances according to cancer outcomes. The analysis was conducted on baseline frozen whole blood samples from 164 patients prospectively enrolled in the IOPREDI study. RESULTS: We found that some immune-related genes and signaling pathways were highly expressed in patients who achieved a durable clinical benefit. Furthermore, analyses of both progression-free survival (PFS) and overall survival (OS) confirmed significantly higher expression levels of immune-related signaling pathways in long-term survivors. Gene expression signatures capable of classifying patients based on clinical response or PFS were also identified. Interestingly, deconvolution analysis revealed a significant higher abundance of resting NK cells in patients with prolonged PFS or OS, in contrast to other cytotoxic cell types. Finally, high expression of the CST7 gene and increased abundance of naïve B lymphocytes were associated with immune-related adverse events (irAE). CONCLUSIONS: Total RNA sequencing from whole blood provides high-quality data to predict clinical response, survival, and occurrence of irAE. The use of this type of sample before immune checkpoint blockage could improve treatment efficacy and irAE management.

> **中文摘要：**
> 目的：免疫检查点阻断剂（ICB）通过在晚期癌症中实现持久的肿瘤反应，彻底改变了肿瘤学领域。然而，目前已批准的生物标志物（PD-L1、微卫星不稳定性和肿瘤突变负荷）在预测肿瘤反应和生存方面的阳性及阴性预测值尚不理想。实验设计：我们旨在评估全血 RNA 测序在预测 ICB 反应中的价值。我们进行了测序深度为 2000 万次读段的全对端总 RNA 测序，并根据癌症预后分析了差异基因表达、信号通路激活和免疫细胞丰度。该分析是基于 IOPREDI 研究中前瞻性招募的 164 名患者的基线冷冻全血样本进行的。结果：我们发现一些免疫相关基因和信号通路在获得持久临床获益的患者中呈高表达。此外，对无进展生存期（PFS）和总生存期（OS）的分析证实，长期生存者的免疫相关信号通路表达水平显著较高。还鉴定了能够根据临床反应或 PFS 对患者进行分类的基因表达特征。有趣的是，反卷积分析显示，与其他细胞毒性细胞类型相比，PFS 或 OS 延长的患者中静息态 NK 细胞的丰度显著较高。最后，CST7 基因的高表达和初始 B 淋巴细胞丰度的增加与免疫相关不良事件（irAE）有关。结论：全血总 RNA 测序为预测临床反应、生存期和 irAE 的发生提供了高质量数据。在接受免疫检查点阻断治疗前使用此类样本，有望提高治疗效力并优化 irAE 的管理。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究通过对 164 例膀胱癌患者的基线全血进行深度转录组测序，探索了循环生物标志物在免疫治疗中的预测价值。研究不仅识别了与临床获益及生存期（PFS/OS）显著相关的基因签名和免疫通路，还通过反卷积技术揭示了静息态 NK 细胞作为预后标志物的独特性。此外，研究将 CST7 基因与 irAE 风险关联，为毒性管理提供了新思路。其创新性在于证明了利用微创全血样本替代组织活检进行多维度疗效和安全性预测的可行性，具有较高的临床转化潜力。

---

## 405. Copanlisib 联合 Niraparib 治疗复发性子宫内膜癌和卵巢癌（COPANIRA）：疗效、毒性及转化研究启示

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41528970)
**期刊：** Clinical cancer research : an official journal of the American Association for Cancer Research
**PMID：** 41528970
**DOI：** 10.1158/1078-0432.CCR-25-1616

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Combination Therapy with Copanlisib and Niraparib in Patients with Recurrent Endometrial and Ovarian Cancer (COPANIRA): Efficacy, Toxicity, and Translational Insights.

> **英文摘要：**
> PURPOSE: Patients with recurrent endometrial or ovarian cancer have poor survival outcomes. We evaluated the clinical efficacy and toxicity of copanlisib [a phosphatidylinositol 3-kinase (PI3K) inhibitor] and niraparib [a poly (ADP-ribose) polymerase inhibitor (PARPi)] in this patient population with translational insights. PATIENTS AND METHODS: This was a phase Ib trial. Copanlisib was administered intravenously on days 1, 8, and 15 of a 28-day cycle, and niraparib was given orally once daily. Four dose levels were explored over a dose-limiting toxicity (DLT) window of 28 days. The primary objective was to determine the recommended phase II dose (RP2D) of this combination. Secondary objectives included safety, objective response rate (ORR), and pharmacokinetics. Tumor biopsies were analyzed using reverse phase protein array (RPPA) to identify molecular correlates of response. RESULTS: Thirty patients were enrolled. An RP2D was not established due to DLTs, most commonly a grade 3 maculopapular rash attributed to copanlisib. The ORR was 12.5% (95% confidence interval, 2.8%-33.6%). RPPA was performed on tumors from eight patients. PI3K pathway activity did not correlate with PI3K mutational status. Nineteen proteins were differentially expressed between patients with stable disease and those with progressive disease; many were substrates of Akt (protein kinase B), implicating downstream PI3K signaling in response. CONCLUSIONS: The combination of copanlisib and niraparib demonstrated limited tolerability, and the ORR was modest. However, functional proteomic analyses identified candidate biomarkers-particularly Akt pathway substrates-which may inform future strategies to optimize PI3K and PARPi combinations.

> **中文摘要：**
> 目的：复发性子宫内膜癌或卵巢癌患者的生存预后较差。我们评估了 copanlisib [一种磷脂酰肌醇 3-激酶 (PI3K) 抑制剂] 联合 niraparib [一种聚 ADP-核糖聚合酶抑制剂 (PARPi)] 在此类患者群体中的临床疗效和毒性，并探讨了转化研究的见解。患者与方法：这是一项 Ib 期试验。Copanlisib 在 28 天为一个周期的第 1、8 和 15 天进行静脉给药，niraparib 每日口服一次。在 28 天的剂量限制性毒性 (DLT) 观察窗口期内探索了四个剂量水平。主要目标是确定该联合方案的推荐 II 期剂量 (RP2D)。次要目标包括安全性、客观缓解率 (ORR) 和药代动力学。通过反相蛋白质阵列 (RPPA) 分析肿瘤活检样本，以识别与疗效相关的分子关联。结果：研究共入组 30 名患者。由于出现 DLT（最常见的是归因于 copanlisib 的 3 级斑丘疹），未能确定 RP2D。ORR 为 12.5%（95% 置信区间：2.8%-33.6%）。对 8 名患者的肿瘤样本进行了 RPPA 分析。结果显示，PI3K 通路活性与 PI3K 突变状态不相关。在疾病稳定患者与疾病进展患者之间存在 19 种差异表达蛋白；其中许多是 Akt（蛋白激酶 B）的底物，提示下游 PI3K 信号传导参与了治疗缓解。结论：Copanlisib 联合 niraparib 的方案耐受性有限，且 ORR 较低。然而，功能蛋白质组学分析确定了候选生物标志物——特别是 Akt 通路底物——这可能为未来优化 PI3K 和 PARPi 联合治疗策略提供参考依据。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该 Ib 期临床试验评估了 PI3K 抑制剂与 PARP 抑制剂联合治疗妇科恶性肿瘤的效果，结果显示该方案因显著的皮肤毒性（DLT）导致耐受性较差，且临床缓解率有限。尽管未能成功建立 RP2D，但该研究的亮点在于转化医学分析，通过 RPPA 技术揭示了 Akt 信号通路底物与治疗反应的关联，而非仅仅依赖基因突变状态。这一发现强调了功能蛋白质组学在指导精准肿瘤治疗联合用药方案中的潜力，为未来的策略优化提供了重要生物标志物线索。

---

## 406. 帕金森病中细胞因子相关的神经炎症：分子通路、治疗靶点及转化见解

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41512596)
**期刊：** Cytokine & growth factor reviews
**PMID：** 41512596
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.cytogfr.2026.01.001

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Cytokine associated neuroinflammation in Parkinson's disease: Molecular pathways, therapeutic targets, and translational insights.

> **英文摘要：**
> Parkinson's disease (PD) is a progressive neurodegenerative disorder in which neuroinflammation plays a key role. An imbalance between pro- and anti-inflammatory cytokines has been observed in both experimental models and PD patients. The inflammatory mediators activate signaling pathways that lead to oxidative stress, excitotoxicity, blood-brain barrier (BBB) disruption, gut dysbiosis, and hypothalamic-pituitary-adrenal axis (HPA-axis) dysregulation. Increased levels of pro-inflammatory cytokines such as tumor necrosis factor-α (TNF-α), Interleukin-1β (IL-1β), Interleukin-6 (IL-6), and others, following PD, stimulate both glial and peripheral immune cells to migrate to injury sites, further promoting neuroinflammation. Cytokines can directly cause neuronal damage and death through various mechanisms. These pathological changes eventually contribute to α-synuclein aggregation and the loss of dopaminergic neurons. The NOD-like receptor family pyrin domain containing 3 (NLRP3) inflammasome, which promotes IL-1β maturation and caspase-1-driven neurotoxicity, has become a critical molecular hub linking innate immune activation to disease progression. Preclinical and clinical studies support that drugs targeting cytokine signaling can reduce neurotoxicity and neurodegeneration. Therapeutic agents that modulate pathways such as ephrin, cyclic GMP-AMP synthase-stimulator of interferon genes (cGAS-STING), Hippo, Receptor-Interacting Protein Kinase 1 (RIPK1), Leucine-rich repeat kinase 2 (LRRK2), and sirtuin pathways have shown anti-inflammatory effects in PD models. Combining approaches targeting immune and cytokine pathways offers a promising strategy for neuroprotection and disease modification in PD.

> **中文摘要：**
> 帕金森病（PD）是一种以神经炎症为关键特征的进展性神经退行性疾病。在实验模型和PD患者中均观察到促炎和抗炎细胞因子之间的平衡失调。炎症介质激活信号通路，导致氧化应激、兴奋性毒性、血脑屏障（BBB）破坏、肠道菌群失调以及下丘脑-垂体-肾上腺轴（HPA轴）功能紊乱。PD发生后，肿瘤坏死因子-α（TNF-α）、白细胞介素-1β（IL-1β）、白细胞介素-6（IL-6）等促炎细胞因子水平升高，刺激神经胶质细胞和外周免疫细胞向损伤部位迁移，进一步促进神经炎症。细胞因子可通过多种机制直接导致神经元损伤和死亡。这些病理变化最终导致α-突触共核蛋白聚集和多巴胺能神经元丢失。含有NOD样受体家族吡啉结构域3（NLRP3）的炎症小体促进IL-1β成熟和caspase-1驱动的神经毒性，已成为连接先天免疫激活与疾病进展的关键分子枢纽。临床前和临床研究支持靶向细胞因子信号传导的药物可以减轻神经毒性和神经变性。调节ephrin、环鸟苷酸-腺苷酸合成酶-干扰素基因刺激因子（cGAS-STING）、Hippo、受体相互作用蛋白激酶1（RIPK1）、富亮氨酸重复激酶2（LRRK2）和sirtuin等通路的治疗药物在PD模型中显示出抗炎作用。结合靶向免疫和细胞因子通路的策略为PD的神经保护和疾病修饰提供了极具前景的方案。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本综述全面系统地阐述了细胞因子介导的神经炎症在帕金森病病理进程中的多重作用，重点强调了NLRP3炎症小体作为先天免疫激活的核心枢纽地位。文章不仅梳理了从氧化应激到肠脑轴紊乱的广泛影响，还前瞻性地总结了cGAS-STING、LRRK2等新兴分子靶点的治疗潜力。评价认为，该文献通过整合分子机制与临床前转化证据，为开发针对PD神经保护的靶向免疫疗法提供了深刻的理论依据与战略指导。

---

## 407. 通过单细胞 DNA 突变与 mRNA 转录本共同捕获技术实现体细胞克隆镶嵌现象的基因型-表型映射

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41481786)
**期刊：** Cancer discovery
**PMID：** 41481786
**DOI：** 10.1158/2159-8290.CD-24-0853

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Genotype-to-Phenotype Mapping of Somatic Clonal Mosaicism via Single-Cell Co-Capture of DNA Mutations and mRNA Transcripts.

> **英文摘要：**
> UNLABELLED: Somatic mosaicism is pervasively observed in human aging, with clonal expansions of cells harboring mutations in recurrently mutated driver genes. Bulk sequencing of tissues captures mutation frequencies but cannot reconstruct clonal architectures nor delineate how driver mutations affect cellular phenotypes. We developed single-cell genotype-to-phenotype sequencing (scG2P) for high-throughput, highly multiplexed, joint capture of genotyping of mutation hotspots and mRNA markers. We applied scG2P to aged esophagus samples from six individuals and observed large numbers of clones with a single driver event, accompanied by rare clones with two driver mutations. NOTCH1 mutants dominate the clonal landscape and are linked to stunted epithelial differentiation, whereas TP53 mutants promote clonal expansion through both differentiation biases and increased cell cycling. Thus, joint single-cell highly multiplexed capture of somatic mutations and mRNA transcripts enables high-resolution reconstruction of clonal architecture and associated phenotypes in solid tissue somatic mosaicism.
> 
> SIGNIFICANCE: Joint single-cell capture of somatic mutations and mRNA transcripts reconstructs clonal architecture and associated phenotypes of the phenotypically normal esophagus, providing the first single-cell genotype-phenotype map of this clonally mosaic tissue to accelerate our understanding of human somatic evolution in solid tissues and provide a window into early cancerous states.

> **中文摘要：**
> 【摘要】在人类衰老过程中普遍观察到体细胞镶嵌现象，其表现为携带反复突变驱动基因的细胞发生克隆扩增。组织的体量测序虽然能捕获突变频率，但无法重建克隆架构，也无法勾勒出驱动突变如何影响细胞表型。我们开发了单细胞基因型-表型测序（scG2P），用于对突变热点基因型和 mRNA 标记物进行高通量、高度多重的联合捕获。我们将 scG2P 应用于来自 6 名个体的老年食管样本，观察到大量具有单一驱动事件的克隆，并伴有携带两个驱动突变的罕见克隆。NOTCH1 突变体在克隆景观中占据主导地位，并与上皮分化受阻相关，而 TP53 突变体则通过分化偏向和细胞周期增加来促进克隆扩增。因此，单细胞水平对体细胞突变和 mRNA 转录本的高度多重联合捕获，能够实现对实体组织体细胞镶嵌现象中克隆架构及其相关表型的高分辨率重建。
> 
> 【意义】体细胞突变与 mRNA 转录本的联合单细胞捕获重建了表型正常的食管的克隆架构及相关表型，提供了该克隆镶嵌组织的首个单细胞基因型-表型图谱，从而加速了我们对实体组织中人类体细胞演化的理解，并为观察早期癌症状态提供了窗口。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文开发了一种名为 scG2P 的创新单细胞多组学技术，旨在解决传统体量测序无法解析克隆架构与细胞表型关联的局限。通过在老年食管组织中的应用，研究揭示了 NOTCH1 和 TP53 突变在驱动克隆扩增中的不同生物学机制，分别涉及分化阻滞和细胞周期加速。该研究首次绘制了正常食管组织的单细胞基因型-表型图谱，为理解实体组织中的体细胞进化及癌症早期演变提供了重要的高分辨率视角。

---

## 409. 靶向脊索瘤肿瘤免疫微环境：从机制见解到治疗突破

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41448553)
**期刊：** Biochimica et biophysica acta. Reviews on cancer
**PMID：** 41448553
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.bbcan.2025.189520

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Targeting the tumor immune microenvironment in chordoma: From mechanistic insights to therapeutic breakthroughs.

> **英文摘要：**
> Chordoma is a rare, malignant bone tumor characterized by high local recurrence rates and resistance to conventional therapies. While immunotherapy has emerged as a promising avenue, its clinical efficacy is currently limited by a profoundly immunosuppressive tumor immune microenvironment (TIME). This review systematically elucidates the molecular and cellular mechanisms underpinning the distinct "immune-excluded" phenotype in chordoma. In this architecture, effector T cells are physically sequestered from tumor cells by dense stromal septa, which paradoxically function as hubs for myeloid-T cell interaction rather than simple physical barriers. This immune-excluded architecture is orchestrated through multiple interconnected mechanisms. Cancer-associated fibroblasts (CAFs), particularly inflammatory and stress-related subpopulations, construct physical barriers via extracellular matrix remodeling while secreting chemokines (such as CXCL12) that spatially anchor T cells within the stroma. The transforming growth factor-beta (TGF-β) pathway reinforces this exclusion by suppressing cytotoxic T cell function and impeding tumor infiltration. Intrinsically, chordoma exhibits a low tumor mutational burden and specific genomic alterations-most notably the loss of CDKN2A/B and PBRM1. Furthermore, despite high chromosomal instability (CIN), co-occurring deletions of 9p and 10q silence the cGAS-STING pathway, thereby impairing antigen presentation and immune cell recruitment. The microenvironment is further dominated by M2-polarized tumor-associated macrophages and regulatory T cells, driving effector T cell exhaustion. Clinical evidence indicates that immune checkpoint inhibitors and targeted vaccines yield limited efficacy as monotherapies, highlighting the immune-excluded phenotype and the scarcity of PD-L1 protein expression as primary obstacles. Future therapeutic breakthroughs will require rational combination strategies, including CAR-T cell therapies targeting novel antigens (e.g., B7-H3) and adoptive T-cell transfer, designed to dismantle stromal barriers and exploit systemic anti-tumor immunity.

> **中文摘要：**
> 脊索瘤是一种罕见的恶性骨肿瘤，其特征是局部复发率高且对常规疗法具有抗性。虽然免疫治疗已成为一种充满前景的途径，但其临床疗效目前受到深度抑制的肿瘤免疫微环境（TIME）的限制。本综述系统地阐明了脊索瘤中独特的“免疫排除型”表型的分子和细胞机制。在这种结构中，效应T细胞被致密的基质隔膜与肿瘤细胞物理隔离，矛盾的是，这些隔膜充当了髓系细胞与T细胞相互作用的中心，而非简单的物理屏障。这种免疫排除结构是通过多种相互关联的机制协调生成的。癌症相关成纤维细胞（CAFs），特别是炎症和压力相关的亚群，通过细胞外基质重塑构建物理屏障，同时分泌趋化因子（如CXCL12），将T细胞空间锁定在基质内。转化生长因子-β（TGF-β）通路通过抑制细胞毒性T细胞功能并阻碍肿瘤浸润，进一步强化了这种排除。从本质上讲，脊索瘤表现出低肿瘤突变负荷和特定的基因组改变——最显著的是CDKN2A/B和PBRM1的缺失。此外，尽管存在高度的染色体不稳定性（CIN），但9p和10q的共同缺失沉默了cGAS-STING通路，从而削弱了抗原呈递和免疫细胞招募。该微环境进一步被M2极化的肿瘤相关巨噬细胞和调节性T细胞主导，驱动效应T细胞耗竭。临床证据表明，免疫检查点抑制剂和靶向疫苗作为单效疗法的疗效有限，凸显了免疫排除型表型和PD-L1蛋白表达匮乏是主要障碍。未来的治疗突破将需要合理的联合策略，包括针对新抗原（如B7-H3）的CAR-T细胞疗法和过继性T细胞转移，旨在拆除基质屏障并利用全身抗肿瘤免疫。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该综述系统剖析了脊索瘤“免疫排除型”微环境的形成机制，重点揭示了基质成纤维细胞（CAFs）介导的物理屏障、CDKN2A/B及PBRM1缺失导致的基因组免疫逃逸，以及cGAS-STING通路沉默的关键作用。文章深入分析了为何单药免疫检查点抑制剂在脊索瘤中疗效有限，并提出了靶向B7-H3的CAR-T疗法及拆除基质屏障的联合策略。其核心贡献在于为这种罕见骨肿瘤提供了从基础分子特征到未来精准免疫治疗转化的清晰路线图。

---

## 410. RESECT：一项关于审计与反馈在非肌层浸润性膀胱癌手术中应用的随机对照试验

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41444076)
**期刊：** European urology
**PMID：** 41444076
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.eururo.2025.09.4174

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** RESECT: A Randomised Controlled Trial of Audit and Feedback in Non-muscle-invasive Bladder Cancer Surgery.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND AND OBJECTIVE: We aimed to determine whether audit, feedback, and education improves surgical performance after transurethral resection of bladder tumour surgery for non-muscle-invasive bladder cancer and as a secondary aim if it reduced recurrence rates. METHODS: This cluster randomised controlled trial compared audit and feedback plus peer comparison and education, with audit alone for four coprimary outcomes: (1) Single-instillation chemotherapy, (2) detrusor muscle sampling, (3) documentation of tumour features, and (4) resection completeness. Early recurrence was a secondary outcome. KEY FINDINGS AND LIMITATIONS: A total of 100 sites were randomised to intervention and 101 to control. In total, 14 915 patients were included. Intervention sites significantly improved documentation of tumour features (adjusted mean difference [95% confidence interval {CI}]: 6.0 [1.8, 10], p = 0.005) and of resection completeness (adjusted mean difference [95% CI]: 5.5 [1.5, 9.5], p = 0.007). There was no statistically significant difference in chemotherapy use (adjusted mean difference [95% CI]: 0.3 [-4.7, 5.3], p = 0.9) or detrusor muscle sampling (adjusted mean difference [95% CI]: 2.6 [-1.3, 6.4], p = 0.2). There was no statistically significant difference in early recurrence rate between arms (adjusted odds ratio [95% CI]: 1.02 [0.8, 1.4], p = 0.9); however, in the control arm, the early recurrence rate reduced compared with baseline (adjusted odds ratio [95% CI]: 0.7 [0.6, 0.9]). CONCLUSIONS AND CLINICAL IMPLICATIONS: Audit and feedback with education improved the documentation of important surgical findings that influence clinical management, but not the performance of detrusor muscle sampling, adjuvant chemotherapy use, or early recurrence rates. Improvements observed in the control arm may explain a lack of effect of the intervention in some outcomes.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景与目标：我们旨在确定审计、反馈和教育是否能改善非肌层浸润性膀胱癌经尿道膀胱肿瘤电切术后的手术表现，并作为次要目标观察其是否能降低复发率。方法：这项集群随机对照试验将“审计和反馈加同行比较及教育”与“仅审计”进行了比较，评估四个共同主要结局：（1）单次灌注化疗；（2）逼尿肌采样；（3）肿瘤特征记录；（4）切除完整性记录。早期复发是次要结局。主要发现与局限性：共有100个中心被随机分配到干预组，101个中心分配到对照组。总共纳入了14,915名患者。干预组显著改善了肿瘤特征记录（调整后的平均差[95%置信区间{CI}]：6.0 [1.8, 10]，p = 0.005）和切除完整性记录（调整后的平均差[95% CI]：5.5 [1.5, 9.5]，p = 0.007）。化疗使用（调整后的平均差[95% CI]：0.3 [-4.7, 5.3]，p = 0.9）或逼尿肌采样（调整后的平均差[95% CI]：2.6 [-1.3, 6.4]，p = 0.2）均无统计学显著差异。两组间的早期复发率无统计学显著差异（调整后的比值比[95% CI]：1.02 [0.8, 1.4]，p = 0.9）；然而，在对照组中，早期复发率较基线有所降低（调整后的比值比[95% CI]：0.7 [0.6, 0.9]）。结论与临床意义：审计、反馈结合教育改善了影响临床管理的重要手术发现的记录，但并未改善逼尿肌采样表现、辅助化疗的使用或早期复发率。在对照组中观察到的改善可能解释了干预措施在某些结局上缺乏效果的原因。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该研究是一项具有重要临床意义的集群随机对照试验，聚焦于通过管理手段提升膀胱癌手术质量。研究结果表明，审计和反馈干预能有效提升手术文档记录的规范化程度，但在改善逼尿肌采样等核心手术技术操作及患者复发率方面表现有限。这一发现提示，单纯的质量反馈可能更容易改变医生的行政行为（如记录），而对于临床核心结局的改善，则可能需要更具针对性的技术培训或流程改进。

---

## 412. 紧密结合的T细胞集群：一类新型高效效应肿瘤杀手

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41421921)
**期刊：** Cytokine & growth factor reviews
**PMID：** 41421921
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.cytogfr.2025.12.007

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Tightly bound T-cell clusters: A new class of hyper-effector tumor killers.

> **英文摘要：**
> T cells have traditionally been characterized as autonomous killers that eliminate malignant cells through single-cell cytotoxicity. However, recent findings reveal that tumor-reactive T cells frequently form tightly bound clusters on the tumor surface, functioning as cooperative hyper-effector units. These clusters establish stable and reinforced immune synapses, sustain prolonged engagement with tumor targets, and coordinate the delivery of perforin, granzymes, and proinflammatory cytokines. As a result, they exhibit markedly enhanced tumor-killing capacity compared with unbound T cells in both ex vivo assays and murine models. This discovery introduces an essential spatial and mechanical dimension to cancer immunology and challenges the prevailing assumption that molecular phenotype alone defines T-cell efficacy. The implications are substantial, extending to tumor-infiltrating lymphocyte (TIL) therapy optimization, the refinement of immunotherapy biomarkers, and the engineering of next-generation CAR-T and CAR-NK platforms. Enriching or mimicking the behavior of cluster-forming T cells may accelerate clinical responses and overcome barriers associated with solid tumors. Collectively, these insights reposition T-cell clustering as a fundamental determinant of effective antitumor immunity.

> **中文摘要：**
> 传统上，T细胞被描述为通过单细胞细胞毒性消除恶性细胞的自主杀手。然而，最近的研究结果显示，肿瘤反应性T细胞经常在肿瘤表面形成紧密结合的集群，作为协同的高效效应单位发挥作用。这些集群建立了稳定且增强的免疫突触，维持与肿瘤靶点的长期接触，并协调穿孔素、颗粒酶和促炎细胞因子的递送。因此，在离体实验和鼠类模型中，与未结合的T细胞相比，它们表现出显著增强的肿瘤杀伤能力。这一发现为癌症免疫学引入了一个关键的空间和机械维度，并挑战了目前认为仅凭分子表型就能定义T细胞效力的普遍假设。其影响是巨大的，可延伸至肿瘤浸润淋巴细胞（TIL）疗法的优化、免疫治疗生物标志物的改进，以及下一代CAR-T和CAR-NK平台的工程化。富集或模仿集群形成T细胞的行为可能会加速临床反应，并克服与实体瘤相关的障碍。总而言之，这些见解将T细胞集群重新定位为有效抗肿瘤免疫的基本决定因素。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文综述了T细胞从“单兵作战”向“集体协作”转变的免疫学新范式，重点阐述了紧密结合的T细胞集群作为高效效应单位的杀伤机制。通过深入探讨集群在稳定免疫突触和协调细胞毒性分子释放方面的空间优势，该综述挑战了传统基于分子表型的T细胞效力评价体系。文章创新性地提出了空间和机械维度在抗肿瘤免疫中的核心作用，为TIL、CAR-T及CAR-NK等新一代细胞疗法的工程化改造提供了极具临床转化价值的新思路。

---

## 414. 前列腺癌中以肿瘤定量替代比例评估：ProQuant 小组的原则

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

## 416. 应用配体 [Ga]Ga-OncoACP3-DOTA 靶向人前列腺癌中前列腺酸性磷酸酶的转化研究及首次人体正电子发射断层扫描成像

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41412909)
**期刊：** European urology
**PMID：** 41412909
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.eururo.2025.11.025

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Translational and First-in-Human Positron Emission Tomography Targeting Prostatic Acid Phosphatase in Prostate Cancer Using the Ligand [Ga]Ga-OncoACP3-DOTA.

> **英文摘要：**
> Prostate-specific membrane antigen (PSMA)-targeted theranostic agents have transformed prostate cancer (PC) management, but their performance is limited by variable PSMA expression and off-target uptake. We investigates the first-in-human positron emission tomography (PET) imaging of prostatic acid phosphatase (ACP3), a novel and highly specific PC target, using the radioligand [Ga]Ga-OncoACP3-DOTA. We analyzed and matched [Ga]Ga-OncoACP3-DOTA and [F]PSMA-1007 PET scans in a cohort of 25 patients with PC. We compared the biodistribution and tumor uptake of the two tracers using the Wilcoxon rank-sum test and compared their performance. Superiority was defined as >10% more lesions detected or >50% higher lesional maximum standardized uptake value (SUV). [Ga]Ga-OncoACP3-DOTA showed low background uptake, including in the salivary glands and kidneys, with a significant difference from the high [F]PSMA-1007 uptake in these organs (p < 0.002). Overall, SUV in localized or metastatic PC did not significantly differ between the two tracers. Better [Ga]Ga-OncoACP3-DOTA performance was observed in 11/25 matched scan pairs, and better [F]PSMA-1007 performance in eight of 25 pairs. [Ga]Ga-OncoACP3-DOTA changed therapeutic management in three of six patients with biochemical recurrence, and in two of 12 patients with known metastases. Although the retrospective comparison is potentially biased, the intense and reliable tumor uptake and the low off-target activity of OncoACP3-DOTA provide a strong rationale for future exploration in trials on PET imaging and radioligand therapy with β- and α-particle emitters.

> **中文摘要：**
> 前列腺特异性膜抗原（PSMA）靶向诊疗剂已经改变了前列腺癌（PC）的管理，但其性能受到可变 PSMA 表达和脱靶摄取的限制。我们使用放射性配体 [Ga]Ga-OncoACP3-DOTA 研究了前列腺酸性磷酸酶（ACP3，一种新型且高度特异性的前列腺癌靶点）的首次人体正电子发射断层扫描（PET）成像。我们在由 25 名前列腺癌患者组成的队列中，分析并匹配了 [Ga]Ga-OncoACP3-DOTA 和 [F]PSMA-1007 PET 扫描。我们使用 Wilcoxon 秩和检验比较了两种显像剂的生物分布和肿瘤摄取，并对比了其性能。优效性定义为检出病变多出 >10% 或病变最大标准化摄取值（SUV）高出 >50%。[Ga]Ga-OncoACP3-DOTA 显示出较低的背景摄取，包括在唾液腺和肾脏中，这与 [F]PSMA-1007 在这些器官中的高摄取具有显著差异（p < 0.002）。总体而言，局限性或转移性前列腺癌中两种显像剂的 SUV 没有显著差异。在 11/25 对匹配的扫描中观察到 [Ga]Ga-OncoACP3-DOTA 表现更好，在 8/25 对中观察到 [F]PSMA-1007 表现更好。在 6 名生化复发患者中的 3 名以及 12 名已知转移患者中的 2 名中，[Ga]Ga-OncoACP3-DOTA 改变了治疗决策。尽管回顾性比较可能存在偏差，但 OncoACP3-DOTA 强烈且可靠的肿瘤摄取以及极低的脱靶活性，为未来探索其在 PET 成像以及利用 β 和 α 粒子发射体进行放射配体治疗的临床试验中提供了强有力的依据。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

这项研究报道了针对前列腺酸性磷酸酶（ACP3）的新型放射性配体 [Ga]Ga-OncoACP3-DOTA 的首次人体 PET 成像，并将其与经典的 PSMA 成像进行了头对头对比。研究发现该显像剂在肿瘤检出和摄取强度上与 PSMA 相当，但其在唾液腺和肾脏等器官的脱靶摄取显著降低，有效规避了 PSMA 靶向药物常见的副作用。尽管作为一项回顾性研究存在局限，但其为 ACP3 作为前列腺癌治疗新靶点提供了坚实的临床证据，尤其在 PSMA 阴性患者和未来的 Alpha/Beta 粒子放射配体治疗中展现出极大的转化应用潜力。

---

## 417. [F]-氟昔洛韦或 [Ga]-PSMA-11 分子显像引导前列腺癌根治术后挽救性放疗剂量递增：EMPIRE-2 试验

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41412908)
**期刊：** European urology
**PMID：** 41412908
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.eururo.2025.12.003

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** [F]-Fluciclovine or [Ga]-PSMA-11 Molecular Imaging To Guide Dose Escalation of Salvage Radiotherapy After Radical Prostatectomy for Prostate Cancer: The EMPIRE-2 Trial.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND AND OBJECTIVE: In EMPIRE-1, [F]-fluciclovine positron emission tomography (PET) imaging to guide salvage radiotherapy (RT) for prostate cancer recurrence after prostatectomy resulted in an improvement in event-free survival (EFS) over conventional imaging alone. The aim of EMPIRE-2 was to explore the impact of RT dose escalation to sites of uptake on PET in comparison to EMPIRE-1. METHODS: EMPIRE-2 was a randomized trial of [F]-fluciclovine versus [Ga]-PSMA-11 in a cohort of men with biochemical progression after prostatectomy and negative conventional imaging findings. After stratification, patients were randomized to RT guided by [F]-fluciclovine PET (arm 1) or [Ga]-PSMA-11 PET (arm 2). PET findings were used for treatment decisions and for RT dose escalation (≤76.0 Gy to the prostate bed and ≤56.0 Gy to the pelvis). The primary endpoint was 2-yr EFS in comparison to the [F]-fluciclovine RT arm in EMPIRE-1. The secondary endpoint was a planned EFS comparison for [F]-fluciclovine versus [Ga]-PSMA-11 in EMPIRE-2. KEY FINDINGS AND LIMITATIONS: In the cohort of 140 patients, 59 randomized to arm 1 patients and 60 randomized to arm 2 completed RT. Median follow-up was 2.6 yr (interquartile range 1.8-4.0). The 2-yr EFS rates were 87% for the overall EMPIRE-2 cohort versus 80% for the EMPIRE-1 comparison cohort (difference 7.7%, 95% confidence interval [CI] 4.7-12%; p = 0.01). After propensity score weighting, the corresponding 2-yr EFS rates were 84% versus 73% (difference 11%, 95% CI 3.6-24%; p = 0.01). The 2-yr EFS rates in the EMPIRE-2 study arms were 87% for [F]-fluciclovine versus 88% for [Ga]-PSMA-11 (difference 0.7%, 95% CI 0.3-1.3%; p > 0.9). CONCLUSIONS AND CLINICAL IMPLICATIONS: Use of either [F]-fluciclovine or [Ga]-PSMA-11 imaging to guide RT dose escalation to sites of PET uptake in the prostate bed and/or pelvis was associated with an improvement in EFS in comparison to a prior trial without dose escalation.

> **中文摘要：**
> 【背景与目的】在 EMPIRE-1 研究中，利用 [F]-氟昔洛韦正电子发射断层扫描 (PET) 显像引导前列腺癌术后复发的挽救性放疗 (RT)，其无事件生存率 (EFS) 较单纯传统显像有所提高。EMPIRE-2 的目的是探讨与 EMPIRE-1 相比，对 PET 摄取部位进行放疗剂量递增的影响。【方法】EMPIRE-2 是一项随机试验，受试者为前列腺癌术后出现生化进展且传统显像结果为阴性的男性群体。经过分层后，患者被随机分配接受 [F]-氟昔洛韦 PET 引导的放疗（第 1 组）或 [Ga]-PSMA-11 PET 引导的放疗（第 2 组）。PET 发现用于治疗决策和放疗剂量递增（前列腺床 ≤76.0 Gy，盆腔 ≤56.0 Gy）。主要终点是与 EMPIRE-1 中 [F]-氟昔洛韦放疗组相比的 2 年 EFS。次要终点是计划在 EMPIRE-2 中对 [F]-氟昔洛韦与 [Ga]-PSMA-11 进行 EFS 比较。【关键发现与局限性】在 140 名患者的队列中，随机分配至第 1 组的 59 名患者和随机分配至第 2 组的 60 名患者完成了放疗。中位随访时间为 2.6 年（四分位间距 1.8-4.0）。EMPIRE-2 总体队列的 2 年 EFS 率为 87%，而 EMPIRE-1 比较队列为 80%（差异 7.7%，95% 置信区间 [CI] 4.7-12%；p = 0.01）。经过倾向评分加权后，相应的 2 年 EFS 率分别为 84% 和 73%（差异 11%，95% CI 3.6-24%；p = 0.01）。EMPIRE-2 研究组中，[F]-氟昔洛韦的 2 年 EFS 率为 87%，[Ga]-PSMA-11 为 88%（差异 0.7%，95% CI 0.3-1.3%；p > 0.9）。【结论与临床意义】使用 [F]-氟昔洛韦或 [Ga]-PSMA-11 显像引导对前列腺床和/或盆腔内 PET 摄取部位进行放疗剂量递增，与此前未进行剂量递增的试验相比，与 EFS 的改善显著相关。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究（EMPIRE-2 试验）通过随机对照设计，证实了在分子显像（[F]-氟昔洛韦或 [Ga]-PSMA-11）引导下对前列腺癌挽救性放疗靶区进行剂量递增可显著提升患者的无事件生存率。研究发现两种示踪剂在引导精准放疗方面的临床获益相近，且均优于 EMPIRE-1 中非剂量递增的方案。这一结果不仅验证了分子显像在个体化放疗决策中的关键作用，也为临床医生提供了灵活的示踪剂选择，是前列腺癌精准治疗领域的又一重要进展。

---

## 419. 下一代多中心研究：利用人工智能自动处理多家机构肺癌患者的非结构化健康记录

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41407195)
**期刊：** Annals of oncology : official journal of the European Society for Medical Oncology
**PMID：** 41407195
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.annonc.2025.12.006

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Next-generation multicenter studies: using artificial intelligence to automatically process unstructured health records of patients with lung cancer across multiple institutions.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND: Manual abstraction of real-world data (RWD) from unstructured health records (HRs) remains resource intensive, error prone, and highly variable across institutions. Large language models (LLMs) offer a scalable alternative, but their performance in multicenter oncology settings is not fully validated.
> 
> PATIENTS AND METHODS: We conducted a multicenter study within the French Large & Unified Cancer Cohort (LUCC) consortium to compare the accuracy of artificial intelligence (AI)-based data extraction against manual abstraction by clinical research professionals. A fine-tuned LLM was applied to de-identified unstructured HRs in PDF format to extract 31 variables from lung cancer patients across 10 centers. Ground truth was defined as concordant values across sources, with discrepant cases adjudicated by a blinded expert. The primary endpoint was the extraction error rates. Secondary endpoints included per-variable performance, interinstitutional variability, F1-score for multiple-choice variables, added value of hybrid AI-human workflows, and survival analyses.
> 
> RESULTS: Among 10 327 patients with AI-based extraction, 311 were included in the test cohort. Across 8708 datapoints for 28 variables with only one correct answer, the LLM achieved a 7.0% error rate, outperforming manual abstraction (14.2%, P <0.001). The F1-scores of three multiple-choice variables were superior (gene alterations 0.97 versus 0.86, comorbidities 0.86 versus 0.76, metastatic sites 0.71 versus 0.69). Interinstitutional variance was lower with AI (0.12% versus 0.39%). A hybrid approach with targeted human review of 30% of low-confidence AI outputs further decreased error rates to 4.4%. Survival analyses based on AI-extracted data closely matched ground truth, with similar median overall and progression-free survival.
> 
> CONCLUSIONS: In a multicenter setting, our AI pipeline yielded lower error rates and greater consistency than manual abstraction. These findings support the feasibility of next-generation, AI-enabled multicenter studies to generate high-quality RWD at scale, with potential applicability in prospective clinical trials.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景：从非结构化健康记录（HRs）中手动提取真实世界数据（RWD）仍然面临资源密集、易出错且机构间差异大的挑战。大语言模型（LLMs）提供了一种可扩展的替代方案，但其在多中心肿瘤学背景下的表现尚未得到充分验证。
> 
> 患者与方法：我们在法国大型统一癌症队列（LUCC）财团内进行了一项多中心研究，旨在比较基于人工智能（AI）的数据提取与临床研究专业人员手动提取的准确性。我们将经过微调的 LLM 应用于 PDF 格式的去隐私化非结构化健康记录，以提取来自 10 个中心的肺癌患者的 31 个变量。基准真相定义为不同来源间一致的数值，不一致的案例由盲法专家裁定。主要终点是提取错误率。次要终点包括各变量表现、机构间变异、多选题变量的 F1 分数、AI-人类混合工作流的附加价值以及生存分析。
> 
> 结果：在 10,327 名接受 AI 提取的患者中，311 名被纳入测试队列。在涉及 28 个仅有一个正确答案的变量的 8708 个数据点中，LLM 的错误率为 7.0%，优于手动提取（14.2%，P <0.001）。三个多选题变量的 F1 分数更高（基因改变 0.97 对比 0.86，合并症 0.86 对比 0.76，转移部位 0.71 对比 0.69）。AI 的机构间差异更低（0.12% 对比 0.39%）。采用对 30% 低置信度 AI 输出进行针对性人工复核的混合方法，进一步将错误率降至 4.4%。基于 AI 提取数据的生存分析与基准真相密切匹配，中位总生存期和无进展生存期相似。
> 
> 结论：在多中心环境下，我们的 AI 流程比手动提取具有更低的错误率和更高的一致性。这些发现支持了开展下一代、AI 赋能的多中心研究以大规模生成高质量 RWD 的可行性，并具有在前瞻性临床试验中的潜在适用性。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究展示了微调大语言模型（LLM）在多中心临床数据自动化提取中的卓越性能，其错误率（7.0%）显著低于临床研究专业人员的手动提取（14.2%），且在机构间一致性上表现更佳。研究通过 F1 分数、生存分析及 AI-人工混合工作流的验证，证明了 AI 处理非结构化医疗数据的可靠性与高效性。这一成果不仅解决了真实世界研究中数据清洗的规模化瓶颈，也为未来 AI 辅助的前瞻性临床试验和大规模临床数据挖掘奠定了技术基础。
