## 421. Imlunestrant联用或不联用阿贝西利治疗晚期乳腺癌：III期EMBER-3试验的更新疗效结果

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41391667)
**期刊：** Annals of oncology : official journal of the European Society for Medical Oncology
**PMID：** 41391667
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.annonc.2025.11.018

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Imlunestrant with or without abemaciclib in advanced breast cancer: updated efficacy results from the phase III EMBER-3 trial.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND: At the primary progression-free survival (PFS) analysis, the phase III EMBER-3 trial in endocrine therapy-pretreated patients with estrogen receptor (ER)-positive, human epidermal growth factor receptor 2 (HER2)-negative advanced breast cancer (ABC) demonstrated significant PFS benefit with imlunestrant versus standard of care (SOC: fulvestrant or exemestane) in patients with ESR1 mutations (ESR1m) and with imlunestrant-abemaciclib versus imlunestrant in all patients, regardless of ESR1m. In this article, we report updated efficacy from a prespecified interim overall survival (OS) analysis.
> 
> PATIENTS AND METHODS: Patients with ER-positive, HER2-negative ABC previously treated with aromatase inhibitors ± cyclin-dependent kinase 4 and 6 inhibitors were randomly assigned (1 : 1 : 1) to receive imlunestrant, SOC, and imlunestrant-abemaciclib. Primary endpoints were PFS in imlunestrant versus SOC in patients with ESR1m and all patients, and versus imlunestrant-abemaciclib in all concurrently randomized patients. OS was a key secondary endpoint (tested if the corresponding PFS was statistically significant). Due to only two of three PFS endpoints being met, a limited significance level was passed to the OS comparisons. Exploratory endpoints included time to chemotherapy, chemotherapy-free survival, and PFS2.
> 
> RESULTS: A total of 874 patients were randomized (imlunestrant, n = 331; SOC, n = 330; imlunestrant-abemaciclib, n = 213). Median follow-up was 28.5 months; 10.1% of patients remained on treatment (data cut-off: 18 August 2025).In patients with ESR1m, median OS (mOS) was 34.5 months for imlunestrant versus 23.1 months for SOC [hazard ratio (HR) 0.60, 95% confidence interval (CI) 0.43-0.86, P = 0.0043, boundary for significance not reached]. In all patients regardless of ESR1m, mOS was not reached with imlunestrant-abemaciclib versus 34.4 months with imlunestrant (HR 0.82, 95% CI 0.59-1.16, P = 0.2622). Updated PFS demonstrated sustained benefit. Notably, in all patients regardless of ESR1m, the median PFS of imlunestrant-abemaciclib versus imlunestrant was 10.9 versus 5.5 months (HR 0.59, 95% CI 0.47-0.74, nominal P < 0.0001). All prespecified exploratory endpoints favored imlunestrant-based regimens. Safety remains consistent with prior reports.
> 
> CONCLUSIONS: These findings reinforce the clinical benefit of imlunestrant-based regimens as a potential all-oral, chemotherapy-free treatment option for endocrine-pretreated patients with ER-positive, HER2-negative ABC.

> **中文摘要：**
> 【背景】在初步无进展生存期（PFS）分析中，针对接受过内分泌治疗的雌激素受体（ER）阳性、人表皮生长因子受体2（HER2）阴性晚期乳腺癌（ABC）患者的III期EMBER-3试验显示，在ESR1突变（ESR1m）患者中，Imlunestrant对比标准治疗（SOC：氟维司群或依西美坦）具有显著的PFS获益；且无论ESR1m状态如何，在所有患者中，Imlunestrant联合阿贝西利对比Imlunestrant均表现出显著的PFS获益。本文报告了预设的中期总生存期（OS）分析的更新疗效结果。
> 
> 【患者与方法】既往接受过芳香化酶抑制剂±细胞周期蛋白依赖性激酶4和6（CDK4/6）抑制剂治疗的ER阳性、HER2阴性ABC患者被随机分配（1:1:1）接受Imlunestrant、SOC或Imlunestrant联合阿贝西利治疗。主要终点是ESR1m患者和所有患者中Imlunestrant对比SOC的PFS，以及在所有同时随机化的患者中Imlunestrant联合阿贝西利对比Imlunestrant的PFS。OS是一个关键次要终点（若相应的PFS具有统计学意义则进行测试）。由于三个PFS终点中仅有两个达到统计学显著，因此仅有有限的显著性水平被传递给OS比较。探索性终点包括至化疗时间、无化疗生存期和PFS2。
> 
> 【结果】共随机分配了874名患者（Imlunestrant组 331例；SOC组 330例；Imlunestrant联合阿贝西利组 213例）。中位随访时间为28.5个月；10.1%的患者仍在接受治疗（数据截止日期：2025年8月18日）。在ESR1m患者中，Imlunestrant组的中位OS（mOS）为34.5个月，而SOC组为23.1个月[风险比（HR）0.60，95%置信区间（CI）0.43-0.86，P=0.0043，未达到显著性界值]。在不考虑ESR1m状态的所有患者中，Imlunestrant联合阿贝西利组的mOS未达到，而Imlunestrant单药组为34.4个月（HR 0.82，95% CI 0.59-1.16，P=0.2622）。更新后的PFS显示出持续获益。值得注意的是，在所有患者中，Imlunestrant联合阿贝西利对比Imlunestrant的中位PFS分别为10.9个月和5.5个月（HR 0.59，95% CI 0.47-0.74，标称P < 0.0001）。所有预设的探索性终点均支持基于Imlunestrant的方案。安全性与之前的报告保持一致。
> 
> 【结论】这些发现强化了基于Imlunestrant方案的临床获益，为既往接受过内分泌治疗的ER阳性、HER2阴性晚期乳腺癌患者提供了一种潜在的全口服、免化疗的治疗选择。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

EMBER-3试验的更新分析进一步巩固了新一代口服SERD药物Imlunestrant在ER+/HER2-晚期乳腺癌二线及以后治疗中的地位。研究显示，Imlunestrant单药在ESR1突变人群中展现出显著的生存获益趋势（HR 0.60），而其与阿贝西利的联合方案在全人群中显著延长了PFS（10.9 vs 5.5个月），提供了强大的协同效应。尽管OS分析因统计学严苛性尚未达到预设的显著性界值，但整体数据的一致性及全口服方案的便利性，使其有望成为后CDK4/6抑制剂时代的重要治疗选择。

## 422. 深度学习利用数字病理学鉴别胸腺上皮肿瘤的组织学亚型

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41390119)
**期刊：** Annals of oncology : official journal of the European Society for Medical Oncology
**PMID：** 41390119
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.annonc.2025.12.003

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Deep learning discriminates thymic epithelial tumors' histological subtypes using digital pathology.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND: Thymic epithelial tumors (TETs) are rare malignancies that pose significant diagnostic challenges due to their heterogeneous histological patterns and substantial interobserver variability in classification. Despite standardized World Health Organization (WHO) classification criteria, diagnostic concordance remains suboptimal, particularly in nonexpert settings, where second-opinion reviews lead to diagnostic reclassification in up to 57% of cases. Deep learning may offer a tool to reduce diagnostic variability and improve the consistency of histological classification. MATERIALS AND METHODS: We trained a deep learning-based model using hematoxylin-eosin (H&E) whole-slide images from The Cancer Genome Atlas as a training dataset. The model incorporated a novel hierarchical loss function designed to reflect clinically relevant tumor groupings based on treatment strategies and patient outcomes. We validated the model on 112 consecutive cases from the University of Chicago, with diagnoses confirmed by an expert thoracic pathologist. Model performances were evaluated using both a three-group hierarchical scheme and the six-class WHO classification. RESULTS: In the clinically relevant hierarchical three-group classification (As: A + AB; Bs: B1 + B2 + B3; and thymic carcinoma), the model achieved an accuracy of 91.1% with Cohen's κ = 0.859, indicating almost perfect agreement. In the six-class classification (A, AB, B1, B2, B3, and thymic carcinoma), the accuracy was 77.7% with κ = 0.716. The model demonstrated 100% sensitivity and 94.6% accuracy for thymic carcinoma detection. Notably, 60% of misclassifications occurred within the same clinical management group, thereby limiting their impact on therapeutic decision making. CONCLUSION: This deep learning model demonstrates strong potential as a diagnostic tool for TETs classification, particularly in settings with limited thoracic pathology expertise. The high sensitivity for thymic carcinoma detection and robust performance across different tissue processing conditions suggest its clinical applicability for improving diagnostic consistency and supporting pathological decision making in both specialized and nonspecialized settings.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景：胸腺上皮肿瘤（TETs）是罕见的恶性肿瘤，由于其异质性的组织学模式以及分类中显著的观察者间差异，给诊断带来了巨大挑战。尽管有标准化的世界卫生组织（WHO）分类标准，但诊断一致性仍不理想，特别是在非专家环境下，二次意见审查导致高达57%的病例发生诊断重新分类。深度学习可能提供一种工具来减少诊断差异并提高组织学分类的一致性。材料与方法：我们利用来自癌症基因组图谱（TCGA）的苏木精-伊红（H&E）全视野数字化切片作为训练数据集，训练了一个基于深度学习的模型。该模型结合了一种新型的分层损失函数，旨在反映基于治疗策略和患者预后的临床相关肿瘤分组。我们在芝加哥大学的112例连续病例中验证了该模型，诊断结果由一名资深的胸部病理学家确认。模型性能分别使用三组分层方案和六类WHO分类进行评估。结果：在临床相关的分层三组分类中（A组：A + AB；B组：B1 + B2 + B3；以及胸腺癌），模型达到了91.1%的准确率，Cohen's κ = 0.859，表明几乎完全一致。在六类分类（A、AB、B1、B2、B3和胸腺癌）中，准确率为77.7%，κ = 0.716。该模型在检测胸腺癌方面表现出100%的敏感性和94.6%的准确性。值得注意的是，60%的误分类发生在同一个临床管理组内，从而限制了它们对治疗决策的影响。结论：该深度学习模型展示了作为TETs分类诊断工具的强大潜力，特别是在胸部病理专业知识有限的环境中。对胸腺癌检测的高敏感性以及在不同组织处理条件下的稳健表现，表明了其在提高诊断一致性以及支持专业和非专业环境下的病理决策方面的临床适用性。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究开发并验证了一种基于深度学习的数字病理模型，旨在解决胸腺上皮肿瘤（TETs）分类中极高的观察者差异问题。该模型的创新之处在于引入了符合临床诊疗逻辑的分层损失函数，在临床相关的三组分类中表现卓越（准确率91.1%），且对胸腺癌的检出达到了100%的敏感性。尽管在精细的WHO六类分类中准确率略有下降，但多数误诊并不影响临床管理，充分证明了该系统作为辅助诊断工具、提升基层医疗诊断一致性的显著临床价值。

---

## 423. 曲妥珠单抗辅助治疗20周年：突破性时刻的回顾与反思

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41386295)
**期刊：** Annals of oncology : official journal of the European Society for Medical Oncology
**PMID：** 41386295
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.annonc.2025.12.002

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** 20th anniversary of adjuvant trastuzumab: reflections on a breakthrough moment.

> **英文摘要：**
> Twenty years after its initial approval, trastuzumab remains a cornerstone in the treatment of patients with human epidermal growth factor receptor 2 (HER2)-positive early breast cancer (eBC). Long-term follow-up from pivotal adjuvant trials has consistently demonstrated significant and durable improvements in survival outcomes across various risk groups and chemotherapy backbones. In parallel, trastuzumab-induced cardiotoxicity (TIC) remains overall infrequent, particularly in patients without prior exposure to anthracycline and appears comparable to the incidence observed in the general population after treatment completion. While real-world data further support the long-term efficacy and safety of trastuzumab, advancements such as more convenient subcutaneous formulations and the widespread availability of more accessible cost-effective biosimilars solidify its ongoing relevance in clinical practice. Conversely, despite two decades of clinical and translational research, no predictive biomarker beyond HER2 overexpression or amplification has yet been validated to guide trastuzumab use. Emerging candidates, including stromal tumor-infiltrating lymphocytes, circulating tumor DNA, and the HER2DX genomic assay, are not yet validated for use in clinical practice, although prospective studies are ongoing. Similarly, while clinical factors and imaging tools may help identify early on patients at higher risk of experiencing TIC, no cardioprotective strategy has yet demonstrated robust and conclusive benefit. Despite the emergence of newer anti-HER2 agents and evolving treatment paradigms, trastuzumab will probably continue to serve as a key therapeutic backbone, especially for patients with lower-risk HER2-positive eBC.

> **中文摘要：**
> 在首次获批二十年后，曲妥珠单抗仍是人表皮生长因子受体2（HER2）阳性早期乳腺癌（eBC）患者治疗的基石。关键性辅助临床试验的长期随访一致表明，在不同的风险组和化疗方案中，生存结局均得到了显著且持久的改善。与此同时，曲妥珠单抗诱导的心脏毒性（TIC）总体上仍然罕见，特别是在既往未接受过蒽环类药物治疗的患者中，且在治疗完成后观察到的发生率与普通人群相当。虽然真实世界数据进一步支持了曲妥珠单抗的长期疗效和安全性，但更便捷的皮下注射剂型以及更具成本效益的生物类似药的广泛普及，巩固了其在临床实践中的持续地位。相反，尽管经过了二十年的临床和转化研究，除了HER2过表达或扩增之外，尚未有其他预测性生物标志物被证实可用于指导曲妥珠单抗的使用。新兴的候选标志物，包括间质肿瘤浸润淋巴细胞（sTILs）、循环肿瘤DNA（ctDNA）和HER2DX基因组检测，虽然前瞻性研究正在进行中，但尚未被证实可用于临床实践。同样，虽然临床因素和影像学工具可能有助于早期识别发生TIC风险较高的患者，但目前尚无心脏保护策略显示出稳健且确凿的获益。尽管出现了更新的抗HER2药物和不断演变的治疗模式，曲妥珠单抗可能仍将作为关键的治疗基石，特别是对于低风险的HER2阳性早期乳腺癌患者。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文回顾了曲妥珠单抗在HER2阳性早期乳腺癌辅助治疗领域应用20年的里程碑意义，肯定了其作为标准疗法的基石地位。文章总结了其在不同风险群体中稳健的生存获益及良好的长期安全性，并指出皮下制剂与生物类似药进一步提升了临床可及性。尽管在寻找新型预测性生物标志物和确切心脏保护策略方面仍存局限，但作者强调，即使在新药涌现的今天，曲妥珠单抗对于低风险患者仍具有不可替代的临床价值。

---

## 424. 晚期卵巢癌中 PARP 抑制剂/免疫治疗的悖论：阳性终点与令人费解的解读

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41386294)
**期刊：** Annals of oncology : official journal of the European Society for Medical Oncology
**PMID：** 41386294
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.annonc.2025.12.004

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** The PARP inhibitor/immunotherapy paradox in advanced ovarian cancer: positive endpoints, perplexing interpretations.

> **英文摘要：**
> No abstract available.

> **中文摘要：**
> 无摘要。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文深入探讨了晚期卵巢癌领域中 PARP 抑制剂联合免疫治疗所面临的临床困境，指出尽管部分临床试验达到了预设的阳性研究终点，但其疗效数据背后的生物学机制和实际获益解读仍存在巨大争议。文章核心目的在于揭示这种“阳性结果与解读困惑”并存的矛盾现象，并对现有治疗方案的有效性提出了批判性反思。这对未来优化卵巢癌的联合免疫治疗策略以及精准筛选获益人群具有重要的学术指导意义。

---

## 425. 度伐利尤单抗联合卡铂/紫杉醇及贝伐珠单抗，随后序贯度伐利尤单抗联合贝伐珠单抗（加或不加奥拉帕利维持治疗）用于新诊断的非BRCA突变晚期卵巢癌。

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41380962)
**期刊：** Annals of oncology : official journal of the European Society for Medical Oncology
**PMID：** 41380962
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.annonc.2025.11.020

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Durvalumab with carboplatin/paclitaxel and bevacizumab followed by durvalumab and bevacizumab with or without olaparib maintenance in newly diagnosed non-BRCA-mutated advanced ovarian cancer.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND: Despite treatment advances in newly diagnosed advanced-stage ovarian cancer (aOC), improved outcomes are needed. PATIENTS AND METHODS: DUO-O (NCT03737643), a phase III placebo-controlled trial, enrolled patients with newly diagnosed aOC. Following one cycle of carboplatin/paclitaxel ± bevacizumab, patients without a tumor BRCA mutation (non-tBRCAm) were randomly assigned (1 : 1 : 1) at cycle 2 to carboplatin/paclitaxel plus bevacizumab followed by bevacizumab (control); carboplatin/paclitaxel, bevacizumab plus durvalumab followed by bevacizumab plus durvalumab (durvalumab arm); or carboplatin/paclitaxel, bevacizumab plus durvalumab followed by bevacizumab, durvalumab plus olaparib (durvalumab + olaparib arm). Investigator-assessed progression-free survival (PFS; primary endpoint) was tested for the durvalumab + olaparib arm versus control in the non-tBRCAm homologous recombination deficiency (HRD)-positive and non-tBRCAm intention-to-treat (ITT) populations. RESULTS: One thousand one hundred and thirty patients were randomly allocated to the study. The prespecified interim PFS analysis [data cut-off (DCO): 5 December 2022] qualified as the primary analysis; PFS hazard ratio (HR) for the durvalumab + olaparib arm versus control was 0.49 [95% confidence interval (CI) 0.34-0.69, P < 0.0001; median (m) PFS 37.3 versus 23.0 months] in the non-tBRCAm HRD-positive and 0.63 (95% CI 0.52-0.76, P < 0.0001; mPFS 24.2 versus 19.3 months) in the non-tBRCAm ITT population. For the durvalumab arm versus control, PFS HR was 0.87 (95% CI 0.73-1.04, P = 0.13; mPFS 20.6 versus 19.3 months) in the non-tBRCAm ITT population. At final PFS and interim overall survival (OS) analysis (DCO: 18 September 2023), PFS results were consistent with primary analysis; interim OS HR for the durvalumab + olaparib arm versus control was 0.95 (95% CI 0.76-1.20, P = 0.68; 39.0% maturity) in the non-tBRCAm ITT population. Safety was generally consistent with the profiles of the individual agents. CONCLUSIONS: DUO-O met its primary PFS endpoints for first-line durvalumab plus carboplatin/paclitaxel and bevacizumab followed by durvalumab, bevacizumab plus olaparib maintenance versus carboplatin/paclitaxel and bevacizumab followed by bevacizumab in the non-tBRCAm HRD-positive and non-tBRCAm ITT populations. Further insight into long-term benefit is anticipated with additional follow-up.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景：尽管新诊断晚期卵巢癌（aOC）的治疗取得了进展，但仍需改善预后。患者与方法：DUO-O（NCT03737643）是一项III期、安慰剂对照试验，招募了新诊断的aOC患者。经过一个周期的卡铂/紫杉醇±贝伐珠单抗治疗后，无肿瘤BRCA突变（non-tBRCAm）的患者在第2周期被随机分配（1:1:1）至：卡铂/紫杉醇联合贝伐珠单抗，随后序贯贝伐珠单抗（对照组）；卡铂/紫杉醇、贝伐珠单抗联合度伐利尤单抗，随后序贯贝伐珠单抗联合度伐利尤单抗（度伐利尤单抗组）；或卡铂/紫杉醇、贝伐珠单抗联合度伐利尤单抗，随后序贯贝伐珠单抗、度伐利尤单抗联合奥拉帕利（度伐利尤单抗+奥拉帕利组）。研究者评估的无进展生存期（PFS；主要终点）在non-tBRCAm同源重组缺陷（HRD）阳性和non-tBRCAm意向性治疗（ITT）人群中针对度伐利尤单抗+奥拉帕利组与对照组进行了检验。结果：1130名患者被随机分配至该研究。预设的PFS中期分析[数据截止日期（DCO）：2022年12月5日]被认定为主要分析；在non-tBRCAm HRD阳性人群中，度伐利尤单抗+奥拉帕利组与对照组相比，PFS风险比（HR）为0.49 [95%置信区间（CI）0.34-0.69，P < 0.0001；中位（m）PFS 37.3个月 vs 23.0个月]；在non-tBRCAm ITT人群中，HR为0.63（95% CI 0.52-0.76，P < 0.0001；mPFS 24.2个月 vs 19.3个月）。在non-tBRCAm ITT人群中，度伐利尤单抗组与对照组相比，PFS HR为0.87（95% CI 0.73-1.04，P = 0.13；mPFS 20.6个月 vs 19.3个月）。在最终PFS和中期总生存期（OS）分析（DCO：2023年9月18日）中，PFS结果与主要分析一致；在non-tBRCAm ITT人群中，度伐利尤单抗+奥拉帕利组与对照组相比，中期OS HR为0.95（95% CI 0.76-1.20，P = 0.68；成熟度39.0%）。安全性与各单药的特征基本一致。结论：DUO-O达到了其主要PFS终点，证明在non-tBRCAm HRD阳性和non-tBRCAm ITT人群中，一线度伐利尤单抗联合卡铂/紫杉醇和贝伐珠单抗，随后序贯度伐利尤单抗、贝伐珠单抗联合奥拉帕利维持治疗，优于卡铂/紫杉醇联合贝伐珠单抗随后序贯贝伐珠单抗。随着进一步随访，预计将获得有关长期获益的更多洞察。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

这项III期DUO-O试验评估了免疫治疗（度伐利尤单抗）与PARP抑制剂（奥拉帕利）联合用药在非BRCA突变晚期卵巢癌一线治疗中的疗效。研究结果显著，特别是在HRD阳性亚组中，三联联合方案显著延长了患者的无进展生存期（PFS），为非BRCA突变患者提供了新的一线治疗路径。尽管度伐利尤单抗单加方案相比对照组未显示出统计学显著的PFS获益，但“免疫+抗血管生成+PARP抑制剂”的维持模式显示出强大的抗肿瘤活性且安全性可控。目前OS数据尚不成熟，其长期生存获益仍需持续观察。

## 426. 曲贝替定联合奥拉帕利对比单药曲贝替定治疗蒽环类药物方案失败后的晚期软组织肉瘤（TOMAS2）：一项来自意大利肉瘤工作组的随机II期研究

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41354211)
**期刊：** Annals of oncology : official journal of the European Society for Medical Oncology
**PMID：** 41354211
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.annonc.2025.11.019

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Trabectedin-olaparib combination or trabectedin in advanced soft tissue sarcomas after failure of anthracycline-based treatment (TOMAS2): a randomized phase II study from the Italian Sarcoma Group.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND: Advanced/metastatic soft tissue sarcomas (STSs) remain an unmet clinical need. We previously reported the feasibility and preliminary activity of trabectedin-olaparib combination in patients with advanced STS progressing after anthracycline-based regimens. PATIENTS AND METHODS: In this investigator-initiated, open-label, phase II randomized trial, adult patients with advanced STS progressing after one or more prior lines of therapy, including at least one anthracycline-based regimen, were randomly assigned 1 : 1 to trabectedin 1.1 mg/m every 21 days (q21d) intravenous (i.v.) plus olaparib tablets 150 mg twice a day, or trabectedin 1.5 mg/m q21d i.v. Randomization stratified patients by histology (L-sarcoma, i.e. leiomyosarcoma and liposarcoma versus non-L-sarcoma) and number of prior therapies (one versus two or more). The primary endpoint was progression-free survival (PFS) rate at 6 months (PFS6m) per RECIST1.1. Secondary endpoints included PFS, overall survival (OS), RECIST1.1 overall response rate (ORR), and safety. Exploratory endpoints encompassed biomarker/molecular analyses. RESULTS: Between 25 May 2020 and 2 November 2022, 130 patients were enrolled at 13 Italian Sarcoma Group centers (81 female; 67 L-sarcoma; 93 one prior line). With a median follow-up of 37.4 months, PFS6m and median PFS were 32% [95% confidence interval (CI) 22% to 46%] and 3.9 months (95% CI 2.7-5.2 months) with trabectedin-olaparib versus 28% (95% CI 19% to 42%) and 2.9 months (95% CI 2.2-3.6 months) with trabectedin [hazard ratio (HR) 0.722, 95% CI 0.501-1.041, P = 0.081]. Among 126 assessable patients, ORR was 12.7% (95% CI 6.1% to 22.7%) versus 7.9% (95% CI 3.0% to 16.7%), respectively (odds ratio 1.60, 95% CI 0.50-5.16, P = 0.43). In the uterine leiomyosarcoma subgroup, 12-month PFS was 42.9% with trabectedin-olaparib versus 0% with trabectedin. PARP1 expression significantly correlated with improved PFS with trabectedin-olaparib (PFS6m and median PFS were 41.5% and 4.3 months versus 27.8% and 2.5 months; HR 0.537, 95% CI 0.337-0.855, P = 0.009). Grade ≥3 hematological toxicities were significantly more frequent with trabectedin-olaparib. CONCLUSIONS: Although trabectedin-olaparib combination reached the prespecified threshold for statistical significance for PFS (P < 0.10), the benefit was marginal in the all-comers STS population. Nonetheless, patients affected by PARP1-expressing STS and uterine leiomyosarcoma derived substantial benefit from the combination, supporting further histology- and biomarker-driven investigation in these settings.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景：晚期/转移性软组织肉瘤（STSs）仍是尚未满足的临床需求。我们此前报道了曲贝替定联合奥拉帕利在蒽环类药物方案治疗后进展的晚期STS患者中的可行性和初步活性。患者与方法：在这项由研究者发起的、开放标签、II期随机试验中，经一线或多线治疗（包括至少一种蒽环类药物方案）后进展的成年晚期STS患者被按1:1的比例随机分配至曲贝替定 1.1 mg/m² 每21天一次（q21d）静脉注射（i.v.）联合奥拉帕利片剂 150 mg 每日两次组，或曲贝替定 1.5 mg/m² q21d i.v. 单药组。随机化根据组织学（L-型肉瘤，即平滑肌肉瘤和脂肪肉瘤，对比非L-型肉瘤）和既往治疗线数（一次对比两次或更多）对患者进行分层。主要终点是根据RECIST 1.1标准评估的6个月无进展生存（PFS6m）率。次要终点包括PFS、总生存期（OS）、根据RECIST 1.1评估的总缓解率（ORR）以及安全性。探索性终点包括生物标志物/分子分析。结果：在2020年5月25日至2022年11月2日期间，来自13家意大利肉瘤工作组中心的130名患者被纳入研究（81名女性；67名L-型肉瘤；93名接受过一次既往治疗）。中位随访时间为37.4个月。曲贝替定-奥拉帕利组的PFS6m和中位PFS分别为32% [95% 置信区间 (CI) 22% - 46%] 和 3.9个月 (95% CI 2.7-5.2个月)，而曲贝替定单药组分别为28% (95% CI 19% - 42%) 和 2.9个月 (95% CI 2.2-3.6个月) [风险比 (HR) 0.722, 95% CI 0.501-1.041, P = 0.081]。在126名可评估患者中，ORR分别为12.7% (95% CI 6.1% - 22.7%) 和 7.9% (95% CI 3.0% - 16.7%)（比值比 1.60, 95% CI 0.50-5.16, P = 0.43）。在子宫平滑肌肉瘤亚组中，曲贝替定-奥拉帕利组的12个月PFS率为42.9%，而曲贝替定单药组为0%。PARP1表达与曲贝替定-奥拉帕利组PFS的改善显著相关（PFS6m和中位PFS分别为41.5%和4.3个月，而对比组为27.8%和2.5个月；HR 0.537, 95% CI 0.337-0.855, P = 0.009）。曲贝替定-奥拉帕利组的≥3级血液学毒性显著更频繁。结论：尽管曲贝替定-奥拉帕利联合方案达到了预设的PFS统计学显著性阈值（P < 0.10），但在全人群STS中获益有限。然而，受PARP1表达STS和子宫平滑肌肉瘤影响的患者从该联合方案中获得了显著获益，这支持在这些领域进一步开展由组织学和生物标志物驱动的研究。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究（TOMAS2）探讨了曲贝替定联合奥拉帕利在晚期软组织肉瘤（STS）二线及以后治疗中的潜力。虽然在非选择的全人群中联合用药对比单药曲贝替定的优势较为有限，但亚组分析揭示了在子宫平滑肌肉瘤及PARP1高表达患者中存在显著的生存获益，具有重要的转化医学价值。研究指出了生物标志物筛选对提高STS免疫/靶向联合治疗响应的重要性。尽管联合方案增加了血液学毒性，但其为特定分子亚型患者提供了精准治疗的新方向。

## 427. 循环肿瘤DNA阳性预测高级别pT1期膀胱尿路上皮癌患者生存期较短

## 428. 膀胱肿瘤微环境是一个动态生态系统：微生物、免疫与癌症的交汇。

## 429. 可切除早中期非小细胞肺癌患者围术期替雷利珠单抗联合新辅助化疗：随机RATIONALE-315试验的最终分析

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41344593)
**期刊：** Annals of oncology : official journal of the European Society for Medical Oncology
**PMID：** 41344593
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.annonc.2025.11.017

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Perioperative tislelizumab plus neoadjuvant chemotherapy for patients with resectable non-small-cell lung cancer: final analysis of the randomized RATIONALE-315 trial.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND: Perioperative immunotherapy, particularly anti-programmed cell death protein 1 therapy, combined with neoadjuvant chemotherapy has emerged as one of the standard-of-care options for resectable non-small-cell lung cancer (NSCLC). We report the final analysis of RATIONALE-315, a randomized, double-blind, phase III trial evaluating the efficacy and safety of perioperative tislelizumab plus neoadjuvant chemotherapy versus neoadjuvant chemotherapy alone in patients with resectable, stage II-IIIA NSCLC. PATIENTS AND METHODS: Adult patients in China were randomized (1 : 1) to receive either perioperative tislelizumab or placebo in combination with neoadjuvant chemotherapy. The dual primary endpoints were event-free survival (EFS) and major pathological response, assessed by blinded independent central review. The secondary endpoints included pathological complete response, overall survival (OS), disease-free survival, and safety. RESULTS: In total, 453 patients were randomized (226 to tislelizumab and 227 to placebo). At the final analysis (median study follow-up of 38.5 months), patients in the tislelizumab group experienced statistically significantly improved OS versus those in the placebo group {hazard ratio (HR) 0.65 [95% confidence interval (CI) 0.45-0.93]; P = 0.009}. The median OS was not reached in either group. The 36-month OS rate was 79.3% in the tislelizumab group versus 69.3% in the placebo group. The median EFS was not reached in the tislelizumab group versus 30.6 months in the placebo group [HR 0.58 (95% CI 0.43-0.79)]. Survival benefits were generally consistent across subgroups. The safety profile of tislelizumab plus chemotherapy was tolerable and consistent with known profiles of the individual therapies. CONCLUSIONS: Neoadjuvant tislelizumab plus chemotherapy and adjuvant tislelizumab demonstrated a statistically significant, clinically meaningful OS benefit and sustained, clinically meaningful EFS improvement compared with neoadjuvant chemotherapy, with a tolerable safety profile in patients with resectable stage II-IIIA NSCLC. These results support the use of this regimen in this patient population.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景：围术期免疫治疗，特别是抗程序性细胞死亡蛋白1（PD-1）治疗联合新辅助化疗，已成为可切除非小细胞肺癌（NSCLC）的标准治疗选择之一。我们报告了RATIONALE-315的最终分析结果，这是一项随机、双盲、III期试验，旨在评估围术期替雷利珠单抗联合新辅助化疗对比单纯新辅助化疗在可切除II-IIIA期NSCLC患者中的疗效和安全性。患者和方法：中国的成年患者被随机（1:1）分配接受围术期替雷利珠单抗或安慰剂联合新辅助化疗。双主要终点是经盲态独立中心评审评估的无事件生存期（EFS）和主要病理缓解。次要终点包括病理完全缓解、总生存期（OS）、无病生存期和安全性。结果：总计453名患者被随机分配（替雷利珠单抗组226名，安慰剂组227名）。在最终分析中（中位随访时间为38.5个月），替雷利珠单抗组患者的OS较安慰剂组有显著统计学意义的改善 {风险比(HR) 0.65 [95%置信区间(CI) 0.45-0.93]; P = 0.009}。两组均未达到中位OS。替雷利珠单抗组的36个月OS率为79.3%，而安慰剂组为69.3%。替雷利珠单抗组的中位EFS未达到，而安慰剂组为30.6个月 [HR 0.58 (95% CI 0.43-0.79)]。各亚组的生存获益基本一致。替雷利珠单抗联合化疗的安全性特征良好，且与已知单药疗法的安全性特征一致。结论：对于可切除II-IIIA期NSCLC患者，新辅助替雷利珠单抗联合化疗及辅助替雷利珠单抗治疗相比于单纯新辅助化疗，表现出具有统计学意义和临床意义的OS获益以及持久、具有临床意义的EFS改善，且安全性可耐受。这些结果支持在该患者人群中使用该方案。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究是RATIONALE-315试验的最终分析结果，具有里程碑式意义。该研究证实，围术期替雷利珠单抗联合化疗方案能显著提高II-IIIA期可切除NSCLC患者的总生存期（OS），HR达到0.65，且风险获益在各亚组中高度一致。作为一项在中国人群中开展的高质量III期临床研究，其长期随访数据进一步夯实了围术期免疫治疗的临床价值，为该类患者提供了更强有力的循证医学证据。

---

## 430. 人类细胞中中心粒生物发生的关键成分与组装原理

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41310006)
**期刊：** Nature reviews. Molecular cell biology
**PMID：** 41310006
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41580-025-00921-5

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Critical constituents and assembly principles of centriole biogenesis in human cells.

> **英文摘要：**
> The centriole is an evolutionarily conserved microtubule-bearing organelle with a striking 9-fold symmetrical architecture that is crucial for fundamental cellular processes in eukaryotes, including polarity, signalling and motility. The last two decades have witnessed important progress in uncovering the molecular architecture and assembly principles governing centriole biogenesis, which are discussed in this Review, with a focus on human cells. Recently developed advanced microscopy approaches have increased our understanding of the mechanisms governing centriole biogenesis, from initiating the assembly process to forming a full-fledged organelle. Some two billion years after its emergence during evolution, and more than 100 years after its identification by pioneering scientists, these advances make the centriole ripe for another era of discoveries.

> **中文摘要：**
> 中心粒是一种在进化上保守的含微管细胞器，具有显著的九重对称结构，对于真核生物的基本细胞过程（包括极性、信号传导和运动）至关重要。过去二十年里，在揭示控制中心粒生物发生的分子结构和组装原理方面取得了重大进展，本文对此进行了综述，并重点关注人类细胞。最近开发的先进显微镜技术增强了我们对控制中心粒生物发生机制的理解，从启动组装过程到形成成熟的细胞器。在其进化出现约二十亿年、以及被先驱科学家发现一百多年后，这些进展使中心粒研究迎来了另一个发现时代。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本综述系统性地梳理了人类细胞中中心粒生物发生的分子架构与组装逻辑，重点总结了过去二十年在该领域取得的里程碑式进展。文章深入探讨了先进显微成像技术如何革新我们对从组装起始到器形成熟全过程的认知，具有极高的学术参考价值。该综述不仅强调了中心粒在生物进化中的保守性，还通过整合最新研究数据，预示了这一经典细胞器研究领域正迈向由新技术驱动的全新爆发期。

---

## 432. ESCRT-III 在膜分裂与修复中的功能

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41299081)
**期刊：** Nature reviews. Molecular cell biology
**PMID：** 41299081
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41580-025-00909-1

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** ESCRT-III function in membrane fission and repair.

> **英文摘要：**
> The endosomal sorting complex required for transport (ESCRT) machinery is an evolutionarily conserved multisubunit protein complex that remodels cellular membranes. Beyond its classical role in endosomal sorting, the ESCRT machinery has been implicated in an ever-growing number of functions, including viral budding, cytokinesis, autophagy, extracellular vesicle release, pruning of synaptic processes and the repair and closure of holes in cellular membranes. Membrane remodelling functions are typically ascribed to the ESCRT-III subcomplex. In this Review, we discuss recent mechanistic and structural insights into how these proteins assemble and are remodelled to achieve membrane severing. We focus particularly on how ESCRT-III is engaged at different subcellular compartments during both interphase and mitosis to repair and remodel membranes.

> **中文摘要：**
> 运输所需的内体分选复合物（ESCRT）机制是一种在进化上保守的多亚基蛋白复合物，负责重塑细胞膜。除了其在内体分选中的经典作用外，ESCRT 机制还涉及越来越多的功能，包括病毒出芽、胞质分裂、自噬、细胞外囊泡释放、突触修剪以及细胞膜孔洞的修复和封闭。膜重塑功能通常归功于 ESCRT-III 亚复合物。在这篇综述中，我们讨论了关于这些蛋白质如何组装和重塑以实现膜切断的最新机制和结构见解。我们特别关注 ESCRT-III 在间期和有丝分裂期间如何参与不同亚细胞区室以修复和重塑膜。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文系统综述了 ESCRT-III 亚复合物在细胞膜重塑中的核心地位，重点探讨了其功能如何从经典的内体分选扩展至膜修复、病毒出芽及胞质分裂等前沿领域。文章整合了最新的结构生物学证据，深入解析了该复合物通过动态组装驱动膜切断的分子机制。通过对间期和有丝分裂中膜完整性维护的对比分析，本文为理解细胞膜自稳态及相关生物学过程提供了权威的理论框架。

---

## 434. 生物分子凝聚体的动态且异质的组成及其功能相关性

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41266895)
**期刊：** Nature reviews. Molecular cell biology
**PMID：** 41266895
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41580-025-00897-2

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** The dynamic and heterogeneous composition of biomolecular condensates and its functional relevance.

> **英文摘要：**
> Biomolecular condensates are non-membrane-encapsulated compartments that control various biological processes, largely by enriching and excluding certain molecules. Emerging evidence demonstrates that condensate compositions dynamically change in response to stimuli and over time. Thus, condensates that share a designation and general function can substantially vary in their composition. In this Review, we discuss the current understanding of condensate composition changes and heterogeneity, how they are regulated and how the changes affect biochemical reactions. We focus on four condensates: DNA double-strand break (DSB) repair foci, promyelocytic leukaemia (PML) nuclear bodies, processing bodies (P-bodies) and RNA transport granules, with examples from stress granules and germ granules. Changes in condensate composition seem to support complex reactions, such as those occurring in DNA repair and RNA processing. Mechanisms regulating composition changes include biophysical features of components, modifications, nodes and enzymatic reactions. We also speculate about the impact of protein mislocalization and mutations on condensate composition and function, including in cancer and neurodegenerative diseases. We conclude by discussing outstanding questions and the implications of studying condensate composition changes for research and therapeutics.

> **中文摘要：**
> 生物分子凝聚体是非膜包裹的隔室，主要通过富集和排除某些分子来控制各种生物过程。新兴证据表明，凝聚体的组成会随着刺激和时间的推移发生动态变化。因此，具有相同名称和一般功能的凝聚体，其组成可能存在显著差异。在这篇综述中，我们讨论了目前对凝聚体组成变化和异质性的理解，它们如何受调控，以及这些变化如何影响生化反应。我们重点关注四种凝聚体：DNA双链断裂 (DSB) 修复灶、早幼粒细胞白血病 (PML) 核体、加工体 (P-bodies) 和 RNA 运输颗粒，并结合应激颗粒和生殖颗粒的实例。凝聚体组成的变化似乎支持复杂的反应，例如发生在 DNA 修复和 RNA 加工中的反应。调节组成变化的机制包括组分的生物物理特征、修饰、节点和酶促反应。我们还推测了蛋白质定位错误和突变对凝聚体组成和功能的影响，包括在癌症和神经退行性疾病中的作用。最后，我们讨论了尚待解决的问题，以及研究凝聚体组成变化对科学研究和临床治疗的意义。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文深度综述了生物分子凝聚体在组成上的动态性与异质性，挑战了将其视为静态均匀结构的传统观点。文章通过剖析 DNA 修复灶和 P-bodies 等核心范例，系统阐述了生物物理特征、翻译后修饰及酶促反应对凝聚体组分的精密调控。该综述不仅揭示了组成异质性在支持复杂生化反应中的功能意义，还探讨了其在癌症和神经退行性疾病中的病理关联，为基于凝聚体异质性的药物研发提供了关键的前瞻性视角。

---

## 439. 回复 Federico Iori、Emanuele Alì 和 Cinzia Iotti 关于 Nicolas Demogeot、Paul Sargos、Julia Salleron 等人发表的《中高危局限性前列腺癌的短期雄激素剥夺疗法联合高剂量放射治疗：GETUG 14 随机 3 期试验结果》的致编辑信

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

Short-term Androgen Deprivation Therapy and High-dose Radiotherapy in Intermediate- and High-risk Localized Prostate Cancer: Results from the GETUG 14 Randomized Phase 3 Trial. Eur Urol. 88;2025:88:510-518.

## 444. 高风险膀胱癌的基因组和转录组图谱揭示了多样化的分子及微环境生态系统

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/41058365)
**期刊：** European urology
**PMID：** 41058365
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.eururo.2025.09.4138

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Genomic and Transcriptomic Profiling of High-risk Bladder Cancer Reveals Diverse Molecular and Microenvironment Ecosystems.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND AND OBJECTIVE: High-risk bladder cancer recurs in 30% of cases and causes fatal outcomes in 10% within 2 yr despite surgical resection, endoscopic surveillance, and bacillus Calmette-Guérin (BCG) immunotherapy. The global shortage of BCG highlights the urgent need for alternative or complementary strategies. This study aimed to identify molecular subtypes and develop a precision framework to predict recurrence risk and guide treatment. METHODS: Transcriptomic profiling and targeted genomic sequencing were performed with validation by single-cell RNA sequencing and spatial transcriptomics. A machine learning model incorporating genomic and transcriptomic features was developed to predict recurrence risk. KEY FINDINGS AND LIMITATIONS: Four subtypes were identified, and an inflamed tumor subtype with high endogenous retroelement expression and increased commensal bacterial presence demonstrated the highest responsiveness to BCG therapy. The predictive model achieved high accuracy (area under the curve = 0.87, 95% confidence interval: 0.72-1.0) for recurrence risk. Findings are limited by sample size, necessitating validation in larger cohorts. CONCLUSIONS AND CLINICAL IMPLICATIONS: We describe a new conceptual framework for T1 tumors. Those with increased immune cells (subtype 2) have a better response to BCG, which may be secondary to enhanced baseline immune activity.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景与目的：尽管进行了手术切除、内镜监测和卡介苗（BCG）免疫治疗，高风险膀胱癌仍有30%的病例会复发，并在2年内导致10%的致命后果。全球BCG短缺凸显了对替代或补充策略的迫切需求。本研究旨在鉴定分子亚型，并开发一种精准框架以预测复发风险并指导治疗。方法：进行了转录组分析和针对性基因组测序，并通过单细胞RNA测序和空间转录组学进行验证。开发了一个结合基因组和转录组特征的机器学习模型来预测复发风险。主要发现与局限性：鉴定了四种亚型，其中一种具有高内源性逆转录元件表达和共生细菌增多特征的炎症型肿瘤亚型表现出对BCG治疗最高的反应性。该预测模型在复发风险预测方面达到了极高的准确度（曲线下面积 = 0.87，95%置信区间：0.72-1.0）。研究结果受限于样本量，需要在更大规模的队列中进行验证。结论与临床意义：我们描述了一种针对T1期肿瘤的新概念框架。具有免疫细胞增加特征的肿瘤（亚型2）对BCG有更好的反应，这可能继发于增强的基础免疫活性。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究通过整合多组学测序与机器学习算法，深入解析了高风险膀胱癌的分子异质性与微环境生态。研究核心创新点在于识别出一种与BCG疗效密切相关的特定炎症亚型，并揭示了内源性逆转录元件和共生菌群对免疫微环境的影响。所构建的预测模型在复发风险分层上展现了优异的性能，为T1期肿瘤的精准治疗提供了重要的分子生物学依据，尽管其临床应用仍需更大样本量的多中心验证。

## 446. 良性前列腺梗阻微创手术治疗（MISTs）功能与性功能结果的系统评价及汇总分析

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/40967932)
**期刊：** European urology
**PMID：** 40967932
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.eururo.2025.09.004

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Systematic Review and Pooled Analysis of Functional and Sexual Outcomes of Minimally Invasive Surgical Treatments for Benign Prostatic Obstruction.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND AND OBJECTIVE: Minimally invasive surgical treatments (MISTs) for benign prostatic obstruction have been developed with the aim of providing superior symptom relief in comparison to pharmacological treatment, while minimizing the impact on sexual function. The aim of our study was to assess key MIST outcomes and to propose a definition of procedural success. METHODS: A systematic literature search was conducted in February 2025 in the PubMed, Scopus, Web of Science, and Cochrane Library databases. The protocol, which follows the PRISMA (Preferred Reporting Items for Systematic Reviews and Meta-Analyses) guidelines and PICOS (Population, Intervention, Comparator, Outcomes, Study design) criteria, was registered on PROSPERO as CRD42024543361. The review focused on randomized controlled trials and prospective studies evaluating surgical and functional outcomes of MISTs (Rezūm, UroLift, temporary implantable nitinol device [iTind], transperineal laser ablation [TPLA], Optilume) for BPO. We assessed the risk of bias and graded the certainty of evidence from the articles included. Pooled analyses were performed to compare perioperative and functional outcomes between study groups. KEY FINDINGS AND LIMITATIONS: The 24 studies included in the review found that most MISTs were effective, showing improvements at 12 mo of ≥50% in the International Prostate Symptom Score (IPSS) and maximum flow rate (Qmax), and of ≥1 point for at quality of life (QoL) questionnaire. Anejaculation rates were 5% with TPLA, 3% with Rezūm, 1% with iTIND, and 0% with UroLift and Optilume. Complication and retreatment rates were low, although the follow-up duration was inconsistently reported and mainly limited to 24 mo. On the basis of these results, we propose a definition of procedural success that comprises achievement of all the following outcomes: IPSS reduction of ≥50%, Qmax improvement of ≥50%, QoL improvement of ≥50% (or ≥1 point), the absence of intraoperative complications and Clavien-Dindo grade ≥III postoperative complications, and preservation of erectile function and of antegrade ejaculation. CONCLUSIONS AND CLINICAL IMPLICATIONS: MISTs represent a promising tool for benign prostatic obstruction management and provide effective symptom relief while preserving sexual function.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景与目的：针对良性前列腺梗阻（BPO）的微创手术治疗（MISTs）旨在提供优于药物治疗的症状缓解，同时最大限度地减少对性功能的影响。本研究旨在评估MISTs的关键结局，并提出手术成功的定义。方法：2025年2月在PubMed、Scopus、Web of Science和Cochrane Library数据库中进行了系统文献检索。方案遵循PRISMA（系统评价和荟萃分析首选报告项目）指南和PICOS（人群、干预、对照、结局、研究设计）标准，并在PROSPERO注册为CRD42024543361。本综述侧重于评估用于BPO的MISTs（Rezūm、UroLift、暂时性植入式镍钛合金装置[iTind]、经会阴激光消融术[TPLA]、Optilume）的手术和功能结局的随机对照试验和前瞻性研究。我们评估了偏倚风险，并对纳入文章的证据确定性进行了分级。进行了汇总分析，以比较各研究组之间的围手术期和功能结局。关键发现与局限性：综述纳入的24项研究发现，大多数MISTs是有效的，在12个月时国际前列腺症状评分（IPSS）和最大尿流率（Qmax）均改善≥50%，且生活质量（QoL）问卷改善≥1分。不射精率在TPLA中为5%，Rezūm为3%，iTIND为1%，UroLift和Optilume为0%。并发症率和再治疗率较低，但随访时间报告不一，主要限制在24个月内。基于这些结果，我们提出了手术成功的定义，包括达到以下所有结果：IPSS降低≥50%，Qmax改善≥50%，QoL改善≥50%（或≥1分），无术中并发症及Clavien-Dindo ≥III级术后并发症，以及保留勃起功能和顺行射精。结论与临床意义：MISTs是良性前列腺梗阻管理的有前景的工具，在提供有效症状缓解的同时保留了性功能。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该系统综述和汇总分析全面评估了多种微创手术治疗（MISTs）在良性前列腺梗阻中的应用。研究证实了Rezūm、UroLift、TPLA等技术在显著缓解症状（IPSS和Qmax改善≥50%）的同时，对性功能具有极佳的保护作用，特别是顺行射精的保留率极高。其核心贡献在于整合多项临床结局指标，提出了一个涵盖疗效、安全性和性功能保护的“手术成功”标准化定义。尽管存在随访时间多限于24个月的局限性，该研究仍为临床医师评价新兴微创技术提供了重要的量化基准和循证依据。

---

## 448. 小分子在细胞内的高特异性泛素化

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/40841494)
**期刊：** Nature chemical biology
**PMID：** 40841494
**DOI：** 10.1038/s41589-025-02011-1

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Highly specific intracellular ubiquitination of a small molecule.

> **英文摘要：**
> Ubiquitin is a small, highly conserved protein that acts as a posttranslational modification in eukaryotes. Ubiquitination of proteins frequently serves as a degradation signal, marking them for disposal by the proteasome. Here we report a novel small molecule from a diversity-oriented synthesis library, BRD1732, that is directly ubiquitinated in cells, resulting in dramatic accumulation of inactive ubiquitin monomers and polyubiquitin chains, which causes broad inhibition of the ubiquitin-proteasome system. Ubiquitination of BRD1732 and its associated cytotoxicity are stereospecific and dependent on two homologous E3 ubiquitin ligases, RNF19A and RNF19B, and their shared E2 conjugating enzyme, UBE2L3. Our finding opens the possibility for indirect ubiquitination of a target through a ubiquitinated bifunctional small molecule and more broadly raises the potential for posttranslational modification in trans.

> **中文摘要：**
> 泛素是一种小型且高度保守的蛋白质，在真核生物中作为一种翻译后修饰发挥作用。蛋白质的泛素化通常作为降解信号，标记它们由蛋白酶体进行处理。在此，我们报道了一种来自多样性导向合成库的新型小分子 BRD1732，它在细胞内被直接泛素化，导致失活的泛素单体和多泛素链剧烈积累，从而引发对泛素-蛋白酶体系统的广泛抑制。BRD1732 的泛素化及其相关的细胞毒性具有立体特异性，并依赖于两种同源的 E3 泛素连接酶 RNF19A 和 RNF19B，以及它们共有的 E2 结合酶 UBE2L3。我们的发现开启了通过泛素化双功能小分子对靶标进行间接泛素化的可能性，并更广泛地提升了跨分子翻译后修饰的潜力。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该研究通过多样性导向合成筛选，首次发现并证实了小分子 BRD1732 能够作为直接底物发生胞内泛素化，挑战了泛素化仅修饰蛋白质的传统认知。研究明确了该反应由 E3 连接酶 RNF19A/B 和 E2 结合酶 UBE2L3 介导，并因泛素库耗竭导致蛋白酶体系统失能。这一发现不仅揭示了泛素化系统的新型生物化学机制，也为开发基于双功能小分子的新型靶向降解技术奠定了重要理论基础。

---

## 449. 循环肿瘤DNA中的致病性基因组改变预测转移性去势抵抗性前列腺癌男性的总生存期

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/40774853)
**期刊：** European urology
**PMID：** 40774853
**DOI：** 10.1016/j.eururo.2025.07.011

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Pathogenic Genomic Alterations in Circulating Tumor DNA Predict Overall Survival in Men with Metastatic Castrate-resistant Prostate Cancer.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND AND OBJECTIVE: Although validated prognostic models exist for men with metastatic castration-resistant prostate cancer (mCRPC), current tools do not incorporate genomic biomarkers such as circulating tumor DNA (ctDNA) aneuploidy or pathogenic genetic alterations (PGAs). This study aimed to estimate the prevalence of PGAs in ctDNA, assess their correlation with ctDNA aneuploidy fraction, and evaluate their association with overall survival (OS). Additionally, we developed and validated a clinical-genetic (CG) model to predict OS. METHODS: We analyzed ctDNA from 776 patients enrolled in the Alliance phase 3 trial (A031201). PGAs were derived using the AR-ctDETECT assay. The net reclassification improvement (NRI) evaluated the added value of the CG model, and the time-dependent area under the receiver operating characteristic curve (tAUC) assessed the accuracy of the OS model. KEY FINDINGS AND LIMITATIONS: Feature selection using random survival forest identified gains in androgen receptor (AR), AR enhancer, MYC, RSPO2, CCND1, BRAF, and MET; losses or pathogenic variants in ZBTB16, PTEN, MSH6, PPP2R2A, NKX3-1, ZFHX3, TP53, ZNFR3, RB1, FANCA, CHECK1, APC, and CHD1; and a pathogenic AR variant. The CG model significantly outperformed the clinical model, with an average tAUC of 0.77 (95% confidence interval [CI]: 0.73-0.79) for the CG model compared with the tAUC of 0.72 (95% CI: 0.69-0.75, p = 0.01) for the clinical model, and NRI of 0.29 between the models. Patients were categorized by the predicted risk scores into poor-, intermediate-, and low-risk groups with median OS of 19.6, 33.6, and 60.8 mo, respectively. CONCLUSIONS AND CLINICAL IMPLICATIONS: Incorporation of PGAs from ctDNA into a CG model improved OS prediction by nearly 30% over a clinical model. This model can classify patients into risk groups and is useful for selecting patients in future mCRPC trials.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景与目标：尽管针对转移性去势抵抗性前列腺癌（mCRPC）男性患者已存在经过验证的预后模型，但目前的工具尚未纳入基因组生物标志物，如循环肿瘤DNA（ctDNA）非整倍体或致病性遗传改变（PGAs）。本研究旨在估算ctDNA中PGAs的流行率，评估其与ctDNA非整倍体分数的评估，并评价其与总生存期（OS）的相关性。此外，我们开发并验证了一个临床-遗传（CG）模型来预测OS。方法：我们分析了参加Alliance 3期试验（A031201）的776名患者的ctDNA。通过AR-ctDETECT检测法获取PGAs。使用净重新分类改进指数（NRI）评估CG模型的附加价值，并使用随时间变化的受试者工作特征曲线下面积（tAUC）评估OS模型的准确性。主要发现与局限性：通过随机生存森林进行的特征选择识别出了雄激素受体（AR）、AR增强子、MYC、RSPO2、CCND1、BRAF和MET的获得；ZBTB16、PTEN、MSH6、PPP2R2A、NKX3-1、ZFHX3、TP53、ZNFR3、RB1、FANCA、CHECK1、APC和CHD1的缺失或致病性变异；以及一种致病性AR变异。CG模型表现显著优于临床模型，CG模型的平均tAUC为0.77（95%置信区间[CI]：0.73-0.79），而临床模型的tAUC为0.72（95% CI：0.69-0.75，p = 0.01），两模型间的NRI为0.29。根据预测的风险评分，患者被分为高危、中危和低危组，其中位OS分别为19.6、33.6和60.8个月。结论与临床意义：将ctDNA中的PGAs整合入CG模型后，对OS的预测能力比临床模型提高了近30%。该模型可以将患者分类至不同的风险组，对于未来mCRPC试验中的患者筛选非常有用。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究基于Alliance A031201三期临床试验的大样本数据，成功将ctDNA中的致病性遗传改变（PGAs）整合入传统的预后预测工具中。该临床-遗传（CG）模型在预测mCRPC患者总生存期（OS）方面的准确性显著优于单纯的临床模型，预测能力提升了约30%，并能有效地将患者划分为不同风险等级。尽管存在液体活检技术本身的局限性，该研究仍为mCRPC的精准风险评估和未来临床试验的患者入组提供了强有力的生物标志物支持。

## 450. 肝细胞特异性C-C基序趋化因子配体9信号转导促进小鼠肝纤维化的进展

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/40359088)
**期刊：** Hepatology (Baltimore, Md.)
**PMID：** 40359088
**DOI：** 10.1097/HEP.0000000000001393

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Hepatocyte-specific C-C motif chemokine ligand 9 signaling promotes liver fibrosis progression in mice.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND AND AIMS: Liver fibrosis involves the activation of HSCs and persistent inflammatory responses. Ccl9, a CC chemokine implicated in inflammation, has an undefined role in liver homeostasis. Our study investigates this murine homolog of human CCL15 to elucidate its role in the development of liver fibrosis. APPROACH AND RESULTS: We investigated the expression of Ccl9 and its upstream regulatory elements in liver fibrosis using mouse models induced by carbon tetrachloride (CCl 4 ), bile-duct ligation, and a high-fat, methionine-deficient and choline-deficient diet. A significant increase in Ccl9 expression was observed in fibrotic liver tissues, predominantly in damaged hepatocytes, with Myc identified as a key driver of this upregulation. The role of Ccl9 was further elucidated through hepatocyte-specific knockout mice, neutralizing antibodies, and in vitro analyses of HSCs and macrophages. Targeted deletion of Ccl9 in hepatocytes mitigated liver fibrosis and injury across multiple models, characterized by reduced inflammation and decreased monocyte/macrophage and neutrophil infiltration. Additionally, neutralizing Ccl9 in CCl 4 -induced models reduced both fibrosis and liver damage. Mechanistically, Ccl9 modulated macrophage infiltration, promoted M1 polarization, and regulated inflammatory cytokine responses through the Ccr1 receptor in models of hepatic injury induced by CCl 4 and bile-duct ligation. Furthermore, Ccl9 directly activated HSCs by recruiting Myh9 via Ccr1, thereby enhancing the Wnt signaling pathway through Myh9-mediated Gsk3β ubiquitination. CONCLUSIONS: Ccl9 is a significant contributor to liver fibrosis, influencing macrophage behavior and directly activating HSCs. Targeting Ccl9 offers a potential therapeutic approach for treating liver fibrosis.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景与目的：肝纤维化涉及肝星状细胞（HSCs）的激活和持续的炎症反应。Ccl9是一种参与炎症的CC趋化因子，其在肝脏稳态中的作用尚不明确。本研究旨在调查这种人类CCL15的小鼠同源物，以阐明其在肝纤维化发展中的作用。
> 
> 方法与结果：我们利用四氯化碳（CCl4）、胆管结扎以及高脂、甲硫氨酸和胆碱缺乏饮食诱导的小鼠模型，研究了Ccl9及其上游调节元件在肝纤维化中的表达。在纤维化肝组织中观察到Ccl9表达显著增加，主要集中在受损的肝细胞中，并确定Myc是这一上调的关键驱动因素。通过肝细胞特异性敲除小鼠、中和抗体以及对HSCs和巨噬细胞的体外分析，进一步阐明了Ccl9的作用。在多种模型中，肝细胞中Ccl9的靶向缺失减轻了肝纤维化和损伤，其特征是炎症减轻以及单核细胞/巨噬细胞和中性粒细胞浸润减少。此外，在CCl4诱导的模型中中和Ccl9可减轻纤维化和肝损伤。从机制上讲，在CCl4和胆管结扎诱导的肝损伤模型中，Ccl9通过Ccr1受体调节巨噬细胞浸润，促进M1型极化，并调节炎症细胞因子反应。此外，Ccl9通过Ccr1招募Myh9直接激活HSCs，从而通过Myh9介导的Gsk3β泛素化增强Wnt信号通路。
> 
> 结论：Ccl9是肝纤维化的重要贡献者，它通过影响巨噬细胞行为并直接激活HSCs发挥作用。靶向Ccl9为治疗肝纤维化提供了一种潜在的治疗途径。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该研究系统地揭示了趋化因子Ccl9在肝纤维化进展中的致病机制。研究者通过多种小鼠模型证实，Myc驱动的肝细胞特异性Ccl9通过Ccr1受体发挥双重作用：一方面促进巨噬细胞向M1型极化以增强炎症反应，另一方面通过招募Myh9介导Gsk3β泛素化，进而激活Wnt通路直接驱动肝星状细胞活化。该研究不仅明确了人类CCL15的小鼠同源物功能，还为开发针对肝纤维化的新型免疫治疗策略提供了坚实的实验依据。

## 451. GPD1L支持甘油-3-磷酸和三酰甘油合成并促进肝细胞癌（HCC）的肿瘤进展

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/40344414)
**期刊：** Hepatology (Baltimore, Md.)
**PMID：** 40344414
**DOI：** 10.1097/HEP.0000000000001394

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** GPD1L supports glycerol-3-phosphate and triacylglycerol synthesis and promotes tumor progression in HCC.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND AND AIMS: Research on metabolic reprogramming in HCC has increased; however, studies on the metabolism of glycerolipids or interactions between different pathways remain scarce. Enzymes of the glycerol phosphate dehydrogenase (GPD) family, which regulate the glycerol-3-phosphate shuttle, link the metabolic processes of glycolysis and glycerolipids. Therefore, we aimed to understand the role and regulation of GPDs in HCC.
> 
> APPROACH AND RESULTS: We performed transcriptomic analysis on clinical HCC samples from in-house and public cohorts and detected the upregulation of glycerol-3-phosphate dehydrogenase 1-like (GPD1L) among GPD family genes in HCC. Further analysis showed that high GPD1L expression was associated with more frequent venous invasion and shorter overall survival. Consistent with these clinical findings, GPD1L knockdown suppressed the invasiveness of HCC cells, reduced colony- and sphere-forming abilities, and inhibited stemness gene expression in vitro, while also inhibiting tumor growth and metastasis in vivo. On the other hand, we used mass-spectrometry-based metabolomics to confirm that GPD1L facilitated the biogenesis of the glycerolipid precursor glycerol-3-phosphate (G3P) from dihydroxyacetone phosphate (DHAP). Further untargeted lipidomic analysis revealed that GPD1L supported triacylglycerol synthesis. In addition, our study identified E74-like E-Twenty-Six transcription factor 1 (ELF1) as a direct activator of GPD1L transcription, binding to the GPD1L promoter to boost its transcription while reducing GPD1L expression when ELF1 levels were lowered.
> 
> CONCLUSIONS: GPD1L is overexpressed in human HCCs and is associated with worse clinical outcomes. Aberrant GPD1L expression, driven by ELF1, facilitates conversion of DHAP to G3P to support triacylglycerol synthesis in HCC, promoting tumor growth and metastasis.

> **中文摘要：**
> 【背景与目的】关于肝细胞癌（HCC）代谢重编程的研究日益增多；然而，关于甘油磷脂代谢或不同通路间相互作用的研究仍然较少。调节甘油-3-磷酸穿梭的甘油磷酸脱氢酶（GPD）家族酶将糖酵解和甘油磷脂的代谢过程联系起来。因此，我们旨在了解GPD在HCC中的作用及其调节机制。
> 
> 【方法与结果】我们对来自内部和公共队列的临床HCC样本进行了转录组分析，并检测到HCC中GPD家族基因中甘油-3-磷酸脱氢酶1样蛋白（GPD1L）的上调。进一步分析显示，GPD1L的高表达与更频繁的静脉侵犯和更短的总生存期相关。与这些临床发现一致，GPD1L敲低在体外抑制了HCC细胞的侵袭性，降低了集落和成球能力，并抑制了干性基因的表达，同时在体内也抑制了肿瘤的生长和转移。另一方面，我们利用基于质谱的代谢组学证实，GPD1L促进了甘油磷脂前体甘油-3-磷酸（G3P）从磷酸二羟丙酮（DHAP）的生物合成。进一步的非靶向脂质组学分析显示，GPD1L支持三酰甘油的合成。此外，我们的研究确定了E74样E-Twenty-Six转录因子1（ELF1）是GPD1L转录的直接激活因子，它结合GPD1L启动子以增强其转录，而当ELF1水平降低时，GPD1L的表达也随之降低。
> 
> 【结论】GPD1L在人类HCC中过度表达，并与较差的临床预后相关。由ELF1驱动的GPD1L异常表达促进了DHAP向G3P的转化，从而支持HCC中的三酰甘油合成，促进肿瘤生长和转移。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究深入探讨了甘油磷脂代谢通路在肝细胞癌（HCC）进展中的关键作用，首次确定了GPD1L作为连接糖酵解与脂质代谢的核心节点。通过整合临床转录组、代谢组学和脂质组学分析，研究揭示了ELF1驱动的GPD1L上调通过促进甘油-3-磷酸（G3P）和三酰甘油（TAG）的生物合成，显著增强了肿瘤的侵袭性、干性及转移能力。该发现不仅完善了HCC代谢重编程的调控网络，也为开发针对甘油磷脂代谢通路的抗癌疗法提供了新的分子靶点，具有较高的临床转化潜力和学术参考价值。

---

## 452. 酒精诱导的肝脏 m6A 修饰破坏通过损害肝脏免疫微环境稳态加重酒精性脂肪性肝炎

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/40304707)
**期刊：** Hepatology (Baltimore, Md.)
**PMID：** 40304707
**DOI：** 10.1097/HEP.0000000000001374

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Alcohol-induced disruption of hepatic m 6 A modification exacerbates alcohol-associated steatohepatitis by impairing liver immune microenvironment homeostasis.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND AND AIMS: Alcohol-associated steatohepatitis (ASH), a severe form of alcohol-associated liver disease, is characterized by pronounced steatosis and immune cell infiltration. As an inflammatory disease, ASH still lacks effective immunotherapies, and the mechanisms underlying alcohol-induced immune imbalance in the liver microenvironment remain elusive. RNA modifications are known to maintain hepatic homeostasis during physiological and pathological processes. This study aimed to investigate the alteration of RNA modification in ASH and its specific roles in regulating immune homeostasis.
> 
> APPROACH AND RESULTS: In this study, we found that the levels of RNA N 6 -methyladenosine (m 6 A) modification and its key writer, methyltransferase-like 3 (METTL3), are markedly reduced in mice livers during ASH. Notably, hepatocyte-specific Mettl3 knockout exacerbated ASH by enhancing steatosis and neutrophil infiltration, whereas hepatocyte-specific Mettl3 overexpression alleviated these effects. Mechanistically, ethanol promotes METTL3 degradation via E3 ubiquitin ligase STUB1-mediated ubiquitination and disrupts the protective interaction between HSP70 and METTL3, impairing hepatic m 6 A modification. Furthermore, the expression of ATF3 was upregulated via an m 6 A-dependent mechanism. Importantly, hepatocyte-specific Atf3 overexpression abolished METTL3-mediated amelioration of ASH, whereas hepatocyte-specific Atf3 knockdown attenuated Mettl3 knockout-induced exacerbation of ASH in vivo. Consistently, high hepatic ATF3 expression is associated with an inflammatory liver microenvironment in patients with alcohol-associated liver disease.
> 
> CONCLUSIONS: Collectively, our results demonstrate that alcohol consumption disrupts the homeostasis of hepatic immune microenvironment in ASH through impairment of METTL3-dependent m 6 A RNA modification. Targeting METTL3 to preserve its enzymatic activity and stability could represent a novel therapeutic avenue for ASH intervention.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景与目的：酒精性脂肪性肝炎（ASH）是酒精性肝病的一种严重形式，其特征是显著的脂肪变性和免疫细胞浸润。作为一种炎症性疾病，ASH 仍缺乏有效的免疫疗法，且酒精诱导肝脏微环境免疫失衡的潜在机制尚不清楚。已知 RNA 修饰在生理和病理过程中维持肝脏稳态。本研究旨在探讨 ASH 中 RNA 修饰的变化及其在调节免疫稳态中的具体作用。
> 
> 研究方法与结果：在本研究中，我们发现 ASH 小鼠肝脏中 RNA N6-甲基腺苷（m6A）修饰及其关键写入酶甲基转移酶样 3（METTL3）的水平显著降低。值得注意的是，肝细胞特异性 Mettl3 敲除通过增强脂肪变性和中性粒细胞浸润加重了 ASH，而肝细胞特异性 Mettl3 过表达则减轻了这些效应。机制上，乙醇通过 E3 泛素连接酶 STUB1 介导的泛素化促进 METTL3 降解，并破坏了 HSP70 与 METTL3 之间的保护性相互作用，从而损伤了肝脏 m6A 修饰。此外，ATF3 的表达通过 m6A 依赖性机制上调。重要的是，肝细胞特异性 Atf3 过表达消除了 METTL3 介导的 ASH 缓解作用，而在体内，肝细胞特异性 Atf3 敲低则减轻了 Mettl3 敲除诱导的 ASH 加重。一致地，酒精性肝病患者的高肝脏 ATF3 表达与炎症性肝脏微环境相关。
> 
> 结论：总之，我们的研究结果表明，饮酒通过损害 METTL3 依赖性 m6A RNA 修饰，破坏了 ASH 中肝脏免疫微环境的稳态。以 METTL3 为靶点以维持其酶活性和稳定性可能成为 ASH 干预的一种新型治疗途径。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究揭示了酒精通过促进 E3 泛素连接酶 STUB1 介导的 METTL3 降解，进而破坏 m6A 修饰并上调 ATF3 表达，最终失衡肝脏免疫微环境并加重 ASH 的分子机制。通过肝细胞特异性基因敲除和过表达模型，研究严谨地论证了 METTL3/m6A/ATF3 信号轴在 ASH 免疫病理中的核心作用。该发现不仅为理解酒精诱导的肝损伤提供了表观转录组学的新视角，还提出了稳定 METTL3 作为 ASH 临床干预的潜在新策略，具有较强的学术创新性和潜在的转化应用价值。

## 453. 一项比较开腹、腹腔镜、机器人辅助及经肛全直肠系膜切除术治疗高危直肠癌患者的前瞻性欧洲试验：RESET研究

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/39263755)
**期刊：** Annals of surgery
**PMID：** 39263755
**DOI：** 10.1097/SLA.0000000000006534

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** A Prospective European Trial Comparing Laparotomy, Laparoscopy, Robotic-assisted, and Transanal Total Mesorectal Excision Procedures in High-risk Patients With Rectal Cancer: The RESET Trial.

> **英文摘要：**
> OBJECTIVE: To compare total mesorectal excision (TME) techniques combined with sphincter-sparing procedures in high-risk patients (HRPs). BACKGROUND: TME is the standard treatment for rectal cancer, but it can be challenging in HRPs. The available surgical approaches must be compared, especially in HRPs. METHODS: Prospective, observational, multicenter trial to compare laparotomy (OTME), laparoscopy (LTME), robotic-assisted surgery (RTME), and transanal surgery (TaTME) in HRPs. The composite primary outcome included circumferential radial margin (CRM) ≥1 mm, TME grade II-III, and absence of Clavien-Dindo grade III-IV complications. Three propensity score analyses were performed (LTME vs RTME, RTME vs TaTME, LTME vs TaTME). RESULTS: A total of 1078 HRPs (75% of men, median body mass index of 27 kg/m 2 , 50% of tumors in the lower third of the rectum) underwent surgery. The RTME and TaTME groups included patients with more advanced and lower tumors and coloanal anastomosis ( P <0.001). Operative time was longer for RTME surgery ( P <0.001). The conversion rate was similar for minimally invasive procedures (4.5%). The global R0 resection rate was 96% without difference among techniques. The primary outcome rates were 82.4%, 64.3%, 74.7%, and 80.3% for LTME, OTME, RTME, and TaTME, respectively. None achieved the expected success rate (85%), and propensity score analyses found no differences. Operative results were similar between high-volume and low-volume inclusion centers only for RTME. CONCLUSIONS: The RESET trial yielded high-quality results despite focusing on HRPs. Minimally invasive procedures showed similar sphincter-sparing procedure outcomes, but LTME included patients with more favorable tumors. Oncologic and functional outcomes will be evaluated at 2 years (ClinicalTrials.gov, ID: NCT03574493).

> **中文摘要：**
> 目的：旨在比较高危患者（HRPs）中全直肠系膜切除术（TME）技术结合保留括约肌手术的效果。背景：TME是直肠癌的标准治疗方法，但在高危患者中实施具有挑战性。必须对现有的手术入路进行比较，特别是在高危患者群体中。方法：这项前瞻性、观察性、多中心试验比较了高危患者中的开腹手术（OTME）、腹腔镜手术（LTME）、机器人辅助手术（RTME）和经肛门手术（TaTME）。复合主要结局指标包括：环周切缘（CRM）≥1 mm、TME质量达到II-III级，且无Clavien-Dindo III-IV级并发症。研究进行了三项倾向评分分析（LTME对比RTME，RTME对比TaTME，LTME对比TaTME）。结果：共1078名高危患者（男性占75%，中位体重指数为27 kg/m²，50%的肿瘤位于直肠下1/3）接受了手术。RTME和TaTME组包含更多晚期、低位肿瘤以及进行结直肠肛管吻合的患者（P < 0.001）。RTME手术的操作时间较长（P < 0.001）。微创手术的中转率相似（4.5%）。总体R0切除率为96%，不同技术间无差异。LTME、OTME、RTME和TaTME的主要结局率分别为82.4%、64.3%、74.7%和80.3%。没有任何一种入路达到预期的成功率（85%），且倾向评分分析未发现显著差异。仅在RTME中，高手术量中心与低手术量中心的手术结果相似。结论：尽管RESET试验聚焦于高危患者，但仍取得了高质量的结果。微创手术在保留括约肌手术结局方面表现相似，但LTME组纳入的患者肿瘤条件更优。肿瘤学和功能性结局将在2年后进行评估（ClinicalTrials.gov ID: NCT03574493）。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

RESET研究是针对高危直肠癌群体开展的一项重要前瞻性多中心试验，其核心价值在于直接对比了目前临床主流的四种TME手术入路。研究发现，尽管RTME和TaTME应对的病例更为复杂，但其在R0切除率和中转率上与LTME表现相当，展现了良好的手术安全性与根治性。此外，RTME在不同手术量中心表现出的结果一致性，提示其学习曲线和技术推广具有优势。虽然主要结局受限于病例难度未达预设目标，但该研究为复杂直肠癌患者的术式选择提供了关键的循证医学参考。

---

## 454. 姜黄素辅助多光子激光成像在先天性巨结肠症肠神经网络动态病理中的应用

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/39263745)
**期刊：** Annals of surgery
**PMID：** 39263745
**DOI：** 10.1097/SLA.0000000000006528

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Dynamic Pathology of Enteric Neural Network Using Curcumin-assisted Multiphoton Laser Imaging in Hirschsprung Disease.

> **英文摘要：**
> BACKGROUND: In living tissue, it has been difficult to make microscopic-level observations without damaging the tissue. We have invented a novel intravital fluorescent observation method (IFOM) for real-time tissue observation, combining multiphoton laser scanning microscopy with curcumin vital staining (CVS-IFOM). The aim of this study was to use CVS-IFOM to analyze the enteric nervous system (ENS) in mice and human patients with hypoganglionosis and Hirschsprung disease (HSCR).
> 
> METHODS: In an initial viability study, we compared live ENS images from nonfluorescent C57BL6 mice stained with curcumin (n = 5) and green fluorescent protein mice (n = 5) using multiphoton laser scanning microscopy. We then explored CVS-IFOM for the live examination of resected colon tissues from 1 patient with hypoganglionosis and 3 patients with HSCR.
> 
> RESULTS: In the viability study, detailed ENS histologic features were only observed in the curcumin-stained mice. In the patient with hypoganglionosis, CVS-IFOM provided ENS details that were not visualized under hematoxylin and eosin staining or calretinin immunohistochemistry, allowing the analysis of ENS size, neural bundle number, and neural cell number per plexus. In patients with HSCR, CVS-IFOM showed a gradual hypoplastic change in the ENS from the oral edge to the anal edge, detecting disproportionate changes in the ENS within the same intestinal level, supporting a circumferentially uneven distribution of the intestinal ENS.
> 
> CONCLUSIONS: CVS-IFOM may be supportive for intraoperative pathologic diagnosis during surgeries for HSCR.

> **中文摘要：**
> 背景：在活体组织中，很难在不损伤组织的情况下进行显微水平的观察。我们发明了一种用于实时组织观察的新型活体荧光观察方法（IFOM），该方法结合了多光子激光扫描显微技术与姜黄素活体染色（CVS-IFOM）。本研究旨在利用 CVS-IFOM 分析小鼠以及神经节细胞减退症和先天性巨结肠症（HSCR）患者的肠神经系统（ENS）。
> 
> 方法：在一项初步的生存力研究中，我们利用多光子激光扫描显微镜比较了姜黄素染色（n = 5）的非荧光 C57BL6 小鼠与绿色荧光蛋白（GFP）小鼠（n = 5）的活体 ENS 图像。随后，我们探索了 CVS-IFOM 在 1 例神经节细胞减退症患者和 3 例 HSCR 患者切除的结肠组织活体检查中的应用。
> 
> 结果：在生存力研究中，仅在姜黄素染色的小鼠中观察到了详细的 ENS 组织学特征。在神经节细胞减退症患者中，CVS-IFOM 提供了苏木精-伊红（H&E）染色或钙结合蛋白（calretinin）免疫组化无法显示的 ENS 细节，从而实现了对每个神经丛的 ENS 大小、神经束数量和神经细胞数量的分析。在 HSCR 患者中，CVS-IFOM 显示了 ENS 从口侧到肛侧的逐渐发育不良变化，并检测到同一肠段水平内 ENS 的不成比例变化，证实了肠道 ENS 在圆周分布上的不均匀性。
> 
> 结论：CVS-IFOM 可能为 HSCR 手术中的术中病理诊断提供支持。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究开发并验证了一种创新的活体成像技术（CVS-IFOM），通过姜黄素染色与多光子激光扫描显微镜的结合，实现了对肠神经系统（ENS）的高分辨率动态观察。该技术不仅在动物模型中表现优于传统的荧光标记方法，更在临床样本中展示了其识别神经节细胞减退及ENS圆周分布不均等微细病理特征的能力。其核心创新点在于能够在不破坏组织的情况下提供比传统H&E染色和免疫组化更详尽的术中解剖细节。虽然样本量有限，但其在辅助先天性巨结肠症术中精准诊断和确定切除边界方面具有极高的临床应用潜力价值。

---

## 455. 旨在明确直肠恶性肿瘤患者造口周围皮肤疾病发生频率及适宜评估时间的前瞻性多中心研究

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/39239714)
**期刊：** Annals of surgery
**PMID：** 39239714
**DOI：** 10.1097/SLA.0000000000006522

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Prospective Multicenter Study to Clarify the Frequency of Peristomal Skin Disorders and Appropriate Evaluation Time in Patients With Malignant Rectal Tumors.

> **英文摘要：**
> OBJECTIVE: This study aimed to understand the effectiveness of regular care in reducing the incidence of severe peristomal skin disorders, as well as to identify their risk factors. BACKGROUND: Peristomal skin disorders occur frequently in outpatient settings and require appropriate intervention. It remains, however, to be demonstrated when the need to follow up these patients decreases and whether assessing severity of peristomal skin disorders is useful. METHODS: This prospective, multicenter, observational cohort study was conducted in 6 regional high-volume Japanese hospitals. The primary endpoint of the study was the effectiveness of regular follow-up in reducing the incidence of severe peristomal skin disorders via a scoring system at a defined regular outpatient visit. Propensity score matching was performed to compare a control group and patients with severe peristomal skin disorders. RESULTS: In total, 217 patients between December 2019 and December 2021 were enrolled, and 191 patients were analyzed. Multivariate analysis showed that loop stoma (odds ratio, 5.017; 95% CI: 1.350-18.639; P =0.016) and stoma height of <10 mm (odds ratio, 7.831; 95% CI: 1.760-34.838; P =0.007) were independent risk factors for all peristomal skin disorders. After propensity score matching, the incidence of the disorders was not significantly different between the specified evaluation timing and historical control groups (75.7% vs 77.2%, P =0.775), and the incidence of the severe disorders based on the ABCD and DET scores (5.9% vs 19.1%, P <0.001 and 1.5% vs 29.4%, P <0.001, respectively) was significantly lower in the specified evaluation timing group than in the historical control group. CONCLUSIONS: Regular peristomal skin disease follow-up and scoring, as well as appropriate stoma care at the stoma outpatient visit, did not change the frequency of peristomal skin disease, but severe peristomal skin disorders were prevented. In addition, risk factors for peristomal skin disorders were found to be height <10 mm and loop stoma.

> **中文摘要：**
> 【目的】本研究旨在了解定期护理在降低严重造口周围皮肤疾病发生率方面的有效性，并识别其危险因素。【背景】造口周围皮肤疾病在门诊环境中频繁发生，需要适当的干预。然而，何时可以减少对这些患者的随访需求，以及评估造口周围皮肤疾病的严重程度是否有用，仍有待证明。【方法】这项前瞻性、多中心、观察性队列研究在日本 6 家区域性大型医院进行。研究的主要终点是在确定的定期门诊就诊中，通过评分系统进行定期随访在降低严重造口周围皮肤疾病发生率方面的有效性。研究采用倾向评分匹配法对比了对照组和严重造口周围皮肤疾病患者。【结果】2019 年 12 月至 2021 年 12 月期间共有 217 名患者入组，对 191 名患者进行了分析。多变量分析显示，袢状造口（比值比 5.017；95% CI：1.350-18.639；P = 0.016）和造口高度 <10 mm（比值比 7.831；95% CI：1.760-34.838；P = 0.007）是所有造口周围皮肤疾病的独立危险因素。倾向评分匹配后，指定评估时间组与历史对照组之间的疾病发生率无显著差异（75.7% vs 77.2%，P = 0.775），但基于 ABCD 和 DET 评分的严重疾病发生率（分别为 5.9% vs 19.1%，P < 0.001 和 1.5% vs 29.4%，P < 0.001）在指定评估时间组显著低于历史对照组。【结论】在造口门诊进行定期的造口周围皮肤疾病随访和评分，以及适当的造口护理，虽然没有改变造口周围皮肤疾病的总发生频率，但预防了严重造口周围皮肤疾病的发生。此外，研究发现造口高度 <10 mm 和袢状造口是造口周围皮肤疾病的危险因素。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

该前瞻性多中心研究通过对191名患者的详细分析，证实了标准化评分系统和定期随访在预防严重造口周围皮肤疾病中的核心价值。研究明确指出袢状造口和低高度造口（<10 mm）是皮肤并发症的关键风险指标，为临床护理提供了精准的预警参考。其创新性在于量化了专业随访对预防重症而非仅仅降低总发生率的贡献，尽管采用了历史对照可能存在一定偏倚，但仍为造口术后精细化管理提供了高质量的循证医学证据。

---

## 456. 机器人与腹腔镜下肝前外侧段微创切除术的倾向评分匹配分析：一项纳入10,517例病例的国际多中心研究

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/39234677)
**期刊：** Annals of surgery
**PMID：** 39234677
**DOI：** 10.1097/SLA.0000000000006523

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Propensity Score-matched Analysis Comparing Robotic Versus Laparoscopic Minor Liver Resections of the Anterolateral Segments: An International Multicenter Study of 10,517 Cases.

> **英文摘要：**
> OBJECTIVE: The aim of this study was to compare the outcomes of robotic minor liver resection (RMLR) versus laparoscopic minor liver resection (LMLR) of the anterolateral segments. BACKGROUND: Robotic liver surgery has been gaining prominence over the years with increasing usage for a myriad of hepatic resections. Robotic liver resection (RLR) has demonstrated noninferiority to laparoscopic resection (LR), while illustrating advantages over conventional laparoscopy especially for technically difficult and major LR. However, the advantage of RMLR for the anterolateral (AL) (segments II, III, IVb, V, and VI) segments, has not been clearly demonstrated. METHODS: Between 2008 to 2022, 15,356 of 29,861 patients from 68 international centres underwent robotic minor liver resection (RMLR) or laparoscopic minor liver resection (LMLR) for the AL segments propensity score-matching (PSM) analysis was performed for matched analysis. RESULTS: A total of 10,517 patients met the study criteria of which 1481 underwent RMLR and 9036 underwent LMLR. A PSM cohort of 1401 patients in each group were identified for analysis. Compared with the LMLR cohort, the RMLR cohort demonstrated significantly lower median blood loss (75 vs 100 mL, P <0.001), decreased blood transfusion (3.1% vs 5.4%, P =0.003), lower incidence of major morbidity (2.5% vs 4.6%, P =0.004), lower proportion of open conversion (1.2% vs 4.5%, P <0.001), shorter postoperative stay (4 vs 5 days, P <0.001), but higher rate of 30-day readmission (3.5% vs 2.1%, P =0.042). These results were then validated by a 1:2 PSM analysis. In the subset analysis for 3614 patients with cirrhosis, RMLR showed lower median blood loss, decreased blood transfusion, lower open conversion, and shorter postoperative stay than LMLR. CONCLUSION: RMLR demonstrated statistically significant advantages over LMLR even for resections in the AL segments although most of the observed clinical differences were minimal.

> **中文摘要：**
> 目的：本研究旨在比较机器人辅助下肝脏微创切除术（RMLR）与腹腔镜下肝脏微创切除术（LMLR）在前外侧段切除中的临床结果。背景：多年来，机器人肝脏外科手术日益受到重视，在各种肝切除术中的应用不断增加。机器人肝切除术（RLR）已被证明在效果上不逊于腹腔镜切除术（LR），并在处理技术难度大及重大肝切除术时显示出优于传统腹腔镜的优势。然而，RMLR在肝前外侧段（AL）（II、III、IVb、V和VI段）切除中的优势尚未得到明确证实。方法：在2008年至2022年期间，来自68个国际中心的29,861名患者中有15,356名接受了针对前外侧段的RMLR或LMLR，本研究采用倾向评分匹配（PSM）进行对比分析。结果：共有10,517名患者符合研究标准，其中1,481例接受了RMLR，9,036例接受了LMLR。每组各筛选出1,401名患者进入PSM队列进行分析。与LMLR组相比，RMLR组的中位出血量显著减少（75 vs 100 mL，P <0.001），输血率降低（3.1% vs 5.4%，P =0.003），严重并发症发生率较低（2.5% vs 4.6%，P =0.004），中转开腹比例较低（1.2% vs 4.5%，P <0.001），术后住院时间较短（4 vs 5天，P <0.001），但30天再入院率较高（3.5% vs 2.1%，P =0.042）。这些结果随后通过1:2的PSM分析得到了验证。在对3,614名肝硬化患者进行的亚组分析中，RMLR在减少中位出血量、降低输血率、降低中转开腹率以及缩短术后住院时间方面均优于LMLR。结论：即使是在前外侧段的肝切除中，RMLR也显示出优于LMLR的统计学优势，尽管观察到的大多数临床差异极小。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究是一项基于大规模国际多中心数据的回顾性分析，通过倾向评分匹配严谨地评估了机器人与腹腔镜在“技术相对简单”的肝前外侧段切除中的差异。研究结果有力证明了机器人辅助系统在减少术中出血、降低并发症率及缩短住院时间方面的优越性，尤其是在肝硬化亚组中获益显著。尽管临床绝对差值较小且面临较高的再入院挑战，但该研究为机器人平台在普通肝切除术中的普适性与安全性提供了高等级的循证医学证据。

---

## 457. 壶腹周围肿瘤胰十二指肠切除术后胰瘘高危胰腺国际胰腺外科研究小组（ISGPS）风险分类的验证与优化

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/39140617)
**期刊：** Annals of surgery
**PMID：** 39140617
**DOI：** 10.1097/SLA.0000000000006485

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Validation and Optimization of the International Study Group of Pancreatic Surgery Risk Classification of High-risk Pancreas for Postoperative Pancreatic Fistula After Pancreatoduodenectomy for Periampullary Tumors.

> **英文摘要：**
> OBJECTIVE: To externally validate the International Study Group of Pancreatic Surgery (ISGPS) classification and test its performance for predicting clinically relevant pancreatic fistula (CRPF) for periampullary (P-amp) tumors.
> 
> BACKGROUND: The ISGPS is a simple 2-factor, 4-tier classification of pancreas-related risk for CRPF after a pancreatoduodenectomy. External validation and performance of the classification specific to P-amps are lacking. P-amps have different disease biology, lesser need for neoadjuvant therapy, softer pancreas, and a higher rate of CRPF, underscoring the importance of site-specific prediction.
> 
> METHODS: Validation was performed in a cohort of 1422 patients, with CRPF as the primary outcome. Model performance was tested by plotting the receiver operating curve and calibration plots. After analyzing the factors predicting CRPF, the model was optimized for P-amps.
> 
> RESULTS: CRPF rate was 22.2% (315/1422), for P-amps being 25.8%. The ISGPS model performed moderately [area under the curve (AUC) = 0.632, 95% CI: 0.598-0.666, P < 0.001], with worse performance for P-amps (AUC = 0.605, 95% CI: 0.566-0.645, P < 0.001). On multivariate analysis, soft pancreas [odds ratio (OR): 1.689, 95% CI: 1.136-2.512, P = 0.010], body mass index ≥ 23 kg/m 2 (OR: 2.112, 95% CI: 1.464-3.046, P < 0.001) and pancreatic duct ≤ 3 mm (OR: 2.113, 95% CI: 1.457-3.064, P < 0.001) emerged as independent predictors, and the model was optimized. The adjusted ISGPS for P-amps showed improved discrimination (AUC = 0.672, P < 0.001, 95% CI: 0.637-0.707), with adequate performance on internal validation.
> 
> CONCLUSIONS: The adjusted ISPGS performs better than the original ISGPS in predicting CRPF for P-amps. Large-scale multicenter data are needed to generate and validate site-specific predictive models.

> **中文摘要：**
> 目的：对国际胰腺外科研究小组（ISGPS）分类进行外部验证，并测试其在预测壶腹周围（P-amp）肿瘤临床相关胰瘘（CRPF）中的性能。
> 
> 背景：ISGPS 是一种简单的、基于 2 个因素并分为 4 层的风险分类系统，用于评估胰十二指肠切除术后与胰腺相关的 CRPF 风险。目前缺乏针对壶腹周围肿瘤该分类系统的外部验证和性能评估。由于壶腹周围肿瘤具有不同的疾病生物学特性、对新辅助治疗的需求较低、胰腺质地较软且 CRPF 发生率较高，这突显了进行针对性部位预测的重要性。
> 
> 方法：在一组包含 1422 名患者的队列中进行了验证研究，以 CRPF 作为主要结局指标。通过绘制受试者工作特征曲线（ROC）和校准图来测试模型性能。在分析了预测 CRPF 的因素后，针对壶腹周围肿瘤对模型进行了优化。
> 
> 结果：CRPF 的总发生率为 22.2% (315/1422)，其中壶腹周围肿瘤的发生率为 25.8%。ISGPS 模型的表现中等 [曲线下面积 (AUC) = 0.632, 95% CI: 0.598-0.666, P < 0.001]，而在壶腹周围肿瘤子集中的表现更差 (AUC = 0.605, 95% CI: 0.566-0.645, P < 0.001)。多因素分析显示，软胰腺 [比值比 (OR): 1.689, 95% CI: 1.136-2.512, P = 0.010]、体质指数 (BMI) ≥ 23 kg/m² (OR: 2.112, 95% CI: 1.464-3.046, P < 0.001) 以及胰管直径 ≤ 3 mm (OR: 2.113, 95% CI: 1.457-3.064, P < 0.001) 是独立的预测因素，并据此对模型进行了优化。优化后的壶腹周围肿瘤 ISGPS 模型显示出更好的区分度 (AUC = 0.672, P < 0.001, 95% CI: 0.637-0.707)，且在内部验证中表现良好。
> 
> 结论：调整后的 ISGPS 模型在预测壶腹周围肿瘤 CRPF 方面优于原始模型。未来需要大规模多中心数据来构建并验证针对特定解剖部位的预测模型。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究针对胰腺外科常用的 ISGPS 风险分类系统在壶腹周围肿瘤患者中的适用性进行了严谨的外部验证，发现原模型在该亚群中的预测效能有限（AUC 仅 0.605）。通过引入 BMI、胰腺硬度和胰管直径等关键临床指标，研究者成功构建了针对性更强的优化模型，将预测区分度提升至 0.672。该研究强调了壶腹周围肿瘤独特的病理生理学特征对并发症风险的影响，为精准外科决策提供了新的循证支持，但其优化模型的普适性仍需在更大规模的国际多中心队列中进一步证实。

---

## 458. 胰腺癌切除术及辅助化疗后切缘阳性对复发和生存的影响：PRODIGE 24-CCTG PA-6 随机对照试验结果

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/39041211)
**期刊：** Annals of surgery
**PMID：** 39041211
**DOI：** 10.1097/SLA.0000000000006449

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Impact of Positive Resection Margins on Recurrence and Survival After Resection and Adjuvant Chemotherapy in Pancreatic Cancer: Results of the PRODIGE 24-CCTG PA-6 Randomized Controlled Trial.

> **英文摘要：**
> OBJECTIVE: To investigate the correlation between positive resection margins and outcomes in patients with pancreatic ductal adenocarcinoma who underwent surgery and adjuvant chemotherapy according to the pivotal trial PRODIGE 24-CCTG PA-6. BACKGROUND: The primary focus is on elucidating the prognostic significance of specific resection margins, including those associated with the superior-mesenteric vein, medial, and posterior pancreas. METHODS: The analysis involved 400 patients across multiple centers in France and Canada. Surgical resection and subsequent adjuvant chemotherapy were core interventions. This study assessed the prognostic impact of resection margins, highlighting the significance of standardized pathology assessments. In addition, the influence of chemotherapy regimen choice, comparing gemcitabine to mFOLFIRINOX, on the implications of positive resection margins was examined. RESULTS: Only 3 margins, superior-mesenteric vein [hazard ratio (HR) = 1.48 (95% CI: 1.11; 1.96); P < 0.001], medial [HR = 1.92 (95% CI: 1.36; 2.73); P < 0.001] and posterior [HR = 1.65 (95% CI: 1.21; 2.24); P = 0.002], had a significant prognostic impact on disease-free survival and were sufficient compared with the 7 recommended margins (Kappa = 0.90; 95% CI: 0.87; 0.94). R1 status was a significant independent prognostic factor for poorer survival in gemcitabine-treated patients [HR = 1.97 (95% CI: 1.23; 3.16); P = 0.005] but lost its significance with mFOLFIRINOX [HR = 1.46 (95% CI: 0.91; 2.35); P = 0.114]. CONCLUSIONS: All efforts should be made to evaluate the 3 margins of the highest prognostic value, with the others being secondary. A key finding of this study is the likely effect of mFOLFIRINOX on local invasion in operated patients, which seems to correct the impairment related to margin involvement, probably explaining the improvements in disease-free survival and overall survival.

> **中文摘要：**
> 目的：根据关键性临床试验 PRODIGE 24-CCTG PA-6，探讨接受手术及辅助化疗的胰腺导管腺癌患者切缘阳性与临床结局之间的相关性。背景：本研究主要关注阐明特定手术切缘的预后意义，包括涉及肠系膜上静脉、胰腺内侧和后侧的切缘。方法：分析涉及来自法国和加拿大多中心的 400 名患者。手术切除及随后的辅助化疗为核心干预措施。本研究评估了切缘对预后的影响，强调了标准化病理评估的重要性。此外，还检查了化疗方案的选择（吉西他滨与 mFOLFIRINOX 的比较）对切缘阳性预后意义的影响。结果：在推荐的 7 个切缘中，仅有 3 个切缘具有显著的预后价值，即肠系膜上静脉切缘 [风险比 (HR) = 1.48 (95% CI: 1.11; 1.96); P < 0.001]、内侧切缘 [HR = 1.92 (95% CI: 1.36; 2.73); P < 0.001] 和后缘 [HR = 1.65 (95% CI: 1.21; 2.24); P = 0.002]，且这三个切缘足以替代 7 个推荐切缘的评估效能 (Kappa = 0.90; 95% CI: 0.87; 0.94)。在吉西他滨治疗的患者中，R1 状态是导致生存率较差的显著独立预后因素 [HR = 1.97 (95% CI: 1.23; 3.16); P = 0.005]，但在接受 mFOLFIRINOX 治疗的患者中，其显著性消失 [HR = 1.46 (95% CI: 0.91; 2.35); P = 0.114]。结论：应尽力评估具有最高预后价值的这 3 个切缘，其他切缘则可视为次要。本研究的一项关键发现是，mFOLFIRINOX 可能通过抑制手术患者的局部侵袭，从而弥补切缘受累带来的生存受损，这可能解释了该方案在改善无病生存期和总生存期方面的优势。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本研究基于著名的 PRODIGE 24 试验，深入探讨了胰腺癌切缘状态与预后的复杂关系。其核心贡献在于提炼出肠系膜上静脉、内侧及后缘三个具有决定性预后意义的关键切缘，为简化标准化病理评估提供了循证医学依据。最重大的发现是 mFOLFIRINOX 方案显示出能消除 R1 切缘不良影响的潜力，这一结果不仅揭示了强效化疗对局部侵袭的控制作用，也为外科医生和肿瘤内科医生在制定术后策略时提供了极具价值的参考，进一步巩固了 mFOLFIRINOX 在胰腺癌辅助治疗中的地位。

---

## 459. 肝脏疾病中微生物组的治疗性干预

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/38922826)
**期刊：** Hepatology (Baltimore, Md.)
**PMID：** 38922826
**DOI：** 10.1097/HEP.0000000000000987

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Therapeutic manipulation of the microbiome in liver disease.

> **英文摘要：**
> Myriad associations between the microbiome and various facets of liver physiology and pathology have been described in the literature. Building on descriptive and correlative sequencing studies, metagenomic studies are expanding our collective understanding of the functional and mechanistic role of the microbiome as mediators of the gut-liver axis. Based on these mechanisms, the functional activity of the microbiome represents an attractive, tractable, and precision medicine therapeutic target in several liver diseases. Indeed, several therapeutics have been used in liver disease even before their description as a microbiome-dependent approach. To bring successful microbiome-targeted and microbiome-inspired therapies to the clinic, a comprehensive appreciation of the different approaches to influence, collaborate with, or engineer the gut microbiome to coopt a disease-relevant function of interest in the right patient is key. Herein, we describe the various levels at which the microbiome can be targeted-from prebiotics, probiotics, synbiotics, and antibiotics to microbiome reconstitution and precision microbiome engineering. Assimilating data from preclinical animal models, human studies as well as clinical trials, we describe the potential for and rationale behind studying such therapies across several liver diseases, including metabolic dysfunction-associated steatotic liver disease, alcohol-associated liver disease, cirrhosis, HE as well as liver cancer. Lastly, we discuss lessons learned from previous attempts at developing such therapies, the regulatory framework that needs to be navigated, and the challenges that remain.

> **中文摘要：**
> 文献中已描述了微生物组与肝脏生理学及病理学各方面之间存在无数关联。在描述性和相关性测序研究的基础上，宏基因组研究正在扩大我们对微生物组作为肠-肝轴介质的功能和机制作用的共同理解。基于这些机制，微生物组的功能活性在多种肝脏疾病中代表了一个极具吸引力、易于操作且符合精准医学要求的治疗目标。事实上，甚至在一些疗法被描述为微生物组依赖性方法之前，它们就已经被用于肝脏疾病。为了将成功的靶向微生物组及受微生物组启发的疗法推向临床，关键是要全面了解各种方法，以便在合适的患者中通过影响、协作或工程化肠道微生物组来利用特定的疾病相关功能。在本文中，我们描述了可以针对微生物组进行干预的各个层面——从益生元、益生菌、合生素和抗生素到微生物组重建和精准微生物组工程。结合临床前动物模型、人体研究以及临床试验的数据，我们描述了在多种肝脏疾病中研究此类疗法的潜力和依据，包括代谢功能障碍相关脂肪性肝病、酒精相关性肝病、肝硬化、肝性脑病（HE）以及肝癌。最后，我们讨论了以往开发此类疗法所取得的经验教训、需要遵循的监管框架以及仍然面临的挑战。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本文全面综述了通过肠-肝轴干预微生物组以治疗各类肝脏疾病的最新进展与潜力。文章系统分类了从益生元、抗生素到精准微生物工程的多层次干预策略，并整合了代谢性肝病、肝硬化及肝癌等领域的临床前与临床证据。其核心贡献在于提出了将微生物组研究从相关性描述向机制驱动的精准医疗转化的技术路线图，并深入剖析了临床转化中的监管挑战，是一篇具有高度行业指导意义的深度综述。

---

## 460. 体育锻炼在肝脏疾病中的作用

**原文链接：** [点击跳转](https://pubmed.ncbi.nlm.nih.gov/38836646)
**期刊：** Hepatology (Baltimore, Md.)
**PMID：** 38836646
**DOI：** 10.1097/HEP.0000000000000941

### 第一部分 原文与翻译

**英文原标题：** Physical exercise in liver diseases.

> **英文摘要：**
> Liver diseases contribute to ~2 million deaths each year and account for 4% of all deaths globally. Despite various treatment options, the management of liver diseases remains challenging. Physical exercise is a promising nonpharmacological approach to maintain and restore homeostasis and effectively prevent and mitigate liver diseases. In this review, we delve into the mechanisms of physical exercise in preventing and treating liver diseases, highlighting its effects on improving insulin sensitivity, regulating lipid homeostasis, and modulating immune function. In addition, we evaluate the impact of physical exercise on various liver diseases, including liver ischemia/reperfusion injury, cardiogenic liver disease, metabolic dysfunction-associated steatotic liver disease, portal hypertension, cirrhosis, and liver cancer. In conclusion, the review underscores the effectiveness of physical exercise as a beneficial intervention in combating liver diseases.

> **中文摘要：**
> 肝脏疾病每年造成约 200 万人死亡，占全球总死亡人数的 4%。尽管存在多种治疗选择，但肝脏疾病的管理仍具挑战性。体育锻炼是一种具有前景的非药物方法，可维持和恢复机体稳态，并有效预防和缓解肝脏疾病。在本综述中，我们深入探讨了体育锻炼预防和治疗肝脏疾病的机制，重点强调了其在改善胰岛素敏感性、调节脂质稳态和调节免疫功能方面的作用。此外，我们评估了体育锻炼对各种肝脏疾病的影响，包括肝缺血/再灌注损伤、心源性肝病、代谢功能障碍相关脂肪性肝病、门脉高压、肝硬化和肝癌。总之，本综述强调了体育锻炼作为对抗肝脏疾病的一种有益干预措施的有效性。

### 第二部分 AI 大师评价

本综述系统地阐述了体育锻炼在肝脏疾病防治中的多维作用。文章深入剖析了运动通过改善胰岛素敏感性、调节脂代谢及免疫功能等分子机制来恢复机体稳态的路径，并详尽评估了其在脂肪肝、肝硬化乃至肝癌等多种病理状态下的临床获益。该综述不仅肯定了运动作为非药物干预手段的高效性，也为未来制定个体化肝病康复运动方案提供了坚实的理论支撑。

---
